OS-Themis: A Scalable Critic Framework for Generalist GUI Rewards
Authors: Zehao Li, Zhenyu Wu, Yibo Zhao, Bowen Yang, Jingjing Xie, Zhaoyang Liu, Zhoumianze Liu, Kaiming Jin, Jianze Liang, Zonglin Li, Feng Wu, Bowen Zhou, Zun Wang, Zichen Ding
First: 2026-03-19T17:47:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T17:47:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has the potential to improve the robustness of GUI agents in stochastic environments, yet training is highly sensitive to the quality of the reward function. Existing reward approaches struggle to achieve both scalability and performance. To address this, we propose OS-Themis, a scalable and accurate multi-agent critic framework. Unlike a single judge, OS-Themis decomposes trajectories into verifiable milestones to isolate critical evidence for decision making and employs a review mechanism to strictly audit the evidence chain before making the final verdict. To facilitate evaluation, we further introduce OmniGUIRewardBench (OGRBench), a holistic cross-platform benchmark for GUI outcome rewards, where all evaluated models achieve their best performance under OS-Themis. Extensive experiments on AndroidWorld show that OS-Themis yields a 10.3% improvement when used to support online RL training, and a 6.9% gain when used for trajectory validation and filtering in the self-training loop, highlighting its potential to drive agent evolution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OS-Themis：面向通用GUI奖励的可扩展评判框架
强化学习（RL）在随机环境中具有提升GUI智能体鲁棒性的潜力，但其训练对奖励函数质量高度敏感。现有奖励方法难以兼顾可扩展性与性能。为此，我们提出OS-Themis——一个可扩展且精准的多智能体评判框架。与单一评判者不同，OS-Themis将轨迹分解为可验证的里程碑，以隔离决策关键证据，并采用审查机制在最终裁决前严格审核证据链。为促进评估，我们进一步引入OmniGUIRewardBench（OGRBench），这是一个跨平台的GUI结果奖励综合性基准测试，所有评估模型在OS-Themis下均取得最佳性能。在AndroidWorld上的大量实验表明，OS-Themis用于支持在线RL训练时带来10.3%的性能提升，在自训练循环中用于轨迹验证与过滤时实现6.9%的增益，凸显了其驱动智能体进化的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that reinforcement learning for GUI agents is highly sensitive to reward function quality, with existing methods struggling to balance scalability and performance. To address this, the authors propose OS-Themis, a scalable multi-agent critic framework that decomposes agent trajectories into verifiable milestones to isolate critical evidence and employs a strict review mechanism for final verdicts. Experimental results on the introduced OmniGUIRewardBench show OS-Themis enables the best performance for all evaluated models, and on AndroidWorld it yields a 10.3% improvement in online RL training and a 6.9% gain in self-training trajectory filtering, demonstrating its effectiveness in driving agent evolution.
本文的动机在于，GUI智能体的强化学习对奖励函数质量高度敏感，而现有方法难以兼顾可扩展性与性能。为此，作者提出了OS-Themis，一个可扩展的多智能体评判框架，该方法将轨迹分解为可验证的里程碑以隔离关键决策证据，并采用严格的审查机制进行最终裁决。实验结果表明，在新引入的OmniGUIRewardBench基准上，所有评估模型在OS-Themis下均取得最佳性能；在AndroidWorld环境中，该框架使在线强化学习训练性能提升10.3%，并在自训练循环的轨迹验证与过滤中带来6.9%的增益，凸显了其推动智能体进化的潜力。
Box Maze: A Process-Control Architecture for Reliable LLM Reasoning
Authors: Zou Qiang
First: 2026-03-19T17:41:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T17:41:18+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 tables, 0 figures. Conceptual architecture with preliminary simulation-based validation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong generative capabilities but remain vulnerable to hallucination and unreliable reasoning under adversarial prompting. Existing safety approaches -- such as reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and output filtering -- primarily operate at the behavioral level and may lack explicit architectural mechanisms for enforcing reasoning process integrity. This paper proposes the Box Maze framework, a conceptual process-control architecture that decomposes LLM reasoning into three explicit layers: memory grounding, structured inference, and boundary enforcement. We introduce preliminary simulation-based evaluation involving progressive boundary erosion scenarios across multiple heterogeneous LLM systems (DeepSeek-V3, Doubao, Qwen). Results from n=50 adversarial scenarios suggest that explicit cognitive control layers may improve consistency in boundary maintenance, with architectural constraints reducing boundary failure rates from approximately 40% (baseline RLHF) to below 1% under adversarial conditions. While current validation is simulation-based, these preliminary results indicate that process-level control may offer a promising direction for improving reliability in large language model reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：盒式迷宫：一种用于可靠大语言模型推理的过程控制架构
大语言模型展现出强大的生成能力，但在对抗性提示下仍易产生幻觉和不可靠推理。现有安全方法——如基于人类反馈的强化学习和输出过滤——主要在行为层面运作，可能缺乏确保推理过程完整性的显式架构机制。本文提出盒式迷宫框架，这是一种将大语言模型推理分解为三个显式层级的概念性过程控制架构：记忆锚定、结构化推理和边界强化。我们通过涉及多个异构大语言模型系统的渐进式边界侵蚀场景进行了初步模拟评估。在n=50个对抗性场景中的结果表明，显式认知控制层可提升边界维护的一致性，其架构约束在对抗条件下将边界失效率从约40%降至1%以下。当前验证虽基于模拟，但这些初步结果表明过程级控制可能为提高大语言模型推理可靠性提供有前景的方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the vulnerability of large language models (LLMs) to hallucination and unreliable reasoning under adversarial prompting, which existing safety methods like RLHF and output filtering address primarily at a behavioral level, this paper proposes the Box Maze framework as a process-control architecture. The method decomposes LLM reasoning into three explicit layers: memory grounding, structured inference, and boundary enforcement. Preliminary simulation-based evaluation across multiple LLM systems in adversarial scenarios shows that this architectural approach reduces boundary failure rates from approximately 40% in baseline RLHF systems to below 1%, indicating improved consistency in boundary maintenance and suggesting process-level control as a promising direction for enhancing reasoning reliability.
本文的动机在于大型语言模型（LLM）在对抗性提示下容易产生幻觉和不可靠推理，而现有如RLHF和输出过滤等安全方法主要在行为层面操作，缺乏明确的架构机制来保证推理过程完整性。为此，论文提出了Box Maze框架，这是一种过程控制架构，其方法将LLM推理分解为三个明确层次：记忆锚定、结构化推理和边界执行。在针对多个异构LLM系统的初步模拟评估中，对抗性场景下的实验结果表明，这种架构约束能将边界失败率从基线RLHF的约40%降低至1%以下，从而提高了边界维护的一致性，表明过程级控制可能是提升大型语言模型推理可靠性的一个有前景的方向。
Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization
Authors: Ting Gao, Stavros Orfanoudakis, Nan Lin, Elvin Isufi, Winnie Daamen, Serge Hoogendoorn
First: 2026-03-18T13:00:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T17:21:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion-based policies have gained significant popularity in Reinforcement Learning (RL) due to their ability to represent complex, non-Gaussian distributions. Stochastic Differential Equation (SDE)-based diffusion policies often rely on indirect entropy control due to the intractability of the exact entropy, while also suffering from computationally prohibitive policy gradients through the iterative denoising chain. To overcome these issues, we propose Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER), an Ordinary Differential Equation (ODE)-based online RL framework. FMER parameterizes the policy via flow matching and samples actions along a straight probability path, motivated by optimal transport. FMER leverages the model's generative nature to construct an advantage-weighted target velocity field from a candidate set, steering policy updates toward high-value regions. By deriving a tractable entropy objective, FMER enables principled maximum-entropy optimization for enhanced exploration. Experiments on sparse multi-goal FrankaKitchen benchmarks demonstrate that FMER outperforms state-of-the-art methods, while remaining competitive on standard MuJoco benchmarks. Moreover, FMER reduces training time by 7x compared to heavy diffusion baselines (QVPO) and 10-15% relative to efficient variants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于熵正则化的流匹配策略
基于扩散的策略因其能表示复杂的非高斯分布，在强化学习中广受关注。基于随机微分方程的扩散策略常因精确熵难以计算而依赖间接熵控制，且需通过迭代去噪链计算计算代价高昂的策略梯度。为克服这些问题，我们提出基于熵正则化的流匹配策略——一种基于常微分方程的在线强化学习框架。该策略通过流匹配参数化策略，并基于最优传输理论沿直线概率路径采样动作。其利用模型的生成特性，从候选集中构建优势加权目标速度场，引导策略更新至高价值区域。通过推导可处理的熵目标，该框架实现了增强探索的最大熵优化。在稀疏多目标FrankaKitchen基准测试中，该策略优于现有先进方法，在标准MuJoco基准上保持竞争力，且训练时间较重型扩散基线减少7倍，较高效变体减少10-15%。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitations of diffusion-based policies in reinforcement learning, which often rely on indirect entropy control and suffer from high computational costs due to iterative denoising. To address this, the authors propose Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER), an ODE-based online RL framework that parameterizes the policy via flow matching, sampling actions along a straight probability path inspired by optimal transport, and constructs an advantage-weighted target velocity field to steer updates toward high-value regions. Experimental results on sparse multi-goal FrankaKitchen benchmarks show that FMER outperforms state-of-the-art methods, remains competitive on standard MuJoco benchmarks, and reduces training time by 7x compared to heavy diffusion baselines and 10-15% relative to efficient variants.
本文的动机是解决强化学习中基于扩散的策略的局限性，这些策略通常依赖间接熵控制，且因迭代去噪导致计算成本高昂。为此，作者提出了带熵正则化的流匹配策略（FMER），这是一个基于常微分方程的在线强化学习框架，通过流匹配参数化策略，沿最优传输启发的直线概率路径采样动作，并构建优势加权目标速度场以引导策略更新朝向高价值区域。在稀疏多目标FrankaKitchen基准测试中的实验结果表明，FMER优于现有先进方法，在标准MuJoco基准上保持竞争力，并将训练时间相比重型扩散基线减少7倍，相比高效变体减少10-15%。
VEPO: Variable Entropy Policy Optimization for Low-Resource Language Foundation Models
Authors: Chonghan Liu, Yimin Du, Qi An, Xin He, Cunqi Zhai, Fei Tan, Weijia Lin, Xiaochun Gong, Yongchao Deng, Shousheng Jia, Xiangzheng Zhang
First: 2026-03-19T17:10:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T17:10:29+00:00
Comments: 23 pages. Includes figures and tables. Conference submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models frequently exhibit suboptimal performance on low resource languages, primarily due to inefficient subword segmentation and systemic training data imbalances. In this paper, we propose Variable Entropy Policy Optimization (VEPO), which leverages Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards to incorporate deterministic structural constraints into the policy alignment process. This framework ensures prescribed sequence length, robust format consistency, and rigorous linguistic well formedness, all enforced during training. Central to our approach is a variable entropy mechanism that enables the model to dynamically calibrate the equilibrium between literal fidelity and semantic naturalness by modulating the exploration exploitation manifold. By integrating entropy tempered advantage estimation with asymmetric clipping, VEPO sustains robust exploration while mitigating policy collapse. Empirical evaluations across 90 FLORES-200, COMET-22, chrF directions demonstrate that VEPO yields substantial improvements in both tokenization efficiency and translation quality, bridging the performance gap for underrepresented languages.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VEPO：面向低资源语言基础模型的变熵策略优化方法
大语言模型在低资源语言上常表现欠佳，主要源于低效的子词切分与系统性的训练数据失衡。本文提出变熵策略优化方法，通过可验证奖励的强化学习将确定性结构约束融入策略对齐过程。该框架在训练中强制执行预设序列长度、鲁棒的格式一致性与严格的语言规范性。核心机制是变熵模块，通过调节探索-利用流形使模型动态校准字面忠实度与语义自然性之间的平衡。通过将熵调优势估计与非对称裁剪相结合，VEPO在维持强探索能力的同时避免策略崩溃。在90个FLORES-200、COMET-22及chrF方向上的实验表明，VEPO在分词效率与翻译质量上均取得显著提升，有效弥合了低资源语言的性能差距。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the suboptimal performance of large language models on low-resource languages, attributed to inefficient subword segmentation and training data imbalances. It introduces Variable Entropy Policy Optimization (VEPO), a reinforcement learning framework that incorporates deterministic structural constraints—such as sequence length, format consistency, and linguistic well-formedness—into policy alignment via verifiable rewards. A key innovation is a variable entropy mechanism that dynamically balances literal fidelity and semantic naturalness through entropy-tempered advantage estimation and asymmetric clipping, preventing policy collapse. Experimental results across 90 FLORES-200, COMET-22, and chrF directions show that VEPO significantly improves tokenization efficiency and translation quality, narrowing the performance gap for underrepresented languages.
本文针对大语言模型在低资源语言上表现不佳的问题，主要源于低效的子词分割和训练数据不平衡。研究提出了可变熵策略优化（VEPO），这是一个利用强化学习与可验证奖励的框架，将确定性结构约束（如序列长度、格式一致性和语言规范性）融入策略对齐过程。其核心是可变熵机制，通过熵调节的优势估计和非对称裁剪，动态校准字面忠实度与语义自然性之间的平衡，避免策略崩溃。在90个FLORES-200、COMET-22和chrF方向上的实证评估表明，VEPO显著提升了分词效率和翻译质量，缩小了低资源语言的性能差距。
Adaptive Regime-Aware Stock Price Prediction Using Autoencoder-Gated Dual Node Transformers with Reinforcement Learning Control
Authors: Mohammad Al Ridhawi, Mahtab Haj Ali, Hussein Al Osman
First: 2026-03-19T16:55:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T16:55:33+00:00
Comments: Submitted to IEEE Transactions on Computational Social Systems. 17 pages, 9 figures, 10 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Stock markets exhibit regime-dependent behavior where prediction models optimized for stable conditions often fail during volatile periods. Existing approaches typically treat all market states uniformly or require manual regime labeling, which is expensive and quickly becomes stale as market dynamics evolve. This paper introduces an adaptive prediction framework that adaptively identifies deviations from normal market conditions and routes data through specialized prediction pathways. The architecture consists of three components: (1) an autoencoder trained on normal market conditions that identifies anomalous regimes through reconstruction error, (2) dual node transformer networks specialized for stable and event-driven market conditions respectively, and (3) a Soft Actor-Critic reinforcement learning controller that adaptively tunes the regime detection threshold and pathway blending weights based on prediction performance feedback. The reinforcement learning component enables the system to learn adaptive regime boundaries, defining anomalies as market states where standard prediction approaches fail. Experiments on 20 S&P 500 stocks spanning 1982 to 2025 demonstrate that the proposed framework achieves 0.68% MAPE for one-day predictions without the reinforcement controller and 0.59% MAPE with the full adaptive system, compared to 0.80% for the baseline integrated node transformer. Directional accuracy reaches 72% with the complete framework. The system maintains robust performance during high-volatility periods, with MAPE below 0.85% when baseline models exceed 1.5%. Ablation studies confirm that each component contributes meaningfully: autoencoder routing accounts for 36% relative MAPE degradation upon removal, followed by the SAC controller at 15% and the dual-path architecture at 7%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自编码器-门控双节点Transformer与强化学习控制的自适应市场状态感知股价预测
股票市场呈现状态依赖行为，在稳定条件下优化的预测模型常在波动期失效。现有方法通常统一处理所有市场状态或需人工标注市场状态，成本高昂且易随市场动态变化而过时。本文提出一种自适应预测框架，能自适应识别偏离正常市场条件的异常状态，并通过专用预测路径处理数据。该架构包含三个组件：(1) 在正常市场条件下训练的自编码器，通过重构误差识别异常状态；(2) 分别针对稳定和事件驱动市场条件设计的双节点Transformer网络；(3) 基于Soft Actor-Critic强化学习的控制器，根据预测性能反馈自适应调整状态检测阈值和路径融合权重。强化学习组件使系统能学习自适应状态边界，将异常定义为标准预测方法失效的市场状态。在1982年至2025年20只标普500股票上的实验表明：无强化控制器时单日预测MAPE为0.68%，完整自适应系统达0.59%，而基线集成节点Transformer为0.80%。完整框架方向准确率达72%。系统在高波动期保持稳健性能，当基线模型MAPE超过1.5%时，本系统MAPE仍低于0.85%。消融研究证实各组件均有贡献：移除自编码器路由导致MAPE相对恶化36%，SAC控制器为15%，双路径架构为7%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the regime-dependent behavior of stock markets where models optimized for stable conditions fail during volatility, this paper introduces an adaptive prediction framework that automatically identifies market regimes and routes data through specialized pathways. The method employs an autoencoder to detect anomalous regimes via reconstruction error, dual node transformers for stable and event-driven conditions, and a Soft Actor-Critic reinforcement learning controller to adaptively tune regime thresholds and blending weights based on performance feedback. Experimental results on 20 S&P 500 stocks from 1982 to 2025 show the full system achieves 0.59% MAPE for one-day predictions and 72% directional accuracy, outperforming a baseline (0.80% MAPE) and maintaining robustness during high-volatility periods, with ablation studies confirming each component's contribution.
针对股票市场因状态依赖行为导致稳定条件下优化的模型在波动期失效的问题，本文提出了一种自适应预测框架，能自动识别市场状态并将数据路由至专用预测路径。方法包括：使用自编码器通过重构误差检测异常状态，采用双节点Transformer网络分别处理稳定和事件驱动条件，并利用Soft Actor-Critic强化学习控制器根据预测反馈自适应调整状态检测阈值和路径混合权重。在1982年至2025年20只标普500股票上的实验表明，完整系统的一日预测MAPE为0.59%，方向准确率达72%，优于基线模型（0.80% MAPE），且在高压波动期保持稳健性能，消融研究验证了各组件均有显著贡献。
CRAFT: Aligning Diffusion Models with Fine-Tuning Is Easier Than You Think
Authors: Zening Sun, Zhengpeng Xie, Lichen Bai, Shitong Shao, Shuo Yang, Zeke Xie
First: 2026-03-19T14:59:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T14:59:46+00:00
Comments: CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning Diffusion models has achieved remarkable breakthroughs in generating high-quality, human preference-aligned images. Existing techniques, such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and DPO-style preference optimization, have become principled tools for fine-tuning diffusion models. However, SFT relies on high-quality images that are costly to obtain, while DPO-style methods depend on large-scale preference datasets, which are often inconsistent in quality. Beyond data dependency, these methods are further constrained by computational inefficiency. To address these two challenges, we propose Composite Reward Assisted Fine-Tuning (CRAFT), a lightweight yet powerful fine-tuning paradigm that requires significantly reduced training data while maintaining computational efficiency. It first leverages a Composite Reward Filtering (CRF) technique to construct a high-quality and consistent training dataset and then perform an enhanced variant of SFT. We also theoretically prove that CRAFT actually optimizes the lower bound of group-based reinforcement learning, establishing a principled connection between SFT with selected data and reinforcement learning. Our extensive empirical results demonstrate that CRAFT with only 100 samples can easily outperform recent SOTA preference optimization methods with thousands of preference-paired samples. Moreover, CRAFT can even achieve 11-220$\times$ faster convergences than the baseline preference optimization methods, highlighting its extremely high efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CRAFT：扩散模型对齐微调比想象中更简单
扩散模型对齐技术在生成符合人类偏好的高质量图像方面取得显著突破。现有方法如监督微调（SFT）和DPO式偏好优化已成为微调扩散模型的原则性工具。然而，SFT依赖获取成本高昂的高质量图像，而DPO式方法需要大规模偏好数据集，其质量往往参差不齐。除数据依赖外，这些方法还受限于计算效率低下。为应对这两大挑战，我们提出复合奖励辅助微调（CRAFT）——一种轻量而强大的微调范式，在保持计算效率的同时大幅减少训练数据需求。该方法首先采用复合奖励过滤（CRF）技术构建高质量且一致的训练数据集，随后执行增强版SFT。我们通过理论证明CRAFT实际上优化了基于群体的强化学习下界，从而在数据筛选的SFT与强化学习之间建立了原则性关联。大量实验结果表明，仅使用100个样本的CRAFT即可超越近期需要数千个偏好配对样本的SOTA偏好优化方法。此外，CRAFT的收敛速度比基线偏好优化方法快11-220倍，突显其极高的效率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the data dependency and computational inefficiency of existing methods for aligning diffusion models with human preferences, such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and DPO-style optimization, which require costly high-quality images or large-scale preference datasets. The authors propose CRAFT, a lightweight fine-tuning paradigm that first uses Composite Reward Filtering to construct a high-quality, consistent training dataset and then performs an enhanced variant of SFT, theoretically linking it to group-based reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that CRAFT outperforms state-of-the-art preference optimization methods using only 100 samples and achieves 11-220 times faster convergence, demonstrating high data and computational efficiency.
本文针对现有扩散模型对齐方法（如监督微调和DPO式偏好优化）存在的数据依赖性强与计算效率低的问题，提出了一种轻量级微调范式CRAFT。该方法首先通过复合奖励过滤技术构建高质量、一致性的训练数据集，然后执行一种增强型监督微调，并从理论上建立了其与基于群体的强化学习之间的联系。主要实验结果表明，CRAFT仅需100个样本即可超越使用数千个偏好配对样本的最新先进方法，并且收敛速度比基线偏好优化方法快11-220倍，展现出极高的数据与计算效率。
Maximum-Entropy Exploration with Future State-Action Visitation Measures
Authors: Adrien Bolland, Gaspard Lambrechts, Damien Ernst
First: 2026-03-19T14:30:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T14:30:08+00:00
Comments: arXiv admin note: substantial text overlap with arXiv:2412.06655
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Maximum entropy reinforcement learning motivates agents to explore states and actions to maximize the entropy of some distribution, typically by providing additional intrinsic rewards proportional to that entropy function. In this paper, we study intrinsic rewards proportional to the entropy of the discounted distribution of state-action features visited during future time steps. This approach is motivated by two results. First, we show that the expected sum of these intrinsic rewards is a lower bound on the entropy of the discounted distribution of state-action features visited in trajectories starting from the initial states, which we relate to an alternative maximum entropy objective. Second, we show that the distribution used in the intrinsic reward definition is the fixed point of a contraction operator and can therefore be estimated off-policy. Experiments highlight that the new objective leads to improved visitation of features within individual trajectories, in exchange for slightly reduced visitation of features in expectation over different trajectories, as suggested by the lower bound. It also leads to improved convergence speed for learning exploration-only agents. Control performance remains similar across most methods on the considered benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于未来状态-动作访问度量的最大熵探索
最大熵强化学习通过提供与熵函数成比例的内在奖励，激励智能体探索状态和动作以最大化特定分布的熵。本文研究的内在奖励与未来时间步访问的状态-动作特征折扣分布的熵成比例。该方法基于两项理论结果：首先，证明这类内在奖励的期望和是从初始状态出发的轨迹中状态-动作特征折扣分布熵的下界，这与替代性最大熵目标相关；其次，证明内在奖励定义中使用的分布是压缩算子的不动点，因而可进行离策略估计。实验表明，新目标能提升单条轨迹内的特征访问覆盖度（但会略微降低跨轨迹的期望特征访问度，符合下界预期），并加速纯探索智能体的收敛速度。在基准测试中，各方法的控制性能基本持平。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need for more effective exploration in reinforcement learning through maximum entropy principles. The method introduces intrinsic rewards proportional to the entropy of the discounted distribution of state-action features visited in future time steps, which is shown to lower-bound the entropy of the discounted feature distribution from initial states and can be estimated off-policy due to its fixed-point contraction property. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach improves feature visitation within individual trajectories and accelerates convergence for exploration-only agents, though it slightly reduces expected feature visitation across trajectories, while maintaining similar control performance on benchmarks.
本文旨在通过最大熵原理提升强化学习中的探索效率。方法引入了与未来时间步访问的状态-动作特征折扣分布的熵成比例的内在奖励，该分布被证明是初始状态折扣特征分布熵的下界，且因其不动点收缩性质可进行离策略估计。实验结果表明，该方法提高了单个轨迹内的特征访问率，并加速了纯探索智能体的收敛速度，尽管略微降低了跨轨迹的期望特征访问，但在基准测试中保持了相似的控制性能。
Context Bootstrapped Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Saaket Agashe, Jayanth Srinivasa, Gaowen Liu, Ramana Kompella, Xin Eric Wang
First: 2026-03-19T14:23:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T14:23:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) suffers from exploration inefficiency, where models struggle to generate successful rollouts, resulting in minimal learning signal. This challenge is particularly severe for tasks that require the acquisition of novel reasoning patterns or domain-specific knowledge. To address this, we propose Context Bootstrapped Reinforcement Learning (CBRL), which augments RLVR training by stochastically prepending few-shot demonstrations to training prompts. The injection probability follows a curriculum that starts high to bootstrap early exploration, then anneals to zero so the model must ultimately succeed without assistance. This forces the policy to internalize reasoning patterns from the demonstrations rather than relying on them at test time. We validate CBRL across two model families and five Reasoning Gym tasks. Our results demonstrate that CBRL consistently improves success rate, provides better exploration efficiency, and is algorithm-agnostic. We further demonstrate CBRL's practical applicability on Q, a domain-specific programming language that diverges significantly from mainstream language conventions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：上下文引导强化学习
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）存在探索效率低下的问题，模型难以生成成功的轨迹，导致学习信号微弱。这一挑战在需要获取新颖推理模式或领域特定知识的任务中尤为突出。为此，我们提出上下文引导强化学习（CBRL），通过在训练提示中随机前置少量示例演示来增强RLVR训练。注入概率遵循课程学习策略：初始较高以引导早期探索，随后逐渐衰减至零，迫使模型最终无需辅助即可成功。这促使策略内化演示中的推理模式，而非在测试时依赖它们。我们在两个模型系列和五个推理健身任务中验证了CBRL。结果表明，CBRL能持续提升成功率，提供更优的探索效率，且与算法无关。我们进一步在Q（一种与主流编程语言规范差异显著的领域特定语言）上证明了CBRL的实际适用性。

Experimental results across two model families and five Reasoning Gym tasks show that CBRL consistently improves success rates and exploration efficiency, and it is algorithm-agnostic, with further validation on a domain-specific programming language Q demonstrating practical applicability.

AutoResearch-RL: Perpetual Self-Evaluating Reinforcement Learning Agents for Autonomous Neural Architecture Discovery
Authors: Nilesh Jain, Rohit Yadav, Sagar Kotian, Claude AI
First: 2026-03-07T17:49:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T13:59:07+00:00
Comments: arXiv admin note: This submission has been withdrawn due to violation of arXiv policies for acceptable submissions
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present AutoResearch-RL, a framework in which a reinforcement learning agent conducts open-ended neural architecture and hyperparameter research without human supervision, running perpetually until a termination oracle signals convergence or resource exhaustion. At each step the agent proposes a code modification to a target training script, executes it under a fixed wall clock time budget, observes a scalar reward derived from validation bits-per-byte (val-bpb), and updates its policy via Proximal Policy Optimisation (PPO). The key design insight is the separation of three concerns: (i) a frozen environment (data pipeline, evaluation protocol, and constants) that guarantees fair cross-experiment comparison; (ii) a mutable target file (train.py) that represents the agent's editable state; and (iii) a meta-learner (the RL agent itself) that accumulates a growing trajectory of experiment outcomes and uses them to inform subsequent proposals. We formalise this as a Markov Decision Process, derive convergence guarantees under mild assumptions, and demonstrate empirically on a single GPU nanochat pretraining benchmark that AutoResearch-RL discovers configurations that match or exceed hand-tuned baselines after approximately 300 overnight iterations, with no human in the loop.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoResearch-RL：用于自主神经架构发现的持续自评估强化学习智能体
本文提出AutoResearch-RL框架，该框架中的强化学习智能体可在无人监督的情况下开展开放式神经架构与超参数研究，持续运行直至终止判定器发出收敛或资源耗尽信号。在每一步中，智能体对目标训练脚本提出代码修改建议，在固定挂钟时间预算内执行修改，通过验证字节比特率（val-bpb）获取标量奖励，并通过近端策略优化（PPO）更新策略。核心设计理念在于三方面分离：（1）冻结环境（数据管道、评估协议与常量）确保实验间公平对比；（2）可变目标文件（train.py）作为智能体可编辑状态；（3）元学习器（即强化学习智能体本身）持续积累实验轨迹并据此指导后续提案。我们将该框架形式化为马尔可夫决策过程，在温和假设下推导收敛保证，并在单GPU纳米对话预训练基准上实证表明：经过约300次夜间迭代后，AutoResearch-RL发现的配置可匹配或超越人工调优基线，全程无需人工干预。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces AutoResearch-RL, a framework designed to automate neural architecture and hyperparameter discovery through perpetual, self-evaluating reinforcement learning agents, motivated by the need to reduce human supervision in machine learning research. The method employs a reinforcement learning agent that iteratively proposes code modifications to a training script, executes them within a fixed time budget, and updates its policy using Proximal Policy Optimisation based on validation performance, with key design elements separating environment, mutable code, and meta-learner concerns. Experimental results on a single GPU nanochat pretraining benchmark show that the framework discovers configurations matching or exceeding hand-tuned baselines after about 300 overnight iterations, demonstrating autonomous effectiveness without human intervention.

MultihopSpatial: Multi-hop Compositional Spatial Reasoning Benchmark for Vision-Language Model
Authors: Youngwan Lee, Soojin Jang, Yoorhim Cho, Seunghwan Lee, Yong-Ju Lee, Sung Ju Hwang
First: 2026-03-19T13:33:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T13:33:26+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://youngwanlee.github.io/multihopspatial
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Spatial reasoning is foundational for Vision-Language Models (VLMs), particularly when deployed as Vision-Language-Action (VLA) agents in physical environments. However, existing benchmarks predominantly focus on elementary, single-hop relations, neglecting the multi-hop compositional reasoning and precise visual grounding essential for real-world scenarios. To address this, we introduce MultihopSpatial, offering three key contributions: (1) A comprehensive benchmark designed for multi-hop and compositional spatial reasoning, featuring 1- to 3-hop complex queries across diverse spatial perspectives. (2) Acc@50IoU, a complementary metric that simultaneously evaluates reasoning and visual grounding by requiring both answer selection and precise bounding box prediction - capabilities vital for robust VLA deployment. (3) MultihopSpatial-Train, a dedicated large-scale training corpus to foster spatial intelligence. Extensive evaluation of 37 state-of-the-art VLMs yields eight key insights, revealing that compositional spatial reasoning remains a formidable challenge. Finally, we demonstrate that reinforcement learning post-training on our corpus enhances both intrinsic VLM spatial reasoning and downstream embodied manipulation performance.
中文标题/摘要

Bridging Network Fragmentation: A Semantic-Augmented DRL Framework for UAV-aided VANETs
Authors: Gaoxiang Cao, Wenke Yuan, Huasen He, Yunpeng Hou, Xiaofeng Jiang, Shuangwu Chen, Jian Yang
First: 2026-03-19T13:15:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T13:15:52+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 13 figures. Submitted to IEEE Transactions on Cognitive Communications and Networking
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vehicular Ad-hoc Networks (VANETs) are the digital cornerstone of autonomous driving, yet they suffer from severe network fragmentation in urban environments due to physical obstructions. Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs), with their high mobility, have emerged as a vital solution to bridge these connectivity gaps. However, traditional Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL)-based UAV deployment strategies lack semantic understanding of road topology, often resulting in blind exploration and sample inefficiency. By contrast, Large Language Models (LLMs) possess powerful reasoning capabilities capable of identifying topological importance, though applying them to control tasks remains challenging. To address this, we propose the Semantic-Augmented DRL (SA-DRL) framework. Firstly, we propose a fragmentation quantification method based on Road Topology Graphs (RTG) and Dual Connected Graphs (DCG). Subsequently, we design a four-stage pipeline to transform a general-purpose LLM into a domain-specific topology expert. Finally, we propose the Semantic-Augmented PPO (SA-PPO) algorithm, which employs a Logit Fusion mechanism to inject the LLM's semantic reasoning directly into the policy as a prior, effectively guiding the agent toward critical intersections. Extensive high-fidelity simulations demonstrate that SA-PPO achieves state-of-the-art performance with remarkable efficiency, reaching baseline performance levels using only 26.6% of the training episodes. Ultimately, SA-PPO improves two key connectivity metrics by 13.2% and 23.5% over competing methods, while reducing energy consumption to just 28.2% of the baseline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：弥合网络碎片化：面向无人机辅助车联网的语义增强深度强化学习框架

RewardFlow: Topology-Aware Reward Propagation on State Graphs for Agentic RL with Large Language Models
Authors: Xiao Feng, Bo Han, Zhanke Zhou, Jiaqi Fan, Jiangchao Yao, Ka Ho Li, Dahai Yu, Michael Kwok-Po Ng
First: 2026-03-19T13:07:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T13:07:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) holds significant promise for enhancing the agentic reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) with external environments. However, the inherent sparsity of terminal rewards hinders fine-grained, state-level optimization. Although process reward modeling offers a promising alternative, training dedicated reward models often entails substantial computational costs and scaling difficulties. To address these challenges, we introduce RewardFlow, a lightweight method for estimating state-level rewards tailored to agentic reasoning tasks. RewardFlow leverages the intrinsic topological structure of states within reasoning trajectories by constructing state graphs. This enables an analysis of state-wise contributions to success, followed by topology-aware graph propagation to quantify contributions and yield objective, state-level rewards. When integrated as dense rewards for RL optimization, RewardFlow substantially outperforms prior RL baselines across four agentic reasoning benchmarks, demonstrating superior performance, robustness, and training efficiency. The implementation of RewardFlow is publicly available at https://github.com/tmlr-group/RewardFlow.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RewardFlow：基于状态图拓扑感知的奖励传播方法，用于大语言模型智能体强化学习
强化学习在提升大语言模型与外部环境交互的智能体推理能力方面潜力显著，但终端奖励的固有稀疏性阻碍了细粒度的状态级优化。尽管过程奖励建模提供了可行替代方案，但训练专用奖励模型通常伴随高昂计算成本与扩展难题。为此，我们提出RewardFlow——一种面向智能体推理任务的轻量级状态级奖励估计方法。该方法通过构建状态图，利用推理轨迹中状态的内在拓扑结构，分析各状态对任务成功的贡献度，进而采用拓扑感知的图传播算法量化贡献值，生成客观的状态级奖励。将RewardFlow作为密集奖励用于强化学习优化时，在四项智能体推理基准测试中均显著超越现有强化学习基线，展现出更优的性能、鲁棒性与训练效率。RewardFlow实现代码已公开于https://github.com/tmlr-group/RewardFlow。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces RewardFlow, a method designed to address the challenge of sparse terminal rewards in reinforcement learning (RL) for agentic reasoning with large language models (LLMs), which hinders fine-grained state-level optimization. The approach constructs state graphs from reasoning trajectories to analyze topological structures, enabling the propagation of rewards to quantify state-wise contributions and generate dense, objective state-level rewards without the high cost of training dedicated reward models. Experimental results across four agentic reasoning benchmarks show that RewardFlow significantly outperforms prior RL baselines in performance, robustness, and training efficiency when used for RL optimization.
本文提出了RewardFlow方法，旨在解决大型语言模型在强化学习中进行代理推理时终端奖励稀疏的问题，该问题阻碍了细粒度的状态级优化。该方法通过从推理轨迹构建状态图来利用其内在拓扑结构，通过图传播分析状态对成功的贡献，从而生成密集的客观状态级奖励，避免了训练专用奖励模型的高昂成本。在四个代理推理基准测试中的实验结果表明，当用于强化学习优化时，RewardFlow在性能、鲁棒性和训练效率上均显著优于先前的强化学习基线方法。
Learn for Variation: Variationally Guided AAV Trajectory Learning in Differentiable Environments
Authors: Xiucheng Wang, Zhenye Chen, Nan Cheng
First: 2026-03-19T12:57:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T12:57:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous aerial vehicles (AAVs) empower sixth-generation (6G) Internet-of-Things (IoT) networks through mobility-driven data collection. However, conventional reward-driven reinforcement learning for AAV trajectory planning suffers from severe credit assignment issues and training instability, because sparse scalar rewards fail to capture the long-term and nonlinear effects of sequential movements. To address these challenges, this paper proposes Learn for Variation (L4V), a gradient-informed trajectory learning framework that replaces high-variance scalar reward signals with dense and analytically grounded policy gradients. Particularly, the coupled evolution of AAV kinematics, distance-dependent channel gains, and per-user data-collection progress is first unrolled into an end-to-end differentiable computational graph. Backpropagation through time then serves as a discrete adjoint solver, which propagates exact sensitivities from the cumulative mission objective to every control action and policy parameter. These structured gradients are used to train a deterministic neural policy with temporal smoothness regularization and gradient clipping. Extensive simulations demonstrate that L4V consistently outperforms representative baselines, including a genetic algorithm, DQN, A2C, and DDPG, in mission completion time, average transmission rate, and training cost
中文标题/摘要
标题：为变分而学：可微分环境中基于变分引导的自主飞行器轨迹学习
自主飞行器通过移动驱动的数据采集赋能第六代物联网网络。然而，传统基于奖励驱动的强化学习方法在规划飞行轨迹时存在严重的信用分配问题和训练不稳定性，因为稀疏的标量奖励难以捕捉序列动作的长期非线性效应。为应对这些挑战，本文提出“为变分而学”框架——一种梯度感知的轨迹学习方法，用密集且具有解析依据的策略梯度替代高方差标量奖励信号。该框架首先将飞行器运动学、距离相关信道增益和用户数据采集进程的耦合演化展开为端到端可微分计算图，进而通过时间反向传播作为离散伴随求解器，将累积任务目标对每个控制动作和策略参数的精确敏感度进行反向传播。利用这些结构化梯度，通过时间平滑正则化与梯度裁剪训练确定性神经策略。大量仿真实验表明，在任务完成时间、平均传输速率和训练成本方面，该方法均优于遗传算法、DQN、A2C和DDPG等代表性基线模型。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the limitations of conventional reward-driven reinforcement learning for autonomous aerial vehicle (AAV) trajectory planning in 6G IoT networks, which suffers from credit assignment issues and training instability due to sparse scalar rewards. The proposed method, Learn for Variation (L4V), introduces a gradient-informed framework that replaces scalar rewards with dense policy gradients derived from an end-to-end differentiable computational graph modeling AAV kinematics, channel gains, and data-collection progress; backpropagation through time computes exact sensitivities to train a deterministic neural policy with regularization. Experimental results from simulations show that L4V consistently outperforms baselines like genetic algorithms, DQN, A2C, and DDPG in mission completion time, average transmission rate, and training cost.
本文的动机是针对6G物联网网络中自主飞行器轨迹规划的传统奖励驱动强化学习存在信用分配问题和训练不稳定的局限性，这是由于稀疏标量奖励无法捕捉序列动作的长期非线性效应。所提出的方法“学习变分”采用梯度引导框架，通过构建包含飞行器运动学、信道增益和数据收集进程的端到端可微分计算图，用密集的策略梯度替代标量奖励，并利用时间反向传播计算精确灵敏度来训练带有正则化的确定性神经策略。主要实验结果表明，在大量仿真中，该方法在任务完成时间、平均传输速率和训练成本上均一致优于遗传算法、DQN、A2C和DDPG等基线模型。
ProRL Agent: Rollout-as-a-Service for RL Training of Multi-Turn LLM Agents
Authors: Hao Zhang, Mingjie Liu, Shaokun Zhang, Songyang Han, Jian Hu, Zhenghui Jin, Yuchi Zhang, Shizhe Diao, Ximing Lu, Binfeng Xu, Zhiding Yu, Jan Kautz, Yi Dong
First: 2026-03-19T12:08:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T12:08:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn LLM agents are increasingly important for solving complex, interactive tasks, and reinforcement learning (RL) is a key ingredient for improving their long-horizon behavior. However, RL training requires generating large numbers of sandboxed rollout trajectories, and existing infrastructures often couple rollout orchestration with the training loop, making systems hard to migrate and maintain. Under the rollout-as-a-service philosophy, we present ProRL Agent , a scalable infrastructure that serves the full agentic rollout lifecycle through an API service. ProRL Agent also provides standardized and extensible sandbox environments that support diverse agentic tasks in rootless HPC settings. We validate ProRL Agent through RL training on software engineering, math, STEM, and coding tasks. ProRL Agent is open-sourced and integrated as part of NVIDIA NeMo Gym.

The motivation for this work is to address the infrastructure challenges in reinforcement learning (RL) training for multi-turn large language model (LLM) agents, where existing systems tightly couple rollout generation with training loops, hindering scalability and maintenance. Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro
Authors: KT Tech innovation Group
First: 2026-03-19T11:37:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T11:37:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The evolving LLM landscape requires capabilities beyond simple text generation, prioritizing multi-step reasoning, long-context understanding, and agentic workflows. This shift challenges existing models in enterprise environments, especially in Korean-language and domain-specific scenarios where scaling is insufficient. We introduce Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro, a 32B parameter flagship LLM designed to address enterprise-grade complexity through reasoning-focused optimization. Our methodology builds a robust data foundation via a quality-centric curation pipeline utilizing abstract syntax tree (AST) analysis for code, gap-filling synthesis for mathematics, and an LLM-based quality evaluator. Pre-training scales the model via layer-predictor-based Depth Upscaling (DuS) and a progressive strategy supporting a 128K token context window. Post-training introduces a specialized multi-stage pipeline, including Reasoning SFT, model merging, and asynchronous reinforcement learning (RL), to develop complex problem-solving skills. "Fusion Training" then rebalances these capabilities with conversational fluency, consistent response styling, and reliable tool-use. The evaluations show that Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro achieves competitive performance against leading global and domestic models. In addition, it sets state-of-the-art results on Korean-specific benchmarks, showcasing deep linguistic and cultural understanding. Finally, Responsible AI evaluations validate safety against attacks, ensuring a secure profile for deployment with a balance of harmlessness and responsiveness.

Automatic Configuration of LLM Post-Training Pipelines
Authors: Channe Chwa, Xinle Wu, Yao Lu
First: 2026-03-19T11:26:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T11:26:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM post-training pipelines that combine supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning are difficult to configure under realistic compute budgets: the configuration space is high-dimensional and heterogeneous, stages are strongly coupled, and each end-to-end evaluation is expensive. We propose AutoPipe, a budget-aware two-stage framework for configuration selection in LLM post-training. Offline, AutoPipe learns a dataset-conditioned learning-to-rank surrogate from historical runs, capturing within-dataset preferences and providing transferable guidance toward promising regions of the configuration space. Online, for a new dataset, AutoPipe uses the offline guidance to steer Bayesian optimization and models dataset-specific deviations with a Gaussian-process residual surrogate. To reduce evaluation cost, each trial is early-stopped and scored by a learned predictor that maps early training signals to a low-cost proxy for final post-training performance. Experiments on biomedical reasoning tasks show that AutoPipe consistently outperforms offline-only baselines and achieves comparable performance with the strongest online HPO baselines while using less than 10\% of their computational cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型后训练流程的自动配置
结合监督微调与强化学习的大语言模型后训练流程在实际计算预算下难以配置：配置空间具有高维异构性、各阶段强耦合性，且每次端到端评估成本高昂。我们提出AutoPipe——一种面向预算感知的两阶段框架，用于大语言模型后训练中的配置选择。离线阶段，AutoPipe从历史运行数据中学习基于数据集条件的学习排序代理模型，捕获数据集内部偏好并为配置空间中有潜力的区域提供可迁移指导。在线阶段，针对新数据集，AutoPipe利用离线指导引导贝叶斯优化，并通过高斯过程残差代理模型建模数据集特定偏差。为降低评估成本，每个试验均采用早停策略，并通过学习到的预测器（将早期训练信号映射为最终后训练性能的低成本代理指标）进行评分。在生物医学推理任务上的实验表明，AutoPipe持续优于纯离线基线，并在使用少于最强在线超参数优化基线10%计算成本的情况下，达到与之相当的性能表现。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the high cost and complexity of configuring large language model (LLM) post-training pipelines, which combine supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, under practical computational budgets. The proposed method, AutoPipe, is a budget-aware two-stage framework that first learns a dataset-conditioned learning-to-rank surrogate model offline from historical runs to guide the search, and then online uses this guidance to steer Bayesian optimization while modeling dataset-specific deviations with a Gaussian-process residual surrogate; it further reduces cost via early stopping and a learned predictor that estimates final performance from early training signals. The main experimental results on biomedical reasoning tasks demonstrate that AutoPipe consistently outperforms offline-only baselines and matches the performance of strong online hyperparameter optimization baselines while using less than 10% of their computational cost.

Memento-Skills: Let Agents Design Agents
Authors: Huichi Zhou, Siyuan Guo, Anjie Liu, Zhongwei Yu, Ziqin Gong, Bowen Zhao, Zhixun Chen, Menglong Zhang, Yihang Chen, Jinsong Li, Runyu Yang, Qiangbin Liu, Xinlei Yu, Jianmin Zhou, Na Wang, Chunyang Sun, Jun Wang
First: 2026-03-19T10:45:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T10:45:22+00:00
Comments: Memento-Skills Technical Report
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We introduce \emph{Memento-Skills}, a generalist, continually-learnable LLM agent system that functions as an \emph{agent-designing agent}: it autonomously constructs, adapts, and improves task-specific agents through experience. The system is built on a memory-based reinforcement learning framework with \emph{stateful prompts}, where reusable skills (stored as structured markdown files) serve as persistent, evolving memory. These skills encode both behaviour and context, enabling the agent to carry forward knowledge across interactions. Starting from simple elementary skills (like Web search and terminal operations), the agent continually improves via the \emph{Read--Write Reflective Learning} mechanism introduced in \emph{Memento~2}~\cite{wang2025memento2}. In the \emph{read} phase, a behaviour-trainable skill router selects the most relevant skill conditioned on the current stateful prompt; in the \emph{write} phase, the agent updates and expands its skill library based on new experience. This closed-loop design enables \emph{continual learning without updating LLM parameters}, as all adaptation is realised through the evolution of externalised skills and prompts. Unlike prior approaches that rely on human-designed agents, Memento-Skills enables a generalist agent to \emph{design agents end-to-end} for new tasks. Through iterative skill generation and refinement, the system progressively improves its own capabilities. Experiments on the \emph{General AI Assistants} benchmark and \emph{Humanity's Last Exam} demonstrate sustained gains, achieving 26.2\% and 116.2\% relative improvements in overall accuracy, respectively. Code is available at https://github.com/Memento-Teams/Memento-Skills.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Memento-Skills：让智能体设计智能体
我们提出\emph{Memento-Skills}，一种通用、持续可学习的大语言模型智能体系统，其功能是作为\emph{智能体设计智能体}：它通过经验自主构建、调整和改进任务专用智能体。该系统建立在基于记忆的强化学习框架之上，采用\emph{状态化提示}，其中可复用技能（以结构化Markdown文件存储）作为持久、演化的记忆。这些技能编码了行为与上下文，使智能体能够在交互间传承知识。 从简单基础技能（如网络搜索和终端操作）出发，智能体通过\emph{Memento~2}~\cite{wang2025memento2}引入的\emph{读写反思学习}机制持续改进。在\emph{读取}阶段，一个行为可训练的技能路由器根据当前状态化提示选择最相关技能；在\emph{写入}阶段，智能体基于新经验更新和扩展其技能库。这种闭环设计实现了\emph{无需更新大语言模型参数的持续学习}，所有适应均通过外化技能与提示的演化实现。 与依赖人工设计智能体的先前方法不同，Memento-Skills使通用智能体能够为新任务\emph{端到端设计智能体}。通过迭代的技能生成与优化，系统逐步提升自身能力。在\emph{通用AI助手}基准和\emph{人类终极考试}上的实验展示了持续增益，整体准确率分别实现26.2\%和116.2\%的相对提升。代码发布于https://github.com/Memento-Teams/Memento-Skills。

Motivated by the need for autonomous and continually improving AI agents without manual design, this paper introduces Memento-Skills, a system where a generalist LLM agent acts as an agent-designing agent to construct, adapt, and refine task-specific agents through experience. The method employs a memory-based reinforcement learning framework with stateful prompts, where reusable skills stored as structured markdown files serve as persistent memory, and uses a Read-Write Reflective Learning mechanism to select and update skills without modifying the underlying LLM parameters. Experimental results on the General AI Assistants benchmark and Humanity's Last Exam show relative accuracy improvements of 26.2% and 116.2%, respectively, demonstrating sustained performance gains through continual skill evolution.
本文旨在实现无需人工设计的自主持续学习智能体，提出了Memento-Skills系统，其中通用大语言模型智能体作为“设计智能体的智能体”，通过经验自主构建、调整和改进任务专用智能体。该方法基于带有状态提示的记忆强化学习框架，将可重用技能以结构化Markdown文件形式存储作为持久记忆，并采用读写反思学习机制来选择和更新技能，而无需修改大语言模型参数。在通用AI助手基准和Humanity's Last Exam上的实验结果显示，整体准确率分别相对提升了26.2%和116.2%，证明了通过技能持续进化能实现性能的稳定提升。
CausalRM: Causal-Theoretic Reward Modeling for RLHF from Observational User Feedbacks
Authors: Hao Wang, Licheng Pan, Zhichao Chen, Chunyuan Zheng, Zhixuan Chu, Xiaoxi Li, Yuan Lu, Xinggao Liu, Haoxuan Li, Zhouchen Lin
First: 2026-03-19T10:37:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T10:37:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the success of reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) in aligning language models, current reward modeling heavily relies on experimental feedback data collected from human annotators under controlled and costly conditions. In this work, we introduce observational reward modeling -- learning reward models with observational user feedback (e.g., clicks, copies, and upvotes) -- as a scalable and cost-effective alternative. We identify two fundamental challenges in this setting: (1) observational feedback is noisy due to annotation errors, which deviates it from true user preference; (2) observational feedback is biased by user preference, where users preferentially provide feedback on responses they feel strongly about, which creats a distribution shift between training and inference data. To address these challenges, we propose CausalRM, a causal-theoretic reward modeling framework that aims to learn unbiased reward models from observational feedback. To tackle challenge (1), CausalRM introduces a noise-aware surrogate loss term that is provably equivalent to the primal loss under noise-free conditions by explicitly modeling the annotation error generation process. To tackle challenge (2), CausalRM uses propensity scores -- the probability of a user providing feedback for a given response -- to reweight training samples, yielding a loss function that eliminates user preference bias. Extensive experiments across diverse LLM backbones and benchmark datasets validate that CausalRM effectively learns accurate reward signals from noisy and biased observational feedback and delivers substantial performance improvements on downstream RLHF tasks -- including a 49.2% gain on WildGuardMix and a 32.7% improvement on HarmBench. Code is available on our project website.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CausalRM：基于因果理论的奖励建模——从观测性用户反馈进行RLHF
尽管基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）在语言模型对齐方面取得了成功，但当前的奖励建模严重依赖在受控且成本高昂条件下从人工标注者收集的实验性反馈数据。本研究提出观测性奖励建模——利用观测性用户反馈（如点击、复制、点赞）学习奖励模型——作为一种可扩展且经济高效的替代方案。我们识别出该场景下的两个根本性挑战：（1）观测性反馈因标注误差存在噪声，使其偏离真实用户偏好；（2）观测性反馈受用户偏好偏差影响，用户倾向于对其强烈关注的回复提供反馈，导致训练数据与推理数据间存在分布偏移。为应对这些挑战，我们提出CausalRM——一个基于因果理论的奖励建模框架，旨在从观测性反馈中学习无偏奖励模型。针对挑战（1），CausalRM通过显式建模标注误差生成过程，引入可证明在无噪声条件下与原始损失函数等效的噪声感知代理损失项。针对挑战（2），CausalRM利用倾向得分（用户对特定回复提供反馈的概率）对训练样本进行重加权，构建可消除用户偏好偏差的损失函数。跨多种大语言模型骨干和基准数据集的广泛实验验证：CausalRM能有效从含噪声和偏差的观测性反馈中学习准确奖励信号，并在下游RLHF任务中实现显著性能提升——在WildGuardMix上获得49.2%的性能增益，在HarmBench上提升32.7%。代码已发布于项目网站。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high cost and limited scalability of collecting controlled human feedback for reward modeling in RLHF by proposing to learn from observational user feedback like clicks and upvotes instead. The method, named CausalRM, tackles two key challenges: noisy feedback due to annotation errors and bias from users preferentially providing feedback on certain responses. It introduces a noise-aware surrogate loss that models error generation and uses propensity scores to reweight samples and correct for bias. Experimental results across various LLMs and benchmarks show that CausalRM effectively learns accurate reward signals, achieving substantial performance gains, including a 49.2% improvement on WildGuardMix and a 32.7% improvement on HarmBench in downstream RLHF tasks.
本文针对强化学习人类反馈中奖励建模依赖昂贵受控实验数据的问题，提出利用点击、复制、点赞等观测性用户反馈作为可扩展且低成本的替代方案。所提出的CausalRM方法旨在解决观测反馈中的两大挑战：因标注错误产生的噪声偏差以及用户偏好导致的反馈分布偏移。该方法通过显式建模标注错误过程引入噪声感知的代理损失函数，并利用倾向得分对训练样本重加权以消除用户偏好偏差。在多种大语言模型和基准数据集上的实验表明，CausalRM能从带噪声和偏差的观测反馈中有效学习准确奖励信号，在下游RLHF任务中取得显著性能提升，如在WildGuardMix上获得49.2%的性能增益，在HarmBench上提升32.7%。
Mixed-Precision Training and Compilation for RRAM-based Computing-in-Memory Accelerators
Authors: Rebecca Pelke, Joel Klein, Jose Cubero-Cascante, Nils Bosbach, Jan Moritz Joseph, Rainer Leupers
First: 2026-01-29T13:54:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T09:56:31+00:00
Comments: PREPRINT - Accepted for publication at the Design, Automation & Test in Europe Conference & Exhibition (DATE), April 20-22, 2026, in Verona, Italy V2 - fixed typos
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Computing-in-Memory (CIM) accelerators are a promising solution for accelerating Machine Learning (ML) workloads, as they perform Matrix-Vector Multiplications (MVMs) on crossbar arrays directly in memory. Although the bit widths of the crossbar inputs and cells are very limited, most CIM compilers do not support quantization below 8 bit. As a result, a single MVM requires many compute cycles, and weights cannot be efficiently stored in a single crossbar cell. To address this problem, we propose a mixed-precision training and compilation framework for CIM architectures. The biggest challenge is the massive search space, that makes it difficult to find good quantization parameters. This is why we introduce a reinforcement learning-based strategy to find suitable quantization configurations that balance latency and accuracy. In the best case, our approach achieves up to a 2.48x speedup over existing state-of-the-art solutions, with an accuracy loss of only 0.086 %.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向RRAM存内计算加速器的混合精度训练与编译
存内计算（CIM）加速器通过在交叉阵列中直接执行矩阵向量乘法（MVM）来加速机器学习（ML）任务，是一种极具前景的解决方案。尽管交叉阵列的输入和单元位宽非常有限，但大多数CIM编译器不支持8位以下的量化。这导致单个MVM需要大量计算周期，且权重无法高效存储在单个交叉单元中。为解决此问题，我们提出了一种面向CIM架构的混合精度训练与编译框架。最大挑战在于巨大的搜索空间使得难以找到合适的量化参数。为此，我们引入了一种基于强化学习的策略，以寻找平衡延迟与精度的量化配置。在最佳情况下，我们的方法相比现有先进方案实现了最高2.48倍的加速，精度损失仅为0.086%。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inefficiency of existing Computing-in-Memory (CIM) accelerators, which typically require many cycles for matrix-vector multiplications due to limited support for quantization below 8 bits, preventing efficient weight storage. To overcome this, the authors propose a mixed-precision training and compilation framework that employs a reinforcement learning strategy to navigate the vast search space and identify optimal quantization configurations that balance latency and model accuracy. Experimental results demonstrate that their method can achieve up to a 2.48x speedup compared to state-of-the-art solutions while maintaining high accuracy, with only a minimal accuracy loss of 0.086% in the best case.
本文针对现有存内计算加速器因量化支持有限（通常不低于8位）导致矩阵向量乘法计算周期多、权重存储效率低的问题，提出了一种混合精度训练与编译框架。该方法采用基于强化学习的策略，在庞大的搜索空间中寻找能平衡延迟和精度的最优量化配置。实验结果表明，该方法在最佳情况下相比现有先进方案可实现高达2.48倍的加速，同时仅带来0.086%的精度损失。
HISR: Hindsight Information Modulated Segmental Process Rewards For Multi-turn Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhicong Lu, Zichuan Lin, Wei Jia, Changyuan Tian, Deheng Ye, Peiguang Li, Li Jin, Nayu Liu, Guangluan Xu, Wei Feng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-03-19T09:42:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T09:42:05+00:00
Comments: Submitted to ACL 2026 on Jan 5, 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models excel in diverse domains, their performance on complex longhorizon agentic decision-making tasks remains limited. Most existing methods concentrate on designing effective reward models (RMs) to advance performance via multi-turn reinforcement learning. However, they suffer from delayed propagation in sparse outcome rewards and unreliable credit assignment with potentially overly fine-grained and unfocused turnlevel process rewards. In this paper, we propose (HISR) exploiting Hindsight Information to modulate Segmental process Rewards, which closely aligns rewards with sub-goals and underscores significant segments to enhance the reliability of credit assignment. Specifically, a segment-level process RM is presented to assign rewards for each sub-goal in the task, avoiding excessively granular allocation to turns. To emphasize significant segments in the trajectory, a hindsight model is devised to reflect the preference of performing a certain action after knowing the trajectory outcome. With this characteristic, we design the ratios of sequence likelihoods between hindsight and policy model to measure action importance. The ratios are subsequently employed to aggregate segment importance scores, which in turn modulate segmental process rewards, enhancing credit assignment reliability. Extensive experimental results on three publicly benchmarks demonstrate the validity of our method.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HISR：基于后见信息调制的分段过程奖励用于多轮智能体强化学习
尽管大语言模型在多个领域表现卓越，但在复杂长程智能体决策任务上的性能仍有限制。现有方法多聚焦于设计有效的奖励模型，通过多轮强化学习提升性能，但面临稀疏结果奖励的延迟传播问题，以及可能过于细碎且缺乏聚焦的轮次级过程奖励导致的不可靠信用分配。本文提出HISR方法，利用后见信息调制分段过程奖励，使奖励与子目标紧密对齐，并突出关键片段以增强信用分配的可靠性。具体而言，我们提出分段级过程奖励模型，为任务中的每个子目标分配奖励，避免对轮次进行过度细粒度分配。为强调轨迹中的重要片段，设计后见模型以反映在获知轨迹结果后执行特定动作的偏好。基于此特性，我们通过后见模型与策略模型的序列似然比来衡量动作重要性，并以此聚合片段重要性分数，进而调制分段过程奖励，提升信用分配可靠性。在三个公开基准上的大量实验结果验证了本方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of large language models in complex, long-horizon agentic decision-making, where existing reward models often suffer from delayed reward propagation and unreliable credit assignment due to overly fine-grained turn-level rewards. The method introduces HISR, which leverages hindsight information to modulate segmental process rewards by employing a segment-level process reward model to assign rewards aligned with sub-goals and a hindsight model to reflect action importance based on trajectory outcomes, using likelihood ratios to aggregate segment importance and modulate rewards. Experimental results on three public benchmarks demonstrate the method's effectiveness in enhancing credit assignment reliability and improving performance.
本研究的动机是解决大型语言模型在复杂长程智能体决策任务中的局限性，现有奖励模型常因过于细粒度的回合级奖励而导致奖励传播延迟和信用分配不可靠。方法上提出了HISR，利用后见信息调节分段过程奖励，通过分段级过程奖励模型为子目标分配奖励，并设计后见模型基于轨迹结果反映动作重要性，使用似然比聚合分段重要性分数以调制奖励。在三个公开基准上的大量实验结果验证了该方法在提升信用分配可靠性和性能方面的有效性。
Thinking with Constructions: A Benchmark and Policy Optimization for Visual-Text Interleaved Geometric Reasoning
Authors: Haokun Zhao, Wanshi Xu, Haidong Yuan, Songjun Cao, Long Ma, Yanghua Xiao
First: 2026-03-19T09:27:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T09:27:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Geometric reasoning inherently requires "thinking with constructions" -- the dynamic manipulation of visual aids to bridge the gap between problem conditions and solutions. However, existing Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) are largely confined to passive inference with static diagrams, lacking the strategic knowledge of when and how to construct effective visual aids. To address this, we present a framework for Visual-Text Interleaved Chain-of-Thought. We first introduce GeoAux-Bench, the first benchmark comprising 4,334 geometry problems that aligns textual construction steps with ground-truth visual updates. Our pilot study reveals two critical insights: (1) interleaved visual-textual aids outperform single-modality counterparts, which cannot losslessly capture geometric synergy; and (2) valid constructions act as entropy reducers, strongly correlating with reduced reasoning perplexity. Building on these findings, we propose Action Applicability Policy Optimization (A2PO), a reinforcement learning paradigm for mastering strategic construction. A2PO employs Adaptive Reward Shaping to regulate the timing and quality of visual aids via counterfactual sampling to distinguish necessary from redundant constructions. Experiments demonstrate our approach enables MLLMs to leverage selective auxiliary constructions, yielding a 3.51% gain over strong baselines. Code and data are available on GitHub.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于构造的思维：视觉-文本交织几何推理的基准与策略优化
几何推理本质上需要'基于构造的思维'——通过动态操作视觉辅助工具来弥合问题条件与解决方案之间的差距。然而，现有的多模态大语言模型大多局限于对静态图表的被动推理，缺乏何时及如何构建有效视觉辅助的策略性知识。为此，我们提出了视觉-文本交织思维链框架。首先推出GeoAux-Bench基准，这是首个包含4,334个几何问题的数据集，将文本构造步骤与真实视觉更新对齐。初步研究揭示两个关键发现：(1) 交织式视觉-文本辅助优于单模态方案，后者无法无损捕捉几何协同效应；(2) 有效构造可作为熵减器，与降低推理困惑度强相关。基于这些发现，我们提出动作适用性策略优化——一种掌握策略性构造的强化学习范式。该方法通过反事实采样采用自适应奖励塑形机制，以区分必要构造与冗余构造。实验表明，我们的方法使多模态大语言模型能利用选择性辅助构造，较基线模型提升3.51%。代码与数据已在GitHub开源。

The paper is motivated by the limitation of current Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) in geometric reasoning, as they passively infer from static diagrams without strategically constructing visual aids. To address this, the authors introduce a Visual-Text Interleaved Chain-of-Thought framework, starting with GeoAux-Bench, a benchmark of 4,334 geometry problems that pair textual construction steps with visual updates. Their pilot study finds that interleaved visual-textual aids outperform single-modality approaches and that valid constructions reduce reasoning perplexity. Building on this, they propose Action Applicability Policy Optimization (A2PO), a reinforcement learning method using adaptive reward shaping to optimize the timing and quality of constructions. Experimental results show that A2PO enables MLLMs to use selective auxiliary constructions, achieving a 3.51% performance improvement over strong baselines.
本文的动机在于当前多模态大语言模型在几何推理中的局限性，即它们只能被动地从静态图表进行推断，缺乏战略性地构建视觉辅助的能力。为此，作者提出了一个视觉-文本交织的思维链框架，首先创建了GeoAux-Bench基准，包含4,334个几何问题，将文本构建步骤与真实视觉更新对齐。初步研究发现，交织的视觉-文本辅助优于单模态方法，且有效构建能降低推理困惑度。在此基础上，他们提出了动作适用性策略优化（A2PO），这是一种通过自适应奖励塑形来优化构建时机和质量的强化学习方法。实验结果表明，A2PO使多模态大语言模型能够利用选择性辅助构建，相比强基线实现了3.51%的性能提升。
Balanced Thinking: Improving Chain of Thought Training in Vision Language Models
Authors: Shaked Perek, Ben Wiesel, Avihu Dekel, Nimrod Shabtay, Eli Schwartz
First: 2026-03-19T09:21:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T09:21:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal reasoning in vision-language models (VLMs) typically relies on a two-stage process: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). In standard SFT, all tokens contribute equally to the loss, even though reasoning data are inherently token-imbalanced. Long <think> traces overshadow short but task-critical <answer> segments, leading to verbose reasoning and inaccurate answers. We propose SCALe (Scheduled Curriculum Adaptive Loss), which explicitly separates supervision over reasoning and answer segments using dynamic, length-independent weighting. Unlike vanilla SFT, which overweights the <think> segment, SCALe-SFT gradually shifts the focus from <think> to <answer> throughout training via a cosine scheduling policy, encouraging concise and well-grounded reasoning. We evaluate SCALe across diverse benchmarks and architectures. Results show that SCALe consistently improves accuracy over vanilla SFT and matches the performance of the full two-phase SFT + GRPO pipeline while requiring only about one-seventh of the training time, making it a lightweight yet effective alternative. When combined with GRPO, SCALe achieves the best overall performance, highlighting its value both as a standalone method and as a strong foundation for reinforcement refinement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：平衡思维：改进视觉语言模型中的思维链训练
视觉语言模型（VLM）的多模态推理通常依赖两阶段流程：监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）。标准SFT中所有词元对损失函数的贡献权重相同，但推理数据本身存在词元分布不均衡问题。冗长的<think>轨迹会掩盖简短但任务关键的<answer>片段，导致推理冗余且答案不准确。我们提出SCALe（计划课程自适应损失），通过动态且与长度无关的加权机制，显式分离对推理段和答案段的监督。与过度加权<think>段的传统SFT不同，SCALe-SFT通过余弦调度策略在训练过程中逐步将焦点从<think>转移至<answer>，从而促进简洁且基于事实的推理。我们在多种基准测试和架构中评估SCALe。结果表明：SCALe持续提升传统SFT的准确率，其性能与完整两阶段SFT+GRPO流程相当，而训练时间仅需约七分之一，成为轻量高效替代方案。当与GRPO结合时，SCALe取得最佳综合性能，彰显其既可作为独立方法，亦可作为强化优化的坚实基础。

The paper addresses the issue of token imbalance in vision-language models (VLMs) during supervised fine-tuning (SFT), where lengthy reasoning traces overshadow short but critical answer segments, leading to verbose reasoning and inaccurate outputs. To mitigate this, the authors propose SCALe (Scheduled Curriculum Adaptive Loss), a method that explicitly separates supervision over reasoning and answer segments using dynamic, length-independent weighting, gradually shifting focus from reasoning to answers via a cosine scheduling policy. Experimental results across diverse benchmarks and architectures show that SCALe consistently improves accuracy over vanilla SFT, matches the performance of the full SFT+GRPO pipeline with only about one-seventh of the training time, and achieves the best overall performance when combined with GRPO, highlighting its effectiveness as both a standalone lightweight method and a foundation for reinforcement refinement.

Preference-Driven Multi-Objective Combinatorial Optimization with Conditional Computation
Authors: Mingfeng Fan, Jianan Zhou, Yifeng Zhang, Yaoxin Wu, Jinbiao Chen, Guillaume Adrien Sartoretti
First: 2025-06-10T15:25:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T08:59:04+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 6 figures, under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent deep reinforcement learning methods have achieved remarkable success in solving multi-objective combinatorial optimization problems (MOCOPs) by decomposing them into multiple subproblems, each associated with a specific weight vector. However, these methods typically treat all subproblems equally and solve them using a single model, hindering the effective exploration of the solution space and thus leading to suboptimal performance. To overcome the limitation, we propose POCCO, a novel plug-and-play framework that enables adaptive selection of model structures for subproblems, which are subsequently optimized based on preference signals rather than explicit reward values. Specifically, we design a conditional computation block that routes subproblems to specialized neural architectures. Moreover, we propose a preference-driven optimization algorithm that learns pairwise preferences between winning and losing solutions. We evaluate the efficacy and versatility of POCCO by applying it to two state-of-the-art neural methods for MOCOPs. Experimental results across four classic MOCOP benchmarks demonstrate its significant superiority and strong generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于偏好驱动的条件计算多目标组合优化
近期深度强化学习方法通过将多目标组合优化问题分解为多个与特定权重向量相关的子问题，取得了显著成果。然而，这些方法通常平等对待所有子问题并使用单一模型求解，限制了解空间的有效探索，导致性能欠佳。为克服此局限，我们提出POCCO——一种新颖的即插即用框架，能够为子问题自适应选择模型结构，并基于偏好信号而非显式奖励值进行优化。具体而言，我们设计了条件计算模块，将子问题路由至专用神经架构。此外，我们提出偏好驱动优化算法，学习获胜解与失败解间的成对偏好关系。通过将POCCO应用于两种先进的MOCOP神经方法，我们在四个经典MOCOP基准测试中验证了其显著优越性与强大泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a limitation in existing deep reinforcement learning methods for multi-objective combinatorial optimization, which treat all subproblems equally with a single model, thereby hindering effective exploration and leading to suboptimal performance. To overcome this, the authors propose POCCO, a plug-and-play framework that adaptively selects specialized neural architectures for different subproblems via a conditional computation block and optimizes them using preference signals rather than explicit rewards through a preference-driven algorithm based on pairwise comparisons. Experimental results on four classic benchmarks show that POCCO significantly outperforms and generalizes well when applied to two state-of-the-art neural methods.
本文针对现有深度强化学习方法在多目标组合优化中平等处理所有子问题并使用单一模型，从而限制解空间探索并导致性能不佳的局限性。为此，作者提出了POCCO框架，该框架通过条件计算块自适应地为不同子问题选择专用神经架构，并采用基于成对比较的偏好驱动算法，利用偏好信号而非显式奖励进行优化。在四个经典基准测试上的实验结果表明，POCCO应用于两种先进神经方法时，表现出显著优越性和强泛化能力。
Learning to Self-Evolve
Authors: Xiaoyin Chen, Canwen Xu, Yite Wang, Boyi Liu, Zhewei Yao, Yuxiong He
First: 2026-03-19T08:41:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T08:41:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Learning to Self-Evolve (LSE), a reinforcement learning framework that trains large language models (LLMs) to improve their own contexts at test time. We situate LSE in the setting of test-time self-evolution, where a model iteratively refines its context from feedback on seen problems to perform better on new ones. Existing approaches rely entirely on the inherent reasoning ability of the model and never explicitly train it for this task. LSE reduces the multi-step evolution problem to a single-step RL objective, where each context edit is rewarded by the improvement in downstream performance. We pair this objective with a tree-guided evolution loop. On Text-to-SQL generation (BIRD) and general question answering (MMLU-Redux), a 4B-parameter model trained with LSE outperforms self-evolving policies powered by GPT-5 and Claude Sonnet 4.5, as well as prompt optimization methods including GEPA and TextGrad, and transfers to guide other models without additional training. Our results highlight the effectiveness of treating self-evolution as a learnable skill.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习自我进化
我们提出了学习自我进化（LSE），这是一个强化学习框架，用于训练大型语言模型（LLM）在测试时优化其自身上下文。LSE定位于测试时自我进化场景，模型通过已见问题的反馈迭代优化上下文，以在新问题上表现更佳。现有方法完全依赖模型固有的推理能力，从未针对此任务进行显式训练。LSE将多步进化问题简化为单步强化学习目标，其中每次上下文编辑的奖励由下游性能提升决定。我们将此目标与树引导进化循环相结合。在文本到SQL生成（BIRD）和通用问答（MMLU-Redux）任务中，采用LSE训练的40亿参数模型超越了基于GPT-5和Claude Sonnet 4.5的自我进化策略，以及包括GEPA和TextGrad在内的提示优化方法，且无需额外训练即可迁移指导其他模型。我们的结果凸显了将自我进化作为可学习技能的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Learning to Self-Evolve (LSE), a reinforcement learning framework motivated by the need to train large language models (LLMs) to actively improve their own contexts during test time, rather than relying solely on their inherent reasoning abilities. The method reduces multi-step self-evolution to a single-step reinforcement learning objective, where each context edit is rewarded based on downstream performance improvement, and pairs this with a tree-guided evolution loop. Experimental results on Text-to-SQL generation (BIRD) and general question answering (MMLU-Redux) show that a 4B-parameter model trained with LSE outperforms self-evolving policies using larger models like GPT-5 and Claude Sonnet 4.5, as well as prompt optimization methods such as GEPA and TextGrad, while also transferring to guide other models without additional training.

iSatCR: Graph-Empowered Joint Onboard Computing and Routing for LEO Data Delivery
Authors: Jiangtao Luo, Bingbing Xu, Shaohua Xia, Yongyi Ran
First: 2026-03-19T06:49:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T06:49:27+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sending massive Earth observation data produced by low Earth orbit (LEO) satellites back to the ground for processing consumes a large amount of on-orbit bandwidth and exacerbates the space-to-ground link bottleneck. Most prior work has concentrated on optimizing the routing of raw data within the constellation, yet cannot cope with the surge in data volume. Recently, advances in onboard computing have made it possible to process data in situ, thus significantly reducing the data volume to be transmitted. In this paper, we present iSatCR, a distributed graph-based approach that jointly optimizes onboard computing and routing to boost transmission efficiency. Within iSatCR, we design a novel graph embedding utilizing shifted feature aggregation and distributed message passing to capture satellite states, and then propose a distributed graph-based deep reinforcement learning algorithm that derives joint computing-routing strategies under constrained on-board storage to handle the complexity and dynamics of LEO networks. Extensive experiments show iSatCR outperforms baselines, particularly under high load.
中文标题/摘要
标题：iSatCR：面向低轨数据交付的图赋能星上计算与路由联合优化
将低地球轨道卫星产生的大规模对地观测数据传回地面处理，消耗大量在轨带宽并加剧星地链路瓶颈。现有研究多集中于优化星座内原始数据的路由，难以应对数据量的激增。近年来，星上计算技术的进步使得数据原位处理成为可能，从而显著减少需传输的数据量。本文提出iSatCR——一种基于分布式图的星上计算与路由联合优化方法，以提升传输效率。该方法设计了采用偏移特征聚合与分布式消息传递的新型图嵌入来捕获卫星状态，并提出基于分布式图的深度强化学习算法，在星载存储受限条件下推导联合计算-路由策略，以应对低轨网络的复杂性与动态性。大量实验表明iSatCR优于基线方法，尤其在高负载场景下表现突出。

The motivation for this work is to address the bottleneck in transmitting massive Earth observation data from low Earth orbit (LEO) satellites to the ground by reducing reliance on limited space-to-ground bandwidth. The method introduces iSatCR, a distributed graph-based approach that jointly optimizes onboard computing and routing; it employs a novel graph embedding with shifted feature aggregation and distributed message passing to capture satellite states, and uses a distributed graph-based deep reinforcement learning algorithm to derive strategies under storage constraints. Main experimental results demonstrate that iSatCR outperforms existing baselines, especially under high-load conditions, thereby boosting transmission efficiency.

Single Agent Robust Deep Reinforcement Learning for Bus Fleet Control
Authors: Yifan Zhang
First: 2025-08-28T13:47:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T06:32:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bus bunching remains a challenge for urban transit due to stochastic traffic and passenger demand. Traditional solutions rely on multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) in loop-line settings, which overlook realistic operations characterized by heterogeneous routes, timetables, fluctuating demand, and varying fleet sizes. We propose a novel single-agent reinforcement learning (RL) framework for bus holding control that avoids the data imbalance and convergence issues of MARL under near-realistic simulation. A bidirectional timetabled network with dynamic passenger demand is constructed. The key innovation is reformulating the multi-agent problem into a single-agent one by augmenting the state space with categorical identifiers (vehicle ID, station ID, time period) in addition to numerical features (headway, occupancy, velocity). This high-dimensional encoding enables single-agent policies to capture inter-agent dependencies, analogous to projecting non-separable inputs into a higher-dimensional space. We further design a structured reward function aligned with operational goals: instead of exponential penalties on headway deviations, a ridge-shaped reward balances uniform headways and schedule adherence. Experiments show that our modified soft actor-critic (SAC) achieves more stable and superior performance than benchmarks, including MADDPG (e.g., -430k vs. -530k under stochastic conditions). These results demonstrate that single-agent deep RL, when enhanced with categorical structuring and schedule-aware rewards, can effectively manage bus holding in non-loop, real-world contexts. This paradigm offers a robust, scalable alternative to MARL frameworks, particularly where agent-specific experiences are imbalanced.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于单智能体鲁棒深度强化学习的公交车辆调度控制
公交串车问题因随机交通流与客流需求持续困扰城市公交系统。传统方案依赖环线场景下的多智能体强化学习（MARL），但忽略了实际运营中存在的异质线路、时刻表、波动需求及可变车队规模等特征。本研究提出一种新颖的单智能体强化学习（RL）框架用于公交驻站控制，通过近真实仿真规避了MARL的数据失衡与收敛难题。构建了具有动态客流需求的双向时刻表网络，其核心创新在于通过扩展状态空间（在数值特征如车头时距、载客量、速度之外增加车辆ID、站点ID、时段等分类标识符），将多智能体问题重构为单智能体问题。这种高维编码使单智能体策略能捕捉智能体间依赖关系，类似于将不可分离输入投影到更高维空间。我们进一步设计了符合运营目标的结构化奖励函数：采用岭形奖励平衡均匀车头时距与时刻表遵循度，而非对车头时距偏差施加指数惩罚。实验表明，改进的柔性演员-评论家算法（SAC）相比基准方法（如随机条件下-43万对比-53万）获得更稳定优异的性能。这些结果证明：通过分类结构化与时刻表感知奖励增强的单智能体深度RL，能有效管理非环线实际场景中的公交驻站控制。该范式为MARL框架提供了鲁棒且可扩展的替代方案，尤其适用于智能体特定经验失衡的场景。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the persistent problem of bus bunching in urban transit, which is exacerbated by stochastic traffic and passenger demand, by moving beyond traditional multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) approaches that often struggle with data imbalance and convergence in realistic, non-loop network settings. The proposed method reformulates the bus holding control task as a single-agent reinforcement learning problem through a key innovation: augmenting the state space with categorical identifiers (such as vehicle ID, station ID, and time period) alongside numerical features, enabling the single agent to capture dependencies between buses, and designing a structured, ridge-shaped reward function to balance headway uniformity and schedule adherence. Experimental results in a simulated bidirectional timetabled network with dynamic demand demonstrate that the modified soft actor-critic (SAC) algorithm achieves more stable and superior performance compared to benchmarks like MADDPG, evidenced by a better cumulative reward (e.g., -430k vs. -530k under stochastic conditions), validating the framework's effectiveness for robust fleet control in real-world transit operations.
本文针对城市公交中因随机交通和客流需求导致的车辆串车问题，提出了一种新颖的单智能体强化学习框架，以克服传统多智能体强化学习方法在现实非环形线路、异构时刻表和动态需求等复杂运营场景中面临的数据不平衡与收敛难题。该方法的核心创新在于，通过将车辆ID、站点ID和时间段等分类标识符与车头时距、载客量等数值特征共同编码至高维状态空间，将多智能体控制问题重构为单智能体问题，使策略能够捕捉智能体间的依赖关系，并设计了一种兼顾均匀车头时距与时刻表遵循的结构化奖励函数。实验在一个具有动态客流的双向时刻表网络仿真中进行，结果表明，改进的软演员-评论家算法相比MADDPG等基准方法取得了更稳定、更优的性能（如在随机条件下累计奖励为-430k对比-530k），证明了这种结合分类结构编码和时刻表感知奖励的单智能体深度强化学习范式，能够为现实公交调度提供一种鲁棒且可扩展的替代方案。
Balancing the Reasoning Load: Difficulty-Differentiated Policy Optimization with Length Redistribution for Efficient and Robust Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yinan Xia, Haotian Zhang, Huiming Wang
First: 2026-03-19T06:30:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T06:30:26+00:00
Comments: 13 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have shown exceptional reasoning capabilities, but they also suffer from the issue of overthinking, often generating excessively long and redundant answers. For problems that exceed the model's capabilities, LRMs tend to exhibit the overconfidence phenomenon, generating overly short but incorrect answers, which may contribute to suboptimal performance. To address these issues, we propose Difficulty-Differentiated Policy Optimization (DDPO), an efficient reinforcement learning algorithm that optimizes simple and complex tasks separately based on the overconfidence phenomenon. Specifically, it reduces the output length for simple tasks without compromising accuracy, while for complex tasks, it expands the exploration space to improve performance. We further derive the theoretical conditions for maximizing expected accuracy, which require the length distribution to closely approximate the optimal length and be as concentrated as possible. Based on these conditions, we propose using the difficulty-level average as a well-founded reference for length optimization. Extensive experiments on both in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks validate the superiority and effectiveness of DDPO. Compared to GRPO, DDPO reduces the average answer length by 12% while improving accuracy by 1.85% across multiple benchmarks, achieving a better trade-off between accuracy and length. The code is available at https://github.com/Yinan-Xia/DDPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：平衡推理负载：基于难度差异化策略优化与长度重分布的高效鲁棒强化学习
大型推理模型（LRMs）展现出卓越的推理能力，但也存在过度思考的问题，常生成冗长冗余的答案。对于超出模型能力的问题，LRMs易出现过度自信现象，生成过短但错误的答案，导致性能欠佳。为解决这些问题，我们提出难度差异化策略优化（DDPO），这是一种基于过度自信现象、对简单与复杂任务分别优化的高效强化学习算法。具体而言，它在不损失准确性的前提下缩短简单任务的输出长度，同时为复杂任务扩展探索空间以提升性能。我们进一步推导了最大化期望准确率的理论条件，要求长度分布尽可能接近最优长度且高度集中。基于这些条件，我们提出以难度层级均值作为长度优化的理论依据。在领域内与跨领域基准测试上的大量实验验证了DDPO的优越性与有效性。相比GRPO，DDPO在多个基准测试中将平均答案长度降低12%，同时准确率提升1.85%，实现了准确率与长度间的更优权衡。代码发布于 https://github.com/Yinan-Xia/DDPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency and overconfidence issues in Large Reasoning Models (LRMs), where they often produce overly long answers for simple tasks and overly short, incorrect ones for complex tasks. To tackle this, the authors propose Difficulty-Differentiated Policy Optimization (DDPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm that separately optimizes simple tasks by reducing output length without sacrificing accuracy, and complex tasks by expanding exploration to enhance performance. Theoretical analysis guides length optimization using difficulty-level averages. Experimental results on various benchmarks show that DDPO reduces average answer length by 12% and improves accuracy by 1.85% compared to GRPO, achieving a better accuracy-length trade-off.
