Scaling Sim-to-Real Reinforcement Learning for Robot VLAs with Generative 3D Worlds
Authors: Andrew Choi, Xinjie Wang, Zhizhong Su, Wei Xu
First: 2026-03-19T06:22:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T06:22:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The strong performance of large vision-language models (VLMs) trained with reinforcement learning (RL) has motivated similar approaches for fine-tuning vision-language-action (VLA) models in robotics. Many recent works fine-tune VLAs directly in the real world to avoid addressing the sim-to-real gap. While real-world RL circumvents sim-to-real issues, it inherently limits the generality of the resulting VLA, as scaling scene and object diversity in the physical world is prohibitively difficult. This leads to the paradoxical outcome of transforming a broadly pretrained model into an overfitted, scene-specific policy. Training in simulation can instead provide access to diverse scenes, but designing those scenes is also costly. In this work, we show that VLAs can be RL fine-tuned without sacrificing generality and with reduced labor by leveraging 3D world generative models. Using these models together with a language-driven scene designer, we generate hundreds of diverse interactive scenes containing unique objects and backgrounds, enabling scalable and highly parallel policy learning. Starting from a pretrained imitation baseline, our approach increases simulation success from 9.7% to 79.8% while achieving a 1.25$\times$ speedup in task completion time. We further demonstrate successful sim-to-real transfer enabled by the quality of the generated digital twins together with domain randomization, improving real-world success from 21.7% to 75% and achieving a 1.13$\times$ speedup. Finally, we further highlight the benefits of leveraging the effectively unlimited data from 3D world generative models through an ablation study showing that increasing scene diversity directly improves zero-shot generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用生成式3D世界扩展机器人视觉语言动作模型的仿真到真实强化学习
通过强化学习训练的大型视觉语言模型表现优异，这推动了在机器人领域采用类似方法微调视觉语言动作模型。近期许多研究为避免仿真到真实的差异，直接在现实世界中微调VLA模型。尽管现实世界强化学习规避了仿真到真实的问题，却因物理世界中场景与物体多样性难以扩展，本质上限制了所得VLA模型的泛化能力，导致广泛预训练的模型退化为过拟合的场景专用策略。在仿真环境中训练虽能提供多样场景，但场景设计成本高昂。本研究证明，通过利用3D世界生成模型，可在保持泛化能力的同时降低人工成本，对VLA模型进行强化学习微调。结合语言驱动的场景设计器，我们生成数百个包含独特物体与背景的多样化交互场景，实现可扩展且高度并行的策略学习。从预训练的模仿基线出发，该方法将仿真成功率从9.7%提升至79.8%，任务完成时间加速1.25倍。通过生成数字孪生的质量与领域随机化技术，我们进一步实现了成功的仿真到真实迁移，将现实世界成功率从21.7%提高至75%，并加速1.13倍。最后，通过消融实验证明增加场景多样性可直接提升零样本泛化能力，凸显了利用3D世界生成模型近乎无限数据资源的优势。

The method leverages 3D world generative models and a language-driven scene designer to automatically produce hundreds of diverse interactive scenes, enabling scalable and parallel policy learning in simulation. 本文针对机器人视觉-语言-动作模型在强化学习微调中难以兼顾规模与泛化性的问题，提出了一种解决方案，因为现实世界训练多样性有限而仿真场景设计成本高昂。该方法利用3D世界生成模型和语言驱动的场景设计器，自动生成数百个多样化的交互场景，从而在仿真中实现可扩展的并行策略学习。实验结果表明，从预训练的模仿基线出发，该方法将仿真成功率从9.7%提升至79.8%，并加快了任务完成速度；通过领域随机化实现了成功的仿真到现实迁移，将现实世界成功率从21.7%提高至75%，同时证明增加场景多样性直接提升了零样本泛化能力。
Representation Finetuning for Continual Learning
Authors: Haihua Luo, Xuming Ran, Tommi Kärkkäinen, Huiyan Xue, Zhonghua Chen, Qi Xu, Fengyu Cong
First: 2026-03-11T18:15:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T06:17:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The world is inherently dynamic, and continual learning aims to enable models to adapt to ever-evolving data streams. While pre-trained models have shown powerful performance in continual learning, they still require finetuning to adapt effectively to downstream tasks. However, prevailing Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) methods operate through empirical, black-box optimization at the weight level. These approaches lack explicit control over representation drift, leading to sensitivity to domain shifts and catastrophic forgetting in continual learning scenarios. In this work, we introduce Continual Representation Learning (CoRe), a novel framework that for the first time shifts the finetuning paradigm from weight space to representation space. Unlike conventional methods, CoRe performs task-specific interventions within a low-rank linear subspace of hidden representations, adopting a learning process with explicit objectives, which ensures stability for past tasks while maintaining plasticity for new ones. By constraining updates to a low-rank subspace, CoRe achieves exceptional parameter efficiency. Extensive experiments across multiple continual learning benchmarks demonstrate that CoRe not only preserves parameter efficiency but also significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods. Our work introduces representation finetuning as a new, more effective and interpretable paradigm for continual learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：持续学习中的表示微调
世界本质上是动态的，持续学习旨在使模型能够适应不断变化的数据流。虽然预训练模型在持续学习中展现出强大性能，但仍需微调以有效适应下游任务。然而，当前主流的参数高效微调方法通过权重层面的经验性黑盒优化运作，缺乏对表示漂移的显式控制，导致对领域偏移敏感并在持续学习场景中出现灾难性遗忘。本文提出持续表示学习框架，首次将微调范式从权重空间转向表示空间。与传统方法不同，该框架在隐藏表示的低秩线性子空间内执行任务特定干预，采用具有显式目标的学习过程，确保对旧任务的稳定性同时保持对新任务的可塑性。通过将更新约束在低秩子空间，该方法实现了卓越的参数效率。在多个持续学习基准上的广泛实验表明，该框架不仅保持了参数效率，还显著超越了现有最优方法。本研究将表示微调确立为一种更高效、可解释的持续学习新范式。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of catastrophic forgetting in continual learning by proposing a shift from weight-level to representation-level adaptation. The authors introduce Continual Representation Learning (CoRe), a framework that performs task-specific interventions within a low-rank linear subspace of hidden representations, explicitly controlling representation drift to balance stability and plasticity. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks show that CoRe maintains parameter efficiency while significantly outperforming existing state-of-the-art methods, establishing representation finetuning as a more effective and interpretable paradigm.
本文针对持续学习中的灾难性遗忘问题，提出从权重层面适应转向表征层面适应的方法。作者引入了持续表征学习框架，通过在隐藏表征的低秩线性子空间中进行任务特定干预，显式控制表征漂移以平衡稳定性和可塑性。在多个基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法在保持参数高效的同时，显著优于现有最先进方法，确立了表征微调作为一种更有效且可解释的新范式。
HopChain: Multi-Hop Data Synthesis for Generalizable Vision-Language Reasoning
Authors: Shenzhi Wang, Shixuan Liu, Jing Zhou, Chang Gao, Xiong-Hui Chen, Binghai Wang, An Yang, Shiji Song, Bowen Yu, Gao Huang, Junyang Lin
First: 2026-03-17T18:04:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T04:12:29+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 8 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) show strong multimodal capabilities but still struggle with fine-grained vision-language reasoning. We find that long chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning exposes diverse failure modes, including perception, reasoning, knowledge, and hallucination errors, which can compound across intermediate steps. However, most existing vision-language data used for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) does not involve complex reasoning chains that rely on visual evidence throughout, leaving these weaknesses largely unexposed. We therefore propose HopChain, a scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop vision-language reasoning data for RLVR training of VLMs. Each synthesized multi-hop query forms a logically dependent chain of instance-grounded hops, where earlier hops establish the instances, sets, or conditions needed for later hops, while the final answer remains a specific, unambiguous number suitable for verifiable rewards. We train Qwen3.5-35B-A3B and Qwen3.5-397B-A17B under two RLVR settings: the original data alone, and the original data plus HopChain's multi-hop data, and compare them across 24 benchmarks spanning STEM and Puzzle, General VQA, Text Recognition and Document Understanding, and Video Understanding. Although this multi-hop data is not synthesized for any specific benchmark, it improves 20 of 24 benchmarks on both models, indicating broad and generalizable gains. Consistently, replacing full chained queries with half-multi-hop or single-hop variants reduces the average score across five representative benchmarks from 70.4 to 66.7 and 64.3, respectively. Notably, multi-hop gains peak in long-CoT vision-language reasoning, exceeding 50 points in the ultra-long-CoT regime. These experiments establish HopChain as an effective, scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop data that improves generalizable vision-language reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HopChain：面向可泛化视觉语言推理的多跳数据合成框架
视觉语言模型（VLMs）展现出强大的多模态能力，但在细粒度视觉语言推理方面仍存在不足。研究发现，长链思维推理会暴露多种错误模式，包括感知、推理、知识和幻觉错误，这些错误可能在中间步骤中累积。然而，现有大多数用于可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的视觉语言数据并未涉及全程依赖视觉证据的复杂推理链，导致这些缺陷难以被充分揭示。为此，我们提出HopChain——一个可扩展的框架，用于合成多跳视觉语言推理数据以支持VLMs的RLVR训练。每个合成的多跳查询构成逻辑上相互依赖的实例锚定跳链，其中前序跳跃为后续跳跃建立所需的实例、集合或条件，而最终答案保持为适用于可验证奖励的明确数值。我们在两种RLVR设置下训练Qwen3.5-35B-A3B和Qwen3.5-397B-A17B模型：仅使用原始数据，以及原始数据结合HopChain的多跳数据，并在涵盖STEM与谜题、通用VQA、文本识别与文档理解、视频理解等24个基准测试中进行比较。尽管多跳数据并非针对特定基准设计，但它在两个模型上均提升了20个基准的性能，显示出广泛且可泛化的增益。一致地，将完整链式查询替换为半多跳或单跳变体会使五个代表性基准的平均得分分别从70.4降至66.7和64.3。值得注意的是，多跳增益在长链视觉语言推理中尤为显著，在超长链推理场景中提升超过50分。这些实验证明HopChain是一种高效、可扩展的多跳数据合成框架，能显著提升视觉语言推理的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that vision-language models (VLMs) exhibit diverse failure modes in fine-grained reasoning, such as perception and hallucination errors, which compound in long chain-of-thought processes, yet existing training data often lacks complex, visually-grounded reasoning chains. To address this, the authors propose HopChain, a scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop vision-language reasoning data where each query forms a logically dependent chain of instance-grounded steps, with a final unambiguous numeric answer suitable for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. Experimental results show that training VLMs with this multi-hop data improves performance on 20 out of 24 diverse benchmarks, including STEM and video understanding, with gains especially pronounced in long chain-of-thought reasoning, and ablation studies confirm the importance of full multi-hop chains over simplified variants.

AcceRL: A Distributed Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning and World Model Framework for Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Chengxuan Lu, Shukuan Wang, Yanjie Li, Wei Liu, Shiji Jin, Fuyuan Qian, Peiming Li, Baigui Sun, Yang Liu
First: 2026-03-19T03:50:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T03:50:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) for large-scale Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models faces significant challenges in computational efficiency and data acquisition. We propose AcceRL, a fully asynchronous and decoupled RL framework designed to eliminate synchronization barriers by physically isolating training, inference, and rollouts. Crucially, AcceRL is the first to integrate a plug-and-play, trainable world model into a distributed asynchronous RL pipeline to generate virtual experiences. Experiments on the LIBERO benchmark demonstrate that AcceRL achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance. Systematically, it exhibits super-linear scaling in throughput and highly efficient hardware utilization. Algorithmically, the world-model-augmented variant delivers unprecedented sample efficiency and robust training stability in complex control tasks.
中文标题/摘要

大规模视觉-语言-动作模型的强化学习在计算效率与数据获取方面面临显著挑战。本文提出AcceRL——一个完全异步解耦的强化学习框架，通过物理隔离训练、推理与轨迹采样消除同步壁垒。其核心创新在于首次将即插即用、可训练的世界模型集成至分布式异步强化学习流程中以生成虚拟经验。在LIBERO基准测试中，AcceRL实现了最先进的性能表现：系统层面展现出超线性吞吐扩展与高效硬件利用率；算法层面，世界模型增强版本在复杂控制任务中实现了前所未有的样本效率与鲁棒训练稳定性。

The motivation for AcceRL stems from the computational inefficiency and data scarcity challenges in scaling reinforcement learning for large Vision-Language-Action models. The method introduces a fully asynchronous, decoupled framework that isolates training, inference, and rollout processes to remove synchronization bottlenecks, and innovatively integrates a plug-and-play, trainable world model to generate synthetic experiences. Experimental results on the LIBERO benchmark show that AcceRL achieves state-of-the-art performance, demonstrates super-linear scaling in throughput with efficient hardware use, and its world-model variant yields exceptional sample efficiency and training stability in complex tasks.
AcceRL的提出动机源于大规模视觉-语言-动作模型的强化学习在计算效率和数据获取方面面临重大挑战。该方法采用了一个完全异步、解耦的框架，通过物理隔离训练、推理和轨迹采样来消除同步障碍，并创新性地集成了一个即插即用、可训练的世界模型来生成虚拟经验。在LIBERO基准测试上的实验结果表明，AcceRL实现了最先进的性能，系统吞吐量呈现超线性扩展且硬件利用率高，其世界模型变体在复杂控制任务中提供了前所未有的样本效率和稳健的训练稳定性。
Discounted Beta--Bernoulli Reward Estimation for Sample-Efficient Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Haechan Kim, Soohyun Ryu, Gyouk Chu, Doohyuk Jang, Eunho Yang
First: 2026-03-19T03:10:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T03:10:47+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as an effective post-training paradigm for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models. However, existing group-based RLVR methods often suffer from severe sample inefficiency. This inefficiency stems from reliance on point estimation of rewards from a small number of rollouts, leading to high estimation variance, variance collapse, and ineffective utilization of generated responses. In this work, we reformulate RLVR from a statistical estimation perspective by modeling rewards as samples drawn from a policy-induced distribution and casting advantage computation as the problem of estimating the reward distribution from finite data. Building on this view, we propose Discounted Beta--Bernoulli (DBB) reward estimation, which leverages historical reward statistics for the non-stationary distribution. Although biased, the resulting estimator exhibits reduced and stable variance, theoretically avoids estimated variance collapse, and achieves lower mean squared error than standard point estimation. Extensive experiments across six in-distribution and three out-of-distribution reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that GRPO with DBB consistently outperforms naive GRPO, achieving average Acc@8 improvements of 3.22/2.42 points in-distribution and 12.49/6.92 points out-of-distribution on the 1.7B and 8B models, respectively, without additional computational cost or memory usage.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于折扣Beta-Bernoulli奖励估计的样本高效强化学习与可验证奖励机制
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的有效后训练范式。然而，现有基于分组的RLVR方法常受样本效率低下的困扰，其根源在于依赖少量轨迹的奖励点估计，导致估计方差高、方差塌缩及生成响应利用不足。本研究从统计估计视角重构RLVR：将奖励建模为策略诱导分布的抽样样本，并将优势计算转化为有限数据下估计奖励分布的问题。基于此视角，我们提出折扣Beta-Bernoulli（DBB）奖励估计方法，该方法利用历史奖励统计量处理非平稳分布。虽然存在偏差，但所得估计量展现出降低且稳定的方差，理论上避免估计方差塌缩，且比标准点估计具有更低的均方误差。在六个分布内和三个分布外推理基准上的大量实验表明：采用DBB的GRPO始终优于原始GRPO，在17亿和80亿参数模型上分别实现分布内平均Acc@8提升3.22/2.42分、分布外提升12.49/6.92分，且未增加计算成本或内存占用。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the sample inefficiency of existing group-based reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) methods, which rely on high-variance point estimates from few rollouts, this work reformulates RLVR as a statistical estimation problem. The proposed method, Discounted Beta-Bernoulli (DBB) reward estimation, models rewards from a policy-induced distribution and leverages historical statistics to estimate the non-stationary reward distribution, yielding a biased but lower-variance estimator that avoids variance collapse and reduces mean squared error. Experimental results across multiple reasoning benchmarks show that GRPO with DBB outperforms naive GRPO, achieving significant accuracy improvements in both in-distribution and out-of-distribution settings for 1.7B and 8B models without extra computational cost.
针对现有基于群体的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）方法因依赖少量样本的点估计而导致样本效率低下的问题，本研究从统计估计角度重新构建了RLVR。所提出的方法——折扣Beta-Bernoulli（DBB）奖励估计——将奖励建模为策略诱导分布的样本，并利用历史统计数据来估计非平稳奖励分布，从而得到一个有偏但方差更低、避免方差崩溃且均方误差更小的估计器。在多个推理基准上的实验结果表明，采用DBB的GRPO优于朴素GRPO，在1.7B和8B模型上，无论分布内还是分布外设置，均实现了显著的准确率提升，且无需额外计算成本或内存开销。
The Flexibility Trap: Why Arbitrary Order Limits Reasoning Potential in Diffusion Language Models
Authors: Zanlin Ni, Shenzhi Wang, Yang Yue, Tianyu Yu, Weilin Zhao, Yeguo Hua, Tianyi Chen, Jun Song, Cheng Yu, Bo Zheng, Gao Huang
First: 2026-01-21T16:41:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T02:53:39+00:00
Comments: Code and pre-trained models: https://github.com/LeapLabTHU/JustGRPO
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) break the rigid left-to-right constraint of traditional LLMs, enabling token generation in arbitrary orders. Intuitively, this flexibility implies a solution space that strictly supersets the fixed autoregressive trajectory, theoretically unlocking superior reasoning potential for general tasks like mathematics and coding. Consequently, numerous works have leveraged reinforcement learning (RL) to elicit the reasoning capability of dLLMs. In this paper, we reveal a counter-intuitive reality: arbitrary order generation, in its current form, narrows rather than expands the reasoning boundary of dLLMs. We find that dLLMs tend to exploit this order flexibility to bypass high-uncertainty tokens that are crucial for exploration, leading to a premature collapse of the solution space. This observation motivates a rethink of RL approaches for dLLMs, where considerable complexities, such as handling combinatorial trajectories and intractable likelihoods, are often devoted to preserving this flexibility. We demonstrate that effective reasoning can be better elicited by intentionally forgoing arbitrary order and applying standard Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) instead. Our approach, JustGRPO, is minimalist yet surprisingly effective (e.g., 89.1% accuracy on GSM8K) while fully retaining the parallel decoding ability of dLLMs. Project page: https://nzl-thu.github.io/the-flexibility-trap
中文标题/摘要
标题：灵活性陷阱：为何任意顺序限制扩散语言模型的推理潜力
扩散大语言模型（dLLMs）打破了传统LLM严格的从左到右约束，实现了按任意顺序生成词元。直观上，这种灵活性意味着其解空间严格包含了固定自回归轨迹，理论上为数学和编程等通用任务解锁了更优的推理潜力。因此，许多研究利用强化学习（RL）来激发dLLMs的推理能力。本文揭示了一个反直觉的现实：当前形式的任意顺序生成非但没有扩展dLLMs的推理边界，反而使其收窄。我们发现dLLMs倾向于利用这种顺序灵活性来规避对探索至关重要的高不确定性词元，导致解空间过早坍缩。这一观察促使我们重新思考针对dLLMs的RL方法——现有方法往往投入大量复杂度（如处理组合轨迹和难解似然）以维持这种灵活性。我们证明，通过主动放弃任意顺序并改用标准组相对策略优化（GRPO），反而能更好地激发有效推理。我们的方法JustGRPO极简却出奇有效（如在GSM8K上达到89.1%准确率），同时完全保留了dLLMs的并行解码能力。项目页面：https://nzl-thu.github.io/the-flexibility-trap

This paper challenges the assumption that arbitrary token generation order in diffusion language models inherently enhances reasoning, showing instead that it can lead models to avoid uncertain but critical tokens, thereby prematurely narrowing the solution space. The authors propose a minimalist method, JustGRPO, which intentionally forgoes arbitrary order generation and applies standard Group Relative Policy Optimization, effectively eliciting reasoning while retaining parallel decoding. Experimental results demonstrate its effectiveness, achieving 89.1% accuracy on the GSM8K benchmark.
本文挑战了扩散语言模型中任意顺序生成令牌能增强推理能力的假设，揭示其反而可能导致模型回避关键但不确定的令牌，从而过早缩小解空间。作者提出了一种极简方法JustGRPO，有意放弃任意顺序生成，采用标准组相对策略优化，在保持并行解码的同时有效激发推理能力。实验结果显示该方法效果显著，在GSM8K基准测试上达到了89.1%的准确率。
Adaptive Decoding via Test-Time Policy Learning for Self-Improving Generation
Authors: Asmita Bhardwaj, Yuya Jeremy Ong, Eelaaf Zahid, Basel Shbita
First: 2026-03-19T02:44:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T02:44:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decoding strategies largely determine the quality of Large Language Model (LLM) outputs, yet widely used heuristics such as greedy or fixed temperature/top-p decoding are static and often task-agnostic, leading to suboptimal or inconsistent generation quality across domains that demand stylistic or structural flexibility. We introduce a reinforcement learning-based decoder sampler that treats decoding as sequential decision-making and learns a lightweight policy to adjust sampling parameters at test-time while keeping LLM weights frozen. We evaluated summarization datasets including BookSum, arXiv, and WikiHow using Granite-3.3-2B and Qwen-2.5-0.5B. Our policy sampler consistently outperforms greedy and static baselines, achieving relative gains of up to +88% (BookSum, Granite) and +79% (WikiHow, Qwen). Reward ablations show that overlap-only objectives underperform compared to composite rewards, while structured shaping terms (length, coverage, repetition, completeness) enable stable and sustained improvements. These findings highlight reinforcement learning as a practical mechanism for test-time adaptation in decoding, enabling domain-aware and user-controllable generation without retraining large models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于测试时策略学习的自适应解码实现自改进生成
解码策略在很大程度上决定了大型语言模型（LLM）输出的质量，但广泛使用的启发式方法（如贪婪解码或固定温度/top-p解码）是静态且通常与任务无关的，导致在需要风格或结构灵活性的领域中生成质量次优或不一致。我们提出一种基于强化学习的解码器采样器，将解码视为序列决策过程，通过学习轻量级策略在测试时调整采样参数，同时保持LLM权重不变。我们在BookSum、arXiv和WikiHow等摘要数据集上使用Granite-3.3-2B和Qwen-2.5-0.5B进行评估。我们的策略采样器始终优于贪婪和静态基线，在BookSum（Granite）和WikiHow（Qwen）上分别实现最高+88%和+79%的相对提升。奖励消融实验表明，仅使用重叠度目标的效果低于复合奖励，而结构化约束项（长度、覆盖率、重复度、完整性）能实现稳定持续的改进。这些发现凸显了强化学习作为解码过程中测试时适应的实用机制，可在无需重新训练大模型的情况下实现领域感知和用户可控的生成。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of static decoding strategies like greedy or fixed temperature sampling, which are task-agnostic and often yield suboptimal generation quality across diverse domains, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning-based decoder sampler that treats decoding as sequential decision-making. The method learns a lightweight policy to dynamically adjust sampling parameters at test-time while keeping the underlying large language model weights frozen, enabling domain-aware adaptation without retraining. 针对贪婪或固定温度采样等静态解码策略任务无关、在不同领域常导致生成质量次优的问题，本文提出了一种基于强化学习的解码器采样器，将解码视为序列决策过程。该方法通过学习一个轻量级策略，在测试时动态调整采样参数，同时保持大语言模型权重不变，从而无需重新训练即可实现领域感知的适应。在BookSum、arXiv和WikiHow等摘要数据集上使用Granite-3.3-2B和Qwen-2.5-0.5B模型的实验结果表明，该策略采样器始终优于贪婪和静态基线，在Granite模型上的BookSum数据集实现了高达+88%的相对提升，在Qwen模型上的WikiHow数据集实现了+79%的提升。奖励消融实验显示，结合长度、覆盖度、重复性和完整性等结构化塑造项的复合奖励能带来稳定改进，而仅基于重叠度的目标则表现较差。
Self-Tuning Sparse Attention: Multi-Fidelity Hyperparameter Optimization for Transformer Acceleration
Authors: Arundhathi Dev, Justin Zhan
First: 2026-03-19T02:24:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T02:24:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the International Conference on Machine Intelligence Theory and Applications (MiTA 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sparse attention mechanisms promise to break the quadratic bottleneck of long-context transformers, yet production adoption remains limited by a critical usability gap: optimal hyperparameters vary substantially across layers and models, and current methods (e.g., SpargeAttn) rely on manual grid search to identify them. We propose AFBS-BO (Adaptive Fidelity Binary Search with Bayesian Optimization), a fully automated framework that discovers optimal layer- and head-specific hyperparameters without human intervention. Our hybrid algorithm combines Bayesian Optimization for global exploration with binary search for local refinement, leveraging multi-fidelity evaluation across sequence lengths to reduce tuning cost. On Llama-2-7B, AFBS-BO accelerates hyperparameter discovery by 3.4x with 8.8x fewer evaluations than grid search, and identifies high-sparsity configurations that outperform existing sparse attention baselines while closely matching dense attention quality. By transforming sparse attention from a manually tuned heuristic into a self-optimizing primitive, AFBS-BO enables plug-and-play acceleration across diverse transformer architectures and domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自调优稀疏注意力：面向Transformer加速的多保真度超参数优化
稀疏注意力机制有望突破长上下文Transformer的二次复杂度瓶颈，但其实际应用仍受限于关键可用性缺陷：最优超参数在不同层级和模型间差异显著，现有方法（如SpargeAttn）依赖人工网格搜索进行参数确定。本文提出AFBS-BO（基于贝叶斯优化的自适应保真度二分搜索），这是一种全自动框架，可在无需人工干预的情况下发现最优的层级与注意力头专属超参数。该混合算法结合了全局探索的贝叶斯优化与局部细化的二分搜索，通过跨序列长度的多保真度评估降低调优成本。在Llama-2-7B模型上，AFBS-BO以比网格搜索少8.8倍的评估次数实现3.4倍的超参数发现加速，并识别出优于现有稀疏注意力基线的高稀疏配置，同时紧密匹配稠密注意力的质量。通过将稀疏注意力从人工调优的启发式方法转化为自优化原语，AFBS-BO实现了跨多样化Transformer架构与领域的即插即用加速。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the usability gap in sparse attention mechanisms for transformers, where optimal hyperparameters vary widely across layers and models, and current methods rely on inefficient manual grid search. The method introduces AFBS-BO, an automated framework that combines Bayesian Optimization for global exploration with binary search for local refinement, using multi-fidelity evaluation across sequence lengths to reduce tuning costs. Experimental results on Llama-2-7B show that AFBS-BO accelerates hyperparameter discovery by 3.4x with 8.8x fewer evaluations than grid search, identifying high-sparsity configurations that outperform existing sparse attention baselines while maintaining dense attention quality.

From Logs to Language: Learning Optimal Verbalization for LLM-Based Recommendation at Industry Scale
Authors: Yucheng Shi, Ying Li, Yu Wang, Yesu Feng, Arjun Rao, Rein Houthooft, Shradha Sehgal, Jin Wang, Hao Zhen, Ninghao Liu, Linas Baltrunas
First: 2026-02-24T05:15:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T02:21:57+00:00
Comments: Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are promising backbones for generative recommender systems, yet a key challenge remains underexplored: verbalization, i.e., converting structured user interaction logs into effective natural language inputs. Existing methods rely on rigid templates that simply concatenate fields, yielding suboptimal representations for recommendation. We propose a data-centric framework that learns verbalization for LLM-based recommendation. Using reinforcement learning, a verbalization agent transforms raw interaction histories into optimized textual contexts, with recommendation accuracy as the training signal. This agent learns to filter noise, incorporate relevant metadata, and reorganize information to improve downstream predictions. Experiments on a large-scale industrial streaming dataset from Netflix show that learned verbalization delivers up to 93% relative improvement in discovery item recommendation accuracy over template-based baselines. Further analysis reveals emergent strategies such as user interest summarization, noise removal, and syntax normalization, offering insights into effective context construction for LLM-based recommender systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从日志到语言：工业级LLM推荐系统中最优语言化表达的学习

RE-SAC: Disentangling aleatoric and epistemic risks in bus fleet control: A stable and robust ensemble DRL approach
Authors: Yifan Zhang, Liang Zheng
First: 2026-03-19T01:37:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T01:37:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bus holding control is challenging due to stochastic traffic and passenger demand. While deep reinforcement learning (DRL) shows promise, standard actor-critic algorithms suffer from Q-value instability in volatile environments. A key source of this instability is the conflation of two distinct uncertainties: aleatoric uncertainty (irreducible noise) and epistemic uncertainty (data insufficiency). Treating these as a single risk leads to value underestimation in noisy states, causing catastrophic policy collapse. We propose a robust ensemble soft actor-critic (RE-SAC) framework to explicitly disentangle these uncertainties. RE-SAC applies Integral Probability Metric (IPM)-based weight regularization to the critic network to hedge against aleatoric risk, providing a smooth analytical lower bound for the robust Bellman operator without expensive inner-loop perturbations. To address epistemic risk, a diversified Q-ensemble penalizes overconfident value estimates in sparsely covered regions. This dual mechanism prevents the ensemble variance from misidentifying noise as a data gap, a failure mode identified in our ablation study. Experiments in a realistic bidirectional bus corridor simulation demonstrate that RE-SAC achieves the highest cumulative reward (approx. -0.4e6) compared to vanilla SAC (-0.55e6). Mahalanobis rareness analysis confirms that RE-SAC reduces Oracle Q-value estimation error by up to 62% in rare out-of-distribution states (MAE of 1647 vs. 4343), demonstrating superior robustness under high traffic variability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RE-SAC：公交车队控制中可分离与认知风险的解耦：一种稳定鲁棒的集成深度强化学习方法
公交车驻站控制因随机交通和乘客需求而具有挑战性。尽管深度强化学习（DRL）展现出潜力，但标准演员-评论家算法在波动环境中存在Q值不稳定的问题。这一不稳定的关键根源在于两种不同不确定性的混淆：可分离不确定性（不可约噪声）和认知不确定性（数据不足）。将其视为单一风险会导致噪声状态下的价值低估，引发灾难性策略崩溃。我们提出一种鲁棒集成软演员-评论家（RE-SAC）框架，以显式解耦这两种不确定性。RE-SAC在评论家网络中应用基于积分概率度量（IPM）的权重正则化来对冲可分离风险，为鲁棒贝尔曼算子提供平滑的解析下界，而无需昂贵的内部循环扰动。针对认知风险，采用多样化Q集成惩罚稀疏覆盖区域的过度自信价值估计。这种双重机制防止集成方差将噪声误判为数据缺口——这是我们在消融研究中发现的一种失效模式。在真实双向公交走廊仿真中的实验表明，RE-SAC相比原始SAC（-0.55e6）获得了最高累积奖励（约-0.4e6）。马氏稀有度分析证实，RE-SAC在罕见分布外状态下将Oracle Q值估计误差降低了高达62%（MAE为1647 vs. 4343），展现了高交通变异性下的卓越鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the instability of deep reinforcement learning (DRL) in bus holding control, where standard actor-critic methods conflate aleatoric and epistemic uncertainties, leading to value underestimation and policy collapse. The proposed RE-SAC framework explicitly disentangles these risks: it uses Integral Probability Metric-based weight regularization on the critic to hedge against aleatoric uncertainty, providing a smooth analytical lower bound, and employs a diversified Q-ensemble to penalize overconfident estimates in data-sparse regions, preventing misidentification of noise as data gaps. Experimental results in a bidirectional bus corridor simulation show RE-SAC achieves the highest cumulative reward (approximately -0.4e6) compared to vanilla SAC (-0.55e6), and reduces Oracle Q-value estimation error by up to 62% in rare out-of-distribution states, demonstrating superior robustness under high traffic variability.
本文针对公交驻站控制中深度强化学习的不稳定性问题展开研究，标准行动者-评论者算法因混淆了偶然不确定性和认知不确定性，导致价值低估与策略崩溃。提出的RE-SAC框架显式解耦了这两种风险：采用基于积分概率度量的评论家网络权重正则化来对冲偶然不确定性，提供平滑的解析下界；并利用多样化的Q值集成惩罚数据稀疏区域的过度自信估计，防止将噪声误判为数据缺口。在双向公交走廊仿真实验中，RE-SAC获得了最高的累积奖励（约-0.4e6），优于原始SAC（-0.55e6），且在罕见分布外状态下将Oracle Q值估计误差降低了高达62%，证明了其在高度交通波动下的优越鲁棒性。

PowerFlow: Unlocking the Dual Nature of LLMs via Principled Distribution Matching
Authors: Ruishuo Chen, Yu Chen, Zhuoran Li, Longbo Huang
First: 2026-03-19T00:00:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T00:00:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unsupervised Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF) has emerged as a promising paradigm for eliciting the latent capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) without external supervision. However, current methods rely on heuristic intrinsic rewards, which often lack a well-defined theoretical optimization target and are prone to degenerative biases. In this work, we introduce PowerFlow, a principled framework that reformulates unsupervised fine-tuning as a distribution matching problem. By casting GFlowNet as an amortized variational sampler for unnormalized densities, we propose a length-aware Trajectory-Balance objective that explicitly neutralizes the structural length biases inherent in autoregressive generation. By targeting $α$-power distributions, PowerFlow enables the directional elicitation of the dual nature of LLMs: sharpening the distribution ($α> 1$) to intensify logical reasoning, or flattening it ($α< 1$) to unlock expressive creativity. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PowerFlow consistently outperforms existing RLIF methods, matching or even exceeding supervised GRPO. Furthermore, by mitigating over-sharpening in aligned models, our approach achieves simultaneous gains in diversity and quality, shifting the Pareto frontier in creative tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PowerFlow：通过基于分布匹配的原则性方法释放大语言模型的双重特性
基于内部反馈的无监督强化学习已成为一种无需外部监督即可激发大语言模型潜在能力的有前景范式。然而，现有方法依赖启发式内在奖励，往往缺乏明确的理论优化目标，且易产生退化偏差。本研究提出PowerFlow，这是一个将无监督微调重构为分布匹配问题的原则性框架。通过将GFlowNet构建为未归一化密度的摊销变分采样器，我们提出一种显式中和自回归生成固有结构长度偏差的长度感知轨迹平衡目标。通过以α幂分布为目标，PowerFlow能够定向激发大语言模型的双重特性：锐化分布（α>1）以增强逻辑推理能力，或展平分布（α<1）以释放表达创造力。大量实验表明，PowerFlow持续优于现有RLIF方法，达到甚至超越有监督GRPO性能。此外，通过缓解对齐模型中的过度锐化问题，我们的方法在多样性与质量上实现同步提升，推动了创造性任务的帕累托前沿边界。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of heuristic intrinsic rewards in unsupervised Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF), which lack theoretical grounding and suffer from degenerative biases, this paper introduces PowerFlow, a principled framework that reformulates unsupervised fine-tuning as a distribution matching problem. The method employs GFlowNet as an amortized variational sampler and proposes a length-aware Trajectory-Balance objective to neutralize structural length biases in autoregressive generation, enabling targeted elicitation of LLMs' dual capabilities by matching α-power distributions—sharpening for logical reasoning (α>1) or flattening for creativity (α<1). Experimental results show that PowerFlow consistently outperforms existing RLIF methods, matches or exceeds supervised GRPO, and mitigates over-sharpening in aligned models to achieve simultaneous gains in diversity and quality, advancing the Pareto frontier in creative tasks.
针对无监督内部反馈强化学习中启发式内在奖励缺乏理论依据且易产生退化偏差的问题，本文提出了PowerFlow框架，将无监督微调重新定义为分布匹配问题。该方法将GFlowNet用作未归一化密度的摊销变分采样器，并提出了长度感知的轨迹平衡目标，以消除自回归生成中的结构长度偏差，通过匹配α幂分布来定向激发大语言模型的双重能力：锐化分布（α>1）以增强逻辑推理，或平缓分布（α<1）以释放表达创造力。大量实验表明，PowerFlow持续优于现有无监督内部反馈强化学习方法，匹配甚至超越了有监督的GRPO，并通过缓解对齐模型中的过度锐化，在多样性和质量上同时取得提升，推动了创意任务中的帕累托前沿。
Shifting Uncertainty to Critical Moments: Towards Reliable Uncertainty Quantification for VLA Model
Authors: Yanchuan Tang, Taowen Wang, Yuefei Chen, Boxuan Zhang, Qiang Guan, Ruixiang Tang
First: 2026-03-18T22:52:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T22:52:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models enable general-purpose robotic policies by mapping visual observations and language instructions to low-level actions, but they often lack reliable introspection. A common practice is to compute a token-level uncertainty signal and take its mean over a rollout. However, mean aggregation can dilute short-lived but safety-critical uncertainty spikes in continuous control. In particular, successful rollouts may contain localized high-entropy segments due to benign noise or non-critical micro-adjustments, while failure rollouts can appear low-entropy for most timesteps and only exhibit brief spikes near the onset of failure. We propose a unified uncertainty quantification approach for predicting rollout success versus failure that (1) uses max-based sliding window pooling to preserve transient risk signals, (2) applies motion-aware stability weighting to emphasize high-frequency action oscillations associated with unstable behaviors, and (3) performs DoF-adaptive calibration via Bayesian Optimization to prioritize kinematically critical axes. Experiments on the LIBERO benchmark show that our method substantially improves failure prediction accuracy and yields more reliable signals for failure detection, which can support downstream human-in-the-loop interventions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将不确定性转移至关键节点：面向视觉-语言-动作模型的可靠不确定性量化方法
视觉-语言-动作模型通过将视觉观测与语言指令映射为底层动作来实现通用机器人策略，但常缺乏可靠的自我评估能力。现有方法通常计算词元级不确定性信号并在执行轨迹上取均值，但均值聚合会弱化连续控制中短暂却关乎安全的不确定性峰值。具体而言，成功轨迹可能因良性噪声或非关键微调包含局部高熵片段，而失败轨迹在多数时间步可能呈现低熵，仅在临近失效时出现短暂峰值。本文提出一种预测轨迹成功与失败的统一不确定性量化方法：（1）采用基于最大值的滑动窗口池化以保留瞬态风险信号；（2）应用运动感知稳定性加权以强调与不稳定行为相关的高频动作振荡；（3）通过贝叶斯优化进行自由度自适应校准以优先处理运动学关键轴。在LIBERO基准测试上的实验表明，该方法显著提升了故障预测准确率，并生成更可靠的故障检测信号，可支持下游人机协同干预。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for reliable introspection in Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models for robotics, where standard mean aggregation of token-level uncertainty can obscure brief but critical failure signals, this paper proposes a unified uncertainty quantification method. The approach employs max-based sliding window pooling to capture transient risk, motion-aware stability weighting to highlight unstable high-frequency action oscillations, and degree-of-freedom-adaptive calibration via Bayesian Optimization to prioritize critical kinematic axes. Experimental results on the LIBERO benchmark demonstrate that the method substantially improves failure prediction accuracy and provides more reliable signals for failure detection, thereby supporting potential human-in-the-loop interventions.
本文的动机在于解决视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在机器人应用中缺乏可靠自省能力的问题，传统基于平均的令牌级不确定性聚合会稀释短暂但关键的安全风险信号。为此，作者提出了一种统一的量化方法，该方法采用基于最大值的滑动窗口池化以保留瞬态风险，应用运动感知的稳定性加权来强调与不稳定行为相关的高频动作振荡，并通过贝叶斯优化进行自由度自适应校准以优先处理运动学关键轴。在LIBERO基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法显著提高了故障预测的准确性，并产生了更可靠的故障检测信号，从而为下游的人机协同干预提供了支持。
Escaping Offline Pessimism: Vector-Field Reward Shaping for Safe Frontier Exploration
Authors: Amirhossein Roknilamouki, Arnob Ghosh, Eylem Ekici, Ness B. Shroff
First: 2026-03-18T22:18:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T22:18:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While offline reinforcement learning provides reliable policies for real-world deployment, its inherent pessimism severely restricts an agent's ability to explore and collect novel data online. Drawing inspiration from safe reinforcement learning, exploring near the boundary of regions well covered by the offline dataset and reliably modeled by the simulator allows an agent to take manageable risks--venturing into informative but moderate-uncertainty states while remaining close enough to familiar regions for safe recovery. However, naively rewarding this boundary-seeking behavior can lead to a degenerate parking behavior, where the agent simply stops once it reaches the frontier. To solve this, we propose a novel vector-field reward shaping paradigm designed to induce continuous, safe boundary exploration for non-adaptive deployed policies. Operating on an uncertainty oracle trained from offline data, our reward combines two complementary components: a gradient-alignment term that attracts the agent toward a target uncertainty level, and a rotational-flow term that promotes motion along the local tangent plane of the uncertainty manifold. Through theoretical analysis, we show that this reward structure naturally induces sustained exploratory behavior along the boundary while preventing degenerate solutions. Empirically, by integrating our proposed reward shaping with Soft Actor-Critic on a 2D continuous navigation task, we validate that agents successfully traverse uncertainty boundaries while balancing safe, informative data collection with primary task completion.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破离线悲观主义：基于向量场奖励塑形的安全边界探索
离线强化学习虽能为实际部署提供可靠策略，但其固有的悲观性严重限制了智能体在线探索与收集新数据的能力。受安全强化学习启发，在离线数据集充分覆盖且仿真器可靠建模的区域边界附近探索，可使智能体承担可控风险——既能进入信息丰富但不确定性适中的状态，又能保持与熟悉区域足够接近以实现安全恢复。然而，简单奖励这种边界探索行为可能导致退化的驻留行为，即智能体抵达边界后便停滞不前。为此，我们提出一种新颖的向量场奖励塑形范式，旨在为非自适应部署策略诱导持续、安全的边界探索。该方法基于离线数据训练的不确定性预测器，将两个互补组件结合：梯度对齐项引导智能体趋近目标不确定性水平，旋流项则促进沿不确定性流形局部切平面的运动。理论分析表明，该奖励结构能自然诱导沿边界的持续探索行为，同时避免退化解。通过将所提奖励塑形与软演员-评论家算法在二维连续导航任务中集成，实证验证了智能体在平衡安全信息收集与主任务完成的同时，能成功遍历不确定性边界。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem that offline reinforcement learning's inherent pessimism limits an agent's ability to explore novel states online. To enable safe and informative exploration, the authors propose a vector-field reward shaping method that guides an agent to explore near the boundary of well-covered, low-uncertainty regions, where risks are manageable. The method uses an uncertainty oracle to shape rewards with two components: a gradient-alignment term directing the agent toward a target uncertainty level and a rotational-flow term encouraging motion along the uncertainty boundary, thereby preventing degenerate parking behavior. Experimental results on a 2D continuous navigation task, using Soft Actor-Critic, demonstrate that agents equipped with this reward successfully traverse uncertainty boundaries, balancing safe data collection with task completion.
本文针对离线强化学习固有的悲观性限制智能体在线探索新状态的问题，提出了一种向量场奖励塑形方法，以引导智能体在覆盖良好、低不确定性的区域边界附近进行安全且信息丰富的探索。该方法利用不确定性预言机，通过梯度对齐项将智能体导向目标不确定性水平，并通过旋转流项促使其沿不确定性边界运动，从而避免智能体到达边界后停滞的退化行为。在二维连续导航任务中，结合柔性演员-评论家算法的实验结果表明，采用该奖励塑形的智能体能成功遍历不确定性边界，在安全收集数据的同时完成主要任务。
Learning to Reason with Curriculum I: Provable Benefits of Autocurriculum
Authors: Nived Rajaraman, Audrey Huang, Miro Dudik, Robert Schapire, Dylan J. Foster, Akshay Krishnamurthy
First: 2026-03-18T22:17:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T22:17:22+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chain-of-thought reasoning, where language models expend additional computation by producing thinking tokens prior to final responses, has driven significant advances in model capabilities. However, training these reasoning models is extremely costly in terms of both data and compute, as it involves collecting long traces of reasoning behavior from humans or synthetic generators and further post-training the model via reinforcement learning. Are these costs fundamental, or can they be reduced through better algorithmic design? We show that autocurriculum, where the model uses its own performance to decide which problems to focus training on, provably improves upon standard training recipes for both supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). For SFT, we show that autocurriculum requires exponentially fewer reasoning demonstrations than non-adaptive fine-tuning, by focusing teacher supervision on prompts where the current model struggles. For RL fine-tuning, autocurriculum decouples the computational cost from the quality of the reference model, reducing the latter to a burn-in cost that is nearly independent of the target accuracy. These improvements arise purely from adaptive data selection, drawing on classical techniques from boosting and learning from counterexamples, and requiring no assumption on the distribution or difficulty of prompts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：课程推理学习 I：自课程设计的可证明优势
思维链推理通过语言模型在最终回答前生成思考标记以消耗额外计算资源，显著推动了模型能力的发展。然而，训练这类推理模型在数据和计算上成本极高，需要收集人类或合成生成器产生的长程推理轨迹，并通过强化学习进行后训练。这些成本是否具有根本性？能否通过优化算法设计降低？我们证明，自课程设计（模型根据自身表现决定训练重点问题）在监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）中均能可证明地改进标准训练方案。对于SFT，自课程通过将教师监督聚焦于当前模型表现欠佳的提示，所需推理演示数量相比非自适应微调呈指数级减少。对于RL微调，自课程将计算成本与参考模型质量解耦，使后者转化为几乎与目标精度无关的预热成本。这些改进完全源于自适应数据选择技术，借鉴了提升算法和反例学习的经典方法，且无需对提示分布或难度作任何假设。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether the high costs of training chain-of-thought reasoning models can be reduced algorithmically, proposing autocurriculum as an adaptive training method. The method leverages the model's own performance to select challenging problems for focus, applying it to both supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). Experimental results demonstrate that autocurriculum provably reduces data needs exponentially in SFT by concentrating on difficult prompts and decouples computational cost from reference model quality in RL, making training more efficient without relying on assumptions about prompt distribution or difficulty.
本文探讨了能否通过算法设计降低思维链推理模型的高昂训练成本，提出了自课程作为一种自适应训练方法。该方法利用模型自身表现来选择有挑战性的问题进行重点训练，应用于监督微调和强化学习。实验结果表明，自课程在监督微调中通过聚焦困难提示可指数级减少数据需求，在强化学习中则使计算成本与参考模型质量解耦，从而在不依赖提示分布或难度假设的情况下提高了训练效率。
Hardware-Aware Neural Architecture Search for Encrypted Traffic Classification on Resource-Constrained Devices
Authors: Adel Chehade, Edoardo Ragusa, Paolo Gastaldo, Rodolfo Zunino
Venue: IEEE Transactions on Network and Service Management, 2026
First: 2025-06-12T21:37:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T22:05:03+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 7 figures. Published in IEEE Transactions on Network and Service Management (2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper presents a hardware-efficient deep neural network (DNN), optimized through hardware-aware neural architecture search (HW-NAS); the DNN supports the classification of session-level encrypted traffic on resource-constrained Internet of Things (IoT) and edge devices. Thanks to HW-NAS, a 1D convolutional neural network (CNN) is tailored on the ISCX VPN-nonVPN dataset to meet strict memory and computational limits while achieving robust performance. The optimized model attains 96.60% accuracy with just 88.26K parameters, 10.08M FLOPs, and a maximum tensor size of 20.12K. Compared to state-of-the-art models, it achieves reductions of up to 444-fold, 312-fold, and 15-fold in these metrics, respectively, minimizing memory footprint and runtime requirements. The model also achieves up to 99.86% across multiple VPN and traffic classification (TC) tasks; it further generalizes to external benchmarks with up to 99.98% accuracy on USTC-TFC and QUIC NetFlow. In addition, an in-depth study of header-level preprocessing confirms that the optimized model can provide performance across a wide range of configurations, even in scenarios with stricter privacy considerations. Likewise, a reduction in the length of sessions of up to 75% yields significant improvements in efficiency, while maintaining high accuracy with only a negligible drop of 1-2%. However, the importance of careful preprocessing and session length selection in the classification of raw traffic data is still present, as improper settings or aggressive reductions can cause a 7% reduction in accuracy. The quantized architecture was deployed on STM32 microcontrollers and evaluated across input sizes; results confirm that the efficiency gains from shorter sessions translate to practical, low-latency embedded inference. These findings demonstrate the method's practicality for encrypted traffic analysis in constrained IoT networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向资源受限设备的加密流量分类的硬件感知神经架构搜索
本文提出一种通过硬件感知神经架构搜索优化的硬件高效深度神经网络，该网络支持在资源受限的物联网和边缘设备上进行会话级加密流量分类。基于HW-NAS方法，在ISCX VPN-nonVPN数据集上定制了一维卷积神经网络，在满足严格内存与计算限制的同时实现了稳健性能。优化模型仅用88.26K参数、10.08M FLOPs和20.12K最大张量尺寸即达到96.60%准确率，相比前沿模型在上述指标上分别实现最高444倍、312倍和15倍的降低，显著减少了内存占用与运行时需求。该模型在多项VPN及流量分类任务中准确率最高达99.86%；在USTC-TFC和QUIC NetFlow外部基准测试中泛化性能达99.98%。对报文头部级预处理的深入研究表明，优化模型能在广泛配置下保持性能，即使在隐私要求更严格的场景中亦然。将会话长度缩减最高75%可显著提升效率，同时仅产生1-2%的可忽略精度损失。但原始流量数据分类仍需谨慎处理预处理与会话长度选择，不当设置或过度缩减可能导致准确率下降7%。量化架构已部署于STM32微控制器并通过多输入尺寸验证，结果表明缩短会话带来的效率提升可转化为实际低延迟嵌入式推理。这些发现证明了该方法在受限物联网网络中加密流量分析的实际可行性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need for efficient encrypted traffic classification on resource-constrained IoT and edge devices. The method employs a hardware-aware neural architecture search (HW-NAS) to design a compact 1D convolutional neural network tailored for session-level encrypted traffic. The main experimental results show the optimized model achieves 96.60% accuracy on the ISCX VPN-nonVPN dataset with only 88.26K parameters and 10.08M FLOPs, representing reductions of up to 444-fold and 312-fold compared to state-of-the-art models, while also generalizing well to external benchmarks like USTC-TFC with up to 99.98% accuracy. Deployment on STM32 microcontrollers confirmed practical low-latency inference, demonstrating the method's viability for constrained IoT networks.
本文旨在为资源受限的物联网和边缘设备实现高效的加密流量分类。研究方法采用硬件感知的神经架构搜索，设计了一个针对会话级加密流量的紧凑一维卷积神经网络。主要实验结果表明，优化后的模型在ISCX VPN-nonVPN数据集上达到96.60%的准确率，仅需88.26K参数和10.08M FLOPs，相比先进模型在参数量和计算量上分别降低了高达444倍和312倍，同时在USTC-TFC等外部基准测试中泛化性能优异，准确率最高达99.98%。在STM32微控制器上的部署验证了其可实现低延迟推理，证明了该方法在受限物联网网络中的实用性。
Cliqueformer: Model-Based Optimization with Structured Transformers
Authors: Jakub Grudzien Kuba, Pieter Abbeel, Sergey Levine
First: 2024-10-17T00:35:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T21:55:54+00:00
Abs · PDF
Abstract
Large neural networks excel at prediction tasks, but their application to design problems, such as protein engineering or materials discovery, requires solving offline model-based optimization (MBO) problems. While predictive models may not directly translate to effective design, recent MBO algorithms incorporate reinforcement learning and generative modeling approaches. Meanwhile, theoretical work suggests that exploiting the target function's structure can enhance MBO performance. We present Cliqueformer, a transformer-based architecture that learns the black-box function's structure through functional graphical models (FGM), addressing distribution shift without relying on explicit conservative approaches. Across various domains, including chemical and genetic design tasks, Cliqueformer demonstrates superior performance compared to existing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Cliqueformer：基于结构化Transformer的模型优化方法
大型神经网络在预测任务中表现出色，但将其应用于蛋白质工程或材料发现等设计问题时，需要解决离线模型优化问题。尽管预测模型可能无法直接转化为有效设计方案，但近期模型优化算法已融合强化学习与生成建模方法。理论研究表明，利用目标函数的结构特性可提升优化性能。本文提出Cliqueformer——一种基于Transformer的架构，通过函数图模型学习黑箱函数结构，无需依赖显式保守方法即可解决分布偏移问题。在化学设计与基因工程等多个领域的实验中，Cliqueformer均展现出优于现有方法的性能。

The paper introduces Cliqueformer, a transformer-based architecture for offline model-based optimization (MBO) in design problems like protein engineering, motivated by the need to translate predictive neural networks into effective design tools while exploiting the target function's structure. The method learns the black-box function's structure via functional graphical models (FGM) to address distribution shift without explicit conservative techniques. Experimental results across chemical and genetic design tasks show that Cliqueformer outperforms existing MBO methods.
本文提出了Cliqueformer，一种基于Transformer的架构，用于解决蛋白质工程等设计问题中的离线模型优化，其动机在于将预测性神经网络转化为有效设计工具，并利用目标函数的结构。该方法通过功能图模型学习黑盒函数的结构，以解决分布偏移问题，无需依赖显式的保守方法。在化学和遗传设计任务中的实验结果表明，Cliqueformer的性能优于现有模型优化方法。
DriveVLM-RL: Neuroscience-Inspired Reinforcement Learning with Vision-Language Models for Safe and Deployable Autonomous Driving
Authors: Zilin Huang, Zihao Sheng, Zhengyang Wan, Yansong Qu, Junwei You, Sicong Jiang, Sikai Chen
First: 2026-03-18T21:55:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T21:55:29+00:00
Comments: 32 pages, 15 figures. Code and demo available online
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Ensuring safe decision-making in autonomous vehicles remains a fundamental challenge despite rapid advances in end-to-end learning approaches. Traditional reinforcement learning (RL) methods rely on manually engineered rewards or sparse collision signals, which fail to capture the rich contextual understanding required for safe driving and make unsafe exploration unavoidable in real-world settings. Recent vision-language models (VLMs) offer promising semantic understanding capabilities; however, their high inference latency and susceptibility to hallucination hinder direct application to real-time vehicle control. To address these limitations, this paper proposes DriveVLM-RL, a neuroscience-inspired framework that integrates VLMs into RL through a dual-pathway architecture for safe and deployable autonomous driving. The framework decomposes semantic reward learning into a Static Pathway for continuous spatial safety assessment using CLIP-based contrasting language goals, and a Dynamic Pathway for attention-gated multi-frame semantic risk reasoning using a lightweight detector and a large VLM. A hierarchical reward synthesis mechanism fuses semantic signals with vehicle states, while an asynchronous training pipeline decouples expensive VLM inference from environment interaction. All VLM components are used only during offline training and are removed at deployment, ensuring real-time feasibility. Experiments in the CARLA simulator show significant improvements in collision avoidance, task success, and generalization across diverse traffic scenarios, including strong robustness under settings without explicit collision penalties. These results demonstrate that DriveVLM-RL provides a practical paradigm for integrating foundation models into autonomous driving without compromising real-time feasibility. Demo video and code are available at: https://zilin-huang.github.io/DriveVLM-RL-website/
中文标题/摘要
标题：DriveVLM-RL：基于神经科学启发的视觉语言模型强化学习框架，实现安全可部署的自动驾驶
尽管端到端学习方法快速发展，确保自动驾驶车辆的安全决策仍是根本性挑战。传统强化学习方法依赖人工设计的奖励或稀疏碰撞信号，难以捕捉安全驾驶所需的丰富上下文理解，且在实际场景中无法避免不安全探索。近期视觉语言模型展现出有前景的语义理解能力，但其高推理延迟和易产生幻觉的特性阻碍了实时车辆控制中的直接应用。为突破这些限制，本文提出DriveVLM-RL——一个受神经科学启发的双通路架构框架，将视觉语言模型融入强化学习以实现安全可部署的自动驾驶。该框架将语义奖励学习分解为：静态通路（基于CLIP对比语言目标实现连续空间安全评估）和动态通路（通过轻量检测器与大视觉语言模型实现注意力门控的多帧语义风险推理）。分层奖励合成机制融合语义信号与车辆状态，异步训练流程将高成本的视觉语言模型推理与环境交互解耦。所有视觉语言模型组件仅用于离线训练，部署时完全移除，确保实时可行性。在CARLA模拟器中的实验表明，该方法在碰撞避免、任务成功率及多样化交通场景泛化能力上均有显著提升，在无显式碰撞惩罚设置下仍保持强鲁棒性。这些结果证明DriveVLM-RL为将基础模型融入自动驾驶提供了不牺牲实时性的实用范式。演示视频与代码详见：https://zilin-huang.github.io/DriveVLM-RL-website/
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of safe decision-making in autonomous driving by proposing DriveVLM-RL, a neuroscience-inspired framework that integrates vision-language models (VLMs) into reinforcement learning (RL) to overcome the limitations of traditional RL methods, which rely on simplistic rewards and unsafe exploration. The method employs a dual-pathway architecture: a Static Pathway for continuous spatial safety assessment using CLIP-based language goals and a Dynamic Pathway for attention-gated multi-frame semantic risk reasoning with a lightweight detector and a large VLM, fused via hierarchical reward synthesis and an asynchronous training pipeline that removes VLM components at deployment for real-time feasibility. Experimental results in the CARLA simulator demonstrate significant improvements in collision avoidance, task success, and generalization across diverse traffic scenarios, even without explicit collision penalties, showcasing a practical paradigm for deploying foundation models in autonomous driving.
本文针对自动驾驶中安全决策的挑战，提出了DriveVLM-RL，这是一个受神经科学启发的框架，将视觉语言模型（VLM）集成到强化学习（RL）中，以克服传统RL方法依赖简单奖励和不安全探索的局限。该方法采用双通路架构：静态通路使用基于CLIP的语言目标进行连续空间安全评估，动态通路通过轻量检测器和大型VLM进行注意力门控的多帧语义风险推理，并通过分层奖励合成和异步训练流程融合，在部署时移除VLM组件以确保实时性。在CARLA模拟器中的实验结果表明，该方法在碰撞避免、任务成功率和跨多样交通场景的泛化能力上均有显著提升，即使在没有明确碰撞惩罚的情况下也表现出强鲁棒性，为在自动驾驶中部署基础模型提供了实用范例。
Approximate Subgraph Matching with Neural Graph Representations and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Kaiyang Li, Shihao Ji, Zhipeng Cai, Wei Li
First: 2026-03-18T21:53:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T21:53:23+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures. Code available at https://github.com/KaiyangLi1992/RL-ASM
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Approximate subgraph matching (ASM) is a task that determines the approximate presence of a given query graph in a large target graph. Being an NP-hard problem, ASM is critical in graph analysis with a myriad of applications ranging from database systems and network science to biochemistry and privacy. Existing techniques often employ heuristic search strategies, which cannot fully utilize the graph information, leading to sub-optimal solutions. This paper proposes a Reinforcement Learning based Approximate Subgraph Matching (RL-ASM) algorithm that exploits graph transformers to effectively extract graph representations and RL-based policies for ASM. Our model is built upon the branch-and-bound algorithm that selects one pair of nodes from the two input graphs at a time for potential matches. Instead of using heuristics, we exploit a Graph Transformer architecture to extract feature representations that encode the full graph information. To enhance the training of the RL policy, we use supervised signals to guide our agent in an imitation learning stage. Subsequently, the policy is fine-tuned with the Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) that optimizes the accumulative long-term rewards over episodes. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our RL-ASM outperforms existing methods in terms of effectiveness and efficiency. Our source code is available at https://github.com/KaiyangLi1992/RL-ASM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于神经图表示与强化学习的近似子图匹配
近似子图匹配（ASM）旨在判断大型目标图中是否近似存在给定查询图。作为NP难问题，ASM在图分析中至关重要，其应用涵盖数据库系统、网络科学、生物化学及隐私保护等领域。现有技术多采用启发式搜索策略，难以充分利用图结构信息，导致次优解。本文提出基于强化学习的近似子图匹配算法（RL-ASM），利用图Transformer有效提取图表示，并采用强化学习策略进行ASM。该模型基于分支定界算法，每次从两个输入图中选取一对节点进行潜在匹配。我们采用图Transformer架构提取编码完整图信息的特征表示，替代传统启发式方法。为增强强化学习策略训练，在模仿学习阶段引入监督信号指导智能体，随后通过近端策略优化（PPO）对策略进行微调，以优化多轮次累积长期奖励。在合成与真实数据集上的大量实验表明，RL-ASM在效果与效率上均优于现有方法。源代码发布于https://github.com/KaiyangLi1992/RL-ASM。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the NP-hard nature of approximate subgraph matching (ASM) and the limitations of heuristic search strategies that fail to fully utilize graph information, this paper introduces RL-ASM, a reinforcement learning-based algorithm that leverages graph transformers to extract comprehensive graph representations and employs an RL policy for matching. The method builds on a branch-and-bound framework, using a Graph Transformer to encode graph features and training the agent via imitation learning followed by fine-tuning with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) to maximize long-term rewards. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world datasets show that RL-ASM surpasses existing methods in both effectiveness and efficiency.
针对近似子图匹配（ASM）这一NP难问题，以及现有启发式搜索策略无法充分利用图信息的局限性，本文提出了RL-ASM算法，该方法结合图变换器提取图表示，并利用强化学习策略进行匹配。该方法基于分支定界框架，通过图变换器编码图特征，并采用模仿学习引导智能体训练，再使用近端策略优化（PPO）进行微调以最大化长期奖励。在合成和真实数据集上的实验结果表明，RL-ASM在效果和效率上均优于现有方法。
Fast and Generalizable NeRF Architecture Selection for Satellite Scene Reconstruction
Authors: Devjyoti Chakraborty, Zaki Sukma, Rakandhiya D. Rachmanto, Kriti Ghosh, In Kee Kim, Suchendra M. Bhandarkar, Lakshmish Ramaswamy, Nancy K. O'Hare, Deepak Mishra
First: 2026-03-18T21:42:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T21:42:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) have emerged as a powerful approach for photorealistic 3D reconstruction from multi-view images. However, deploying NeRF for satellite imagery remains challenging. Each scene requires individual training, and optimizing architectures via Neural Architecture Search (NAS) demands hours to days of GPU time. While existing approaches focus on architectural improvements, our SHAP analysis reveals that multi-view consistency, rather than model architecture, determines reconstruction quality. Based on this insight, we develop PreSCAN, a predictive framework that estimates NeRF quality prior to training using lightweight geometric and photometric descriptors. PreSCAN selects suitable architectures in < 30 seconds with < 1 dB prediction error, achieving 1000$\times$ speedup over NAS. We further demonstrate PreSCAN's deployment utility on edge platforms (Jetson Orin), where combining its predictions with offline cost profiling reduces inference power by 26% and latency by 43% with minimal quality loss. Experiments on DFC2019 datasets confirm that PreSCAN generalizes across diverse satellite scenes without retraining.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向卫星场景重建的快速泛化型NeRF架构选择方法
神经辐射场（NeRF）已成为从多视角图像实现逼真三维重建的强大方法，但在卫星影像中的应用仍面临挑战。现有方法需对每个场景单独训练，且通过神经架构搜索（NAS）优化架构需耗费数小时至数天的GPU时间。本研究通过SHAP分析发现，决定重建质量的关键在于多视角一致性而非模型架构。基于此，我们提出PreSCAN预测框架，利用轻量级几何与光度描述符在训练前预估NeRF质量。该框架可在30秒内以小于1 dB的预测误差完成架构选择，速度较NAS提升1000倍。在边缘计算平台（Jetson Orin）的部署实验中，结合离线成本分析可使推理功耗降低26%、延迟减少43%且质量损失极小。DFC2019数据集实验证实，PreSCAN无需重新训练即可泛化至多样化的卫星场景。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the inefficiency of deploying Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) for satellite imagery, where traditional Neural Architecture Search (NAS) is prohibitively slow. The method introduces PreSCAN, a predictive framework that uses lightweight geometric and photometric descriptors to estimate NeRF reconstruction quality before training, bypassing the need for lengthy architecture searches. The main experimental results show that PreSCAN selects suitable architectures in under 30 seconds with less than 1 dB prediction error, achieving a 1000x speedup over NAS, and its deployment on edge platforms like Jetson Orin reduces inference power by 26% and latency by 43% with minimal quality loss, as validated on DFC2019 datasets.
本研究的动机是解决将神经辐射场（NeRF）应用于卫星图像时的低效问题，因为传统的神经架构搜索（NAS）耗时过长。方法上提出了PreSCAN预测框架，利用轻量级的几何和光度描述符在训练前估计NeRF重建质量，从而避免冗长的架构搜索。主要实验结果表明，PreSCAN能在30秒内以小于1 dB的预测误差选择合适的架构，相比NAS实现了1000倍的速度提升，在Jetson Orin等边缘平台上的部署将推理功耗降低26%、延迟减少43%且质量损失最小，这在DFC2019数据集上得到了验证。
ARISE: Agent Reasoning with Intrinsic Skill Evolution in Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yu Li, Rui Miao, Zhengling Qi, Tian Lan
First: 2026-03-17T02:03:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T20:32:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The dominant paradigm for improving mathematical reasoning in language models relies on Reinforcement Learning with verifiable rewards. Yet existing methods treat each problem instance in isolation without leveraging the reusable strategies that emerge and accumulate during training. To this end, we introduce ARISE (Agent Reasoning via Intrinsic Skill Evolution), a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework, in which a shared policy operates both to manage skills at high-level and to generate responses at low-level (denoted as a Skills Manager and a Worker, respectively). The Manager maintains a tiered skill library through a dedicated skill generation rollout that performs structured summarization of successful solution traces (after execution), while employing a policy-driven selection mechanism to retrieve relevant skills to condition future rollouts (before execution). A hierarchical reward design guides the co-evolution of reasoning ability and library quality. Experiments on two base models and seven benchmarks spanning both competition mathematics and Omni-MATH show that ARISE consistently outperforms GRPO-family algorithms and memory-augmented baselines, with particularly notable gains on out-of-distribution tasks. Ablation studies confirm that each component contributes to the observed improvements and that library quality and reasoning performance improve in tandem throughout training. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARISE：分层强化学习中基于内在技能演化的智能体推理
当前提升语言模型数学推理能力的主流范式依赖于可验证奖励的强化学习。然而，现有方法孤立处理每个问题实例，未能充分利用训练过程中涌现和积累的可复用策略。为此，我们提出ARISE（基于内在技能演化的智能体推理），一种分层强化学习框架，其中共享策略同时执行高层技能管理与低层响应生成（分别称为技能管理器与执行器）。管理器通过专用技能生成推演维护分层技能库，对成功解题轨迹进行结构化总结（执行后），并采用策略驱动的选择机制检索相关技能以指导后续推演（执行前）。分层奖励设计引导推理能力与技能库质量的协同演化。在两个基础模型和涵盖竞赛数学与Omni-MATH的七个基准测试上的实验表明，ARISE持续优于GRPO系列算法及记忆增强基线方法，在分布外任务上提升尤为显著。消融研究证实各组件均对性能提升有贡献，且技能库质量与推理能力在训练过程中同步提升。代码发布于 \href{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation of existing reinforcement learning methods that treat each mathematical reasoning problem in isolation without reusing learned strategies, this paper introduces ARISE, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework where a shared policy acts as both a high-level Skills Manager and a low-level Worker. The method involves the Manager building a tiered skill library by summarizing successful solution traces and selecting relevant skills to condition future responses, guided by a hierarchical reward design that co-evolves reasoning ability and library quality. Experimental results on seven benchmarks with two base models show that ARISE consistently outperforms GRPO-family algorithms and memory-augmented baselines, especially on out-of-distribution tasks, with ablations confirming the contribution of each component and the tandem improvement of library quality and reasoning performance.
针对现有强化学习方法在数学推理中孤立处理每个问题、未能复用已学策略的局限，本文提出了ARISE，一种分层强化学习框架，其中共享策略同时充当高层技能管理器和低层工作者。该方法通过管理器对成功解题轨迹进行结构化总结以构建分层技能库，并在执行前检索相关技能来指导后续生成，辅以分层奖励设计共同演化推理能力和库质量。在七个基准测试和两个基础模型上的实验结果表明，ARISE持续优于GRPO系列算法和记忆增强基线，尤其在分布外任务上提升显著，消融研究证实了各组件的作用以及技能库质量与推理性能在训练中的协同提升。
Discovering What You Can Control: Interventional Boundary Discovery for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiaxin Liu
First: 2026-03-18T20:26:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T20:26:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Selecting relevant state dimensions in the presence of confounded distractors is a causal identification problem: observational statistics alone cannot reliably distinguish dimensions that correlate with actions from those that actions cause. We formalize this as discovering the agent's Causal Sphere of Influence and propose Interventional Boundary Discovery IBD, which applies Pearl's do-operator to the agent's own actions and uses two-sample testing to produce an interpretable binary mask over observation dimensions. IBD requires no learned models and composes with any downstream RL algorithm as a preprocessing step. Across 12 continuous control settings with up to 100 distractor dimensions, we find that: (1) observational feature selection can actively select confounded distractors while discarding true causal dimensions; (2) full-state RL degrades sharply once distractors outnumber relevant features by roughly 3:1 in our benchmarks; and (3)IBD closely tracks oracle performance across all distractor levels tested, with gains transferring across SAC and TD3.
中文标题/摘要
标题：发现可控因素：强化学习的干预边界发现
在存在混杂干扰变量的情况下选择相关状态维度是一个因果识别问题：仅凭观测统计无法可靠区分与行动相关的维度和行动导致的维度。我们将其形式化为发现智能体的因果影响范围，并提出干预边界发现方法，该方法将Pearl的do-算子应用于智能体自身行动，并利用双样本检验生成观测维度的可解释二元掩码。该方法无需学习模型，可作为预处理步骤与任何下游强化学习算法组合。在包含多达100个干扰维度的12个连续控制场景中，我们发现：（1）观测性特征选择可能主动选择混杂干扰变量而丢弃真实因果维度；（2）当干扰变量数量超过相关特征约3:1时，全状态强化学习性能急剧下降；（3）该方法在所有测试干扰水平下均接近理论最优性能，其增益在SAC和TD3算法中均得到验证。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of distinguishing causally relevant state dimensions from confounded distractors in reinforcement learning, which is a causal identification problem that cannot be resolved with observational data alone. The authors propose Interventional Boundary Discovery (IBD), a method that applies Pearl's do-operator to the agent's actions and uses two-sample testing to generate a binary mask over observation dimensions, requiring no learned models and serving as a preprocessing step for any RL algorithm. Experimental results across 12 continuous control settings with up to 100 distractors show that observational feature selection often fails by selecting confounded distractors, full-state RL performance degrades when distractors outnumber relevant features by about 3:1, and IBD consistently matches oracle performance across all distractor levels, with benefits transferring to algorithms like SAC and TD3.
本文针对强化学习中从混杂干扰维度中区分因果相关状态维度的挑战，这是一个仅靠观测数据无法解决的因果识别问题。作者提出了干预边界发现（IBD）方法，该方法对智能体的动作应用Pearl的do-算子，并利用双样本检验生成观测维度的二元掩码，无需学习模型，可作为任何RL算法的预处理步骤。在多达100个干扰维度的12个连续控制环境中的实验结果表明：观测特征选择常因选择混杂干扰维度而失败，当干扰维度与相关特征比例约达3:1时，全状态RL性能显著下降，而IBD在所有干扰水平下均接近最优性能，其优势可迁移至SAC和TD3等算法。
MolRGen: A Training and Evaluation Setting for De Novo Molecular Generation with Reasonning Models
Authors: Philippe Formont, Maxime Darrin, Ismail Ben Ayed, Pablo Piantanida
First: 2026-03-18T20:21:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T20:21:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in reasoning-based large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated substantial improvements in complex problem-solving tasks. Motivated by these advances, several works have explored the application of reasoning LLMs to drug discovery and molecular design. However, most existing approaches either focus on evaluation or rely on training setups that require ground-truth labels, such as molecule pairs with known property modifications. Such supervision is unavailable in \textit{de novo} molecular generation, where the objective is to generate novel molecules that optimize a desirability score without prior knowledge of high-scoring candidates. To bridge this gap, we introduce MolRGen, a large-scale benchmark and dataset for training and evaluating reasoning-based LLMs on \textit{de novo} molecular generation. Our contributions are threefold. First, we propose a setting to evaluate and train models for \textit{de novo} molecular generation and property prediction. Second, we introduce a novel diversity-aware top-$k$ score that captures both the quality and diversity of generated molecules. Third, we show our setting can be used to train LLMs for molecular generation, training a 24B LLM with reinforcement learning, and we provide a detailed analysis of its performance and limitations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MolRGen：基于推理模型的新分子生成训练与评估框架

Motivated by the success of reasoning-based large language models (LLMs) in complex problem-solving, this paper addresses the lack of suitable training and evaluation frameworks for applying such models to de novo molecular generation, where novel molecules must be generated to optimize properties without known high-scoring examples. The method introduces MolRGen, a large-scale benchmark and dataset that provides a setting for both training and evaluation, along with a novel diversity-aware top-k score to assess the quality and diversity of generated molecules. Experimental results demonstrate the framework's utility by training a 24B LLM with reinforcement learning, offering a detailed performance analysis that highlights its capabilities and limitations in molecular generation and property prediction.
本文受推理大语言模型在复杂问题解决中成功的启发，针对其在从头分子生成领域缺乏合适训练与评估框架的问题，提出了MolRGen这一大规模基准和数据集。方法上，该工作建立了一个用于训练和评估的设置，并引入了一种新颖的多样性感知top-k评分，以同时衡量生成分子的质量与多样性。实验结果表明，通过使用强化学习训练一个240亿参数的模型，该框架能够有效应用于分子生成，并提供了详细的性能分析，揭示了其在分子生成和性质预测方面的能力与局限。
Vector Optimization with Gaussian Process Bandits
Authors: İlter Onat Korkmaz, Yaşar Cahit Yıldırım, Çağın Ararat, Cem Tekin
First: 2024-12-03T14:47:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T19:03:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study black-box vector optimization with Gaussian process bandits, where there is an incomplete order relation on objective vectors described by a polyhedral convex cone. Existing black-box vector optimization approaches either suffer from high sample complexity or lack theoretical guarantees. We propose Vector Optimization with Gaussian Process (VOGP), an adaptive elimination algorithm that identifies Pareto optimal solutions sample efficiently by exploiting the smoothness of the objective function. We establish theoretical guarantees, deriving information gain-based and kernel-specific sample complexity bounds. Finally, we conduct a thorough empirical evaluation of VOGP and compare it with the state-of-the-art multi-objective and vector optimization algorithms on several real-world and synthetic datasets, emphasizing VOGP's efficiency (e.g., $\sim18\times$ lower sample complexity on average). We also provide heuristic adaptations of VOGP for cases where the design space is continuous and where the Gaussian process model lacks access to the true kernel hyperparameters. This work opens a new frontier in sample-efficient multi-objective black-box optimization by incorporating preference structures while maintaining theoretical guarantees and practical efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程赌博机的向量优化
本文研究基于高斯过程赌博机的黑盒向量优化问题，其中目标向量间存在由多面体凸锥描述的不完全序关系。现有黑盒向量优化方法或面临高样本复杂度，或缺乏理论保证。我们提出向量优化高斯过程（VOGP）算法，这是一种自适应淘汰算法，通过利用目标函数的平滑性高效采样识别帕累托最优解。我们建立了理论保证，推导了基于信息增益及核函数特性的样本复杂度界限。最后，我们在多个真实与合成数据集上对VOGP进行了全面实证评估，并与前沿多目标及向量优化算法进行对比，突显了VOGP的高效性（例如平均样本复杂度降低约18倍）。同时，针对设计空间连续及高斯过程模型无法获取真实核超参数的情况，提供了VOGP的启发式适配方案。本研究通过融合偏好结构并保持理论保证与实践效率，为样本高效的多目标黑盒优化开辟了新前沿。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of sample-efficient black-box vector optimization, where multiple objectives are partially ordered by a convex cone, and existing methods often lack theoretical guarantees or require many samples. The authors propose Vector Optimization with Gaussian Process (VOGP), an adaptive elimination algorithm that leverages Gaussian processes to exploit function smoothness and identify Pareto-optimal solutions with theoretical sample complexity bounds. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate VOGP's efficiency, showing it reduces sample complexity by approximately 18 times on average compared to state-of-the-art methods, while also offering heuristic extensions for continuous design spaces and unknown kernel hyperparameters.
本文针对黑盒向量优化中样本效率低下的问题展开研究，其中多个目标通过凸锥进行偏序排列，而现有方法常缺乏理论保证或需要大量样本。作者提出了向量优化高斯过程（VOGP）方法，这是一种自适应消除算法，利用高斯过程挖掘函数平滑性来识别帕累托最优解，并建立了基于信息增益和核函数的样本复杂度理论界限。在合成和真实数据集上的实验表明，VOGP相比现有最优方法平均降低了约18倍的样本复杂度，同时提供了针对连续设计空间和未知核超参数的启发式扩展，从而在保证理论严谨性和实践效率的前提下，为融入偏好结构的样本高效多目标黑盒优化开辟了新方向。
R2-Dreamer: Redundancy-Reduced World Models without Decoders or Augmentation
Authors: Naoki Morihira, Amal Nahar, Kartik Bharadwaj, Yasuhiro Kato, Akinobu Hayashi, Tatsuya Harada
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-18T18:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T18:54:07+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 12 figures, 2 tables. Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026. Code available at https://github.com/NM512/r2dreamer
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
A central challenge in image-based Model-Based Reinforcement Learning (MBRL) is to learn representations that distill essential information from irrelevant visual details. While promising, reconstruction-based methods often waste capacity on large task-irrelevant regions. Decoder-free methods instead learn robust representations by leveraging Data Augmentation (DA), but reliance on such external regularizers limits versatility. We propose R2-Dreamer, a decoder-free MBRL framework with a self-supervised objective that serves as an internal regularizer, preventing representation collapse without resorting to DA. The core of our method is a redundancy-reduction objective inspired by Barlow Twins, which can be easily integrated into existing frameworks. On DeepMind Control Suite and Meta-World, R2-Dreamer is competitive with strong baselines such as DreamerV3 and TD-MPC2 while training 1.59x faster than DreamerV3, and yields substantial gains on DMC-Subtle with tiny task-relevant objects. These results suggest that an effective internal regularizer can enable versatile, high-performance decoder-free MBRL. Code is available at https://github.com/NM512/r2dreamer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：R2-Dreamer：无需解码器或数据增强的冗余缩减世界模型
基于图像的模型强化学习（MBRL）的核心挑战在于从无关视觉细节中提炼关键信息的表征学习。基于重构的方法虽具潜力，却常将模型容量浪费于大范围任务无关区域。无解码器方法转而通过数据增强（DA）学习鲁棒表征，但依赖此类外部正则化器限制了方法通用性。我们提出R2-Dreamer——一种配备自监督目标的无解码器MBRL框架，该目标作为内部正则化器，无需依赖DA即可防止表征坍缩。方法核心是受Barlow Twins启发的冗余缩减目标，可轻松集成至现有框架。在DeepMind Control Suite和Meta-World环境中，R2-Dreamer与DreamerV3、TD-MPC2等强基线性能相当，且训练速度比DreamerV3快1.59倍；在包含微小任务相关对象的DMC-Subtle环境中取得显著增益。结果表明，有效的内部正则化器能够实现通用且高性能的无解码器MBRL。代码发布于https://github.com/NM512/r2dreamer。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge in image-based Model-Based Reinforcement Learning (MBRL) of learning representations that focus on task-relevant visual information while ignoring irrelevant details. The proposed method, R2-Dreamer, introduces a decoder-free framework with a self-supervised redundancy-reduction objective inspired by Barlow Twins, which acts as an internal regularizer to prevent representation collapse without relying on data augmentation. Experimental results on DeepMind Control Suite and Meta-World show that R2-Dreamer is competitive with strong baselines like DreamerV3 and TD-MPC2, trains 1.59x faster than DreamerV3, and achieves substantial gains on the DMC-Subtle benchmark with tiny task-relevant objects, demonstrating the effectiveness of internal regularization for versatile, high-performance MBRL.
本文针对基于图像的模型基强化学习（MBRL）中学习表征的挑战，旨在提取任务相关的视觉信息而忽略无关细节。所提出的方法R2-Dreamer采用无解码器框架，引入受Barlow Twins启发的自监督冗余减少目标，作为内部正则化器，避免表征崩溃且不依赖数据增强。在DeepMind Control Suite和Meta-World上的实验结果表明，R2-Dreamer与DreamerV3和TD-MPC2等强基线表现相当，训练速度比DreamerV3快1.59倍，并在具有微小任务相关对象的DMC-Subtle基准上取得显著提升，证明了内部正则化对于实现通用高性能MBRL的有效性。
Adversarial Latent-State Training for Robust Policies in Partially Observable Domains
Authors: Angad Singh Ahuja
First: 2026-03-07T19:06:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T18:48:25+00:00
Comments: 30 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robustness under latent distribution shift remains challenging in partially observable reinforcement learning. We formalize a focused setting where an adversary selects a hidden initial latent distribution before the episode, termed an adversarial latent-initial-state POMDP. Theoretically, we prove a latent minimax principle, characterize worst-case defender distributions, and derive approximate best-response inequalities with finite-sample concentration bounds that make the optimization and sampling terms explicit. Empirically, using a Battleship benchmark, we demonstrate that targeted exposure to shifted latent distributions reduces average robustness gaps between Spread and Uniform distributions from 10.3 to 3.1 shots at equal budget. Furthermore, iterative best-response training exhibits budget-sensitive behavior that is qualitatively consistent with the theorem-guided diagnostics once one accounts for discounted PPO surrogates and finite-sample noise. Ultimately, we show that for latent-initial-state problems, the framework yields a clean evaluation game and useful theorem-motivated diagnostics while also making clear where implementation-level surrogates and optimization limits enter.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对抗性潜在状态训练：面向部分可观测领域的鲁棒策略
在部分可观测强化学习中，潜在分布偏移下的鲁棒性仍是挑战。我们形式化了一个聚焦场景：智能体在回合开始前选择隐藏的初始潜在分布，称为对抗性潜在初始状态POMDP。理论上，我们证明了潜在极小极大原理，刻画了最坏情况防御者分布，并推导出具有有限样本集中界限的近似最优响应不等式，使优化项与采样项显式化。在Battleship基准测试中，实验表明定向暴露于偏移潜在分布可将Spread与Uniform分布间的平均鲁棒性差距在同等预算下从10.3次射击降至3.1次。进一步，迭代最优响应训练展现出预算敏感行为，在考虑折扣PPO替代函数与有限样本噪声后，该行为与定理指导的诊断定性一致。最终研究表明，对于潜在初始状态问题，该框架提供了清晰的评估博弈与实用的定理驱动诊断，同时明确了实现层替代函数与优化限制的介入边界。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of robustness under latent distribution shifts in partially observable reinforcement learning by formalizing an adversarial latent-initial-state POMDP, where an adversary selects a hidden initial latent distribution before each episode. Theoretically, it establishes a latent minimax principle, characterizes worst-case defender distributions, and derives approximate best-response inequalities with explicit finite-sample concentration bounds.
