Enhancing Reinforcement Learning Fine-Tuning with an Online Refiner
Authors: Hao Ma, Zhiqiang Pu, Yang Liu, Xiaolin Ai
First: 2026-03-18T08:37:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T08:37:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Constraints are essential for stabilizing reinforcement learning fine-tuning (RFT) and preventing degenerate outputs, yet they inherently conflict with the optimization objective because stronger constraints limit the ability of a fine-tuned model to discover better solutions. We propose \textit{dynamic constraints} that resolve this tension by adapting to the evolving capabilities of the fine-tuned model based on the insight that constraints should only intervene when degenerate outputs occur. We implement this by using a reference model as an \textit{online refiner} that takes the response from the fine-tuned model and generates a minimally corrected version which preserves correct content verbatim while fixing errors. A supervised fine-tuning loss then trains the fine-tuned model to produce the refined output. This mechanism yields a constraint that automatically strengthens or relaxes based on output quality. Experiments on dialogue and code generation show that dynamic constraints outperform both KL regularization and unconstrained baselines, achieving substantially higher task rewards while maintaining training stability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用在线精炼器增强强化学习微调
约束条件对于稳定强化学习微调（RFT）和防止退化输出至关重要，但由于更强的约束会限制微调模型发现更优解的能力，它们本质上与优化目标存在冲突。我们提出通过动态约束解决这一矛盾，其核心思想是：约束应仅在出现退化输出时介入，并随微调模型能力演进而自适应调整。具体实现采用参考模型作为在线精炼器，接收微调模型的响应并生成最小化修正版本——在逐字保留正确内容的同时修正错误。随后通过监督微调损失训练微调模型生成精炼后的输出。该机制形成了一种根据输出质量自动强化或松弛的约束。在对话和代码生成任务上的实验表明，动态约束在保持训练稳定性的同时，显著超越了KL正则化和无约束基线，获得了更高的任务奖励。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inherent tension between constraints and optimization in reinforcement learning fine-tuning (RFT), where strong constraints stabilize training but limit solution discovery. To resolve this, the authors propose dynamic constraints, implemented via an online refiner—a reference model that minimally corrects the fine-tuned model's outputs, preserving correct content while fixing errors, and a supervised loss trains the model to produce these refined outputs. Experiments on dialogue and code generation demonstrate that this approach outperforms KL regularization and unconstrained baselines, achieving higher task rewards while maintaining training stability.
本文针对强化学习微调中约束与优化目标之间的固有矛盾，即强约束虽能稳定训练却限制解决方案的发现。为解决此问题，作者提出动态约束，通过在线精炼器实现——一个参考模型对微调模型的输出进行最小化修正，保留正确内容并修复错误，再通过监督损失训练模型生成这些精炼输出。在对话和代码生成任务上的实验表明，该方法优于KL正则化和无约束基线，在保持训练稳定性的同时获得了显著更高的任务奖励。
Efficient Soft Actor-Critic with LLM-Based Action-Level Guidance for Continuous Control
Authors: Hao Ma, Zhiqiang Pu, Xiaolin Ai, Huimu Wang
First: 2026-03-18T08:22:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T08:22:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present GuidedSAC, a novel reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that facilitates efficient exploration in vast state-action spaces. GuidedSAC leverages large language models (LLMs) as intelligent supervisors that provide action-level guidance for the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm. The LLM-based supervisor analyzes the most recent trajectory using state information and visual replays, offering action-level interventions that enable targeted exploration. Furthermore, we provide a theoretical analysis of GuidedSAC, proving that it preserves the convergence guarantees of SAC while improving convergence speed. Through experiments in both discrete and continuous control environments, including toy text tasks and complex MuJoCo benchmarks, we demonstrate that GuidedSAC consistently outperforms standard SAC and state-of-the-art exploration-enhanced variants (e.g., RND, ICM, and E3B) in terms of sample efficiency and final performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型动作级引导的高效软演员-评论家连续控制算法

This paper introduces GuidedSAC, a reinforcement learning algorithm designed to improve exploration efficiency in large state-action spaces by integrating large language models (LLMs) as intelligent supervisors. The method enhances the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm by having an LLM analyze recent trajectories, including state data and visual replays, to provide targeted action-level guidance that directs exploration. Uncovering Latent Phase Structures and Branching Logic in Locomotion Policies: A Case Study on HalfCheetah
Authors: Daisuke Yasui, Toshitaka Matsuki, Hiroshi Sato
First: 2026-03-18T08:12:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T08:12:40+00:00
Comments: Accepted at XAI-2026: The 4th World Conference on eXplainable Artificial Intelligence
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In locomotion control tasks, Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) has demonstrated high performance; however, the decision-making process of the learned policy remains a black box, making it difficult for humans to understand. On the other hand, in periodic motions such as walking, it is well known that implicit motion phases exist, such as the stance phase and the swing phase. Focusing on this point, this study hypothesizes that a policy trained for locomotion control may also represent a phase structure that is interpretable by humans. To examine this hypothesis in a controlled setting, we consider a locomotion task that is amenable to observing whether a policy autonomously acquires temporally structured phases through interaction with the environment. To verify this hypothesis, in the MuJoCo locomotion benchmark HalfCheetah-v5, the state transition sequences acquired by a policy trained for walking control through interaction with the environment were aggregated into semantic phases based on state similarity and consistency of subsequent transitions. As a result, we demonstrated that the state sequences generated by the trained policy exhibit periodic phase transition structures as well as phase branching. Furthermore, by approximating the states and actions corresponding to each semantic phase using Explainable Boosting Machines (EBMs), we analyzed phase-dependent decision making-namely, which state features the policy function attends to and how it controls action outputs in each phase. These results suggest that neural network-based policies, which are often regarded as black boxes, can autonomously acquire interpretable phase structures and logical branching mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：揭示运动策略中的潜在相位结构与分支逻辑：以HalfCheetah为例的研究
在运动控制任务中，深度强化学习（DRL）已展现出高性能，但习得策略的决策过程仍是一个黑箱，难以被人类理解。另一方面，在行走等周期性运动中，已知存在隐含的运动相位（如支撑相与摆动相）。本研究聚焦于此，假设为运动控制训练的策略也可能表征人类可解释的相位结构。为在受控环境中检验该假设，我们考虑一项运动任务，以观察策略是否通过与环境交互自主获取时间结构化的相位。为验证假设，在MuJoCo运动基准环境HalfCheetah-v5中，将策略通过交互习得的行走控制状态转移序列，基于状态相似性和后续转移一致性聚合为语义相位。结果表明，训练策略生成的状态序列呈现周期性相位转移结构及相位分支现象。进一步，通过可解释增强机（EBMs）近似各语义相位对应的状态与动作，分析了相位依赖的决策机制——即策略函数在每相位中关注哪些状态特征，以及如何控制动作输出。这些发现表明，常被视为黑箱的神经网络策略能够自主习得可解释的相位结构与逻辑分支机制。
Summary / 总结

The method involves training a policy on the HalfCheetah-v5 benchmark and aggregating its state transitions into semantic phases based on similarity and transition consistency, followed by analyzing phase-specific decision-making using Explainable Boosting Machines (EBMs). Experimental results reveal that the policy exhibits periodic phase structures with branching logic, and EBM analysis uncovers which state features influence actions in each phase, demonstrating that neural network policies can acquire human-understandable temporal structures.
本研究针对深度强化学习在运动控制中决策过程不透明的问题，假设训练后的策略能自主学习类似生物步态的可解释运动相位。方法基于HalfCheetah-v5基准环境，通过聚合策略与环境交互产生的状态序列，依据状态相似性和转移一致性将其划分为语义相位，并利用可解释提升机分析各相位的决策逻辑。实验结果表明，训练后的策略呈现出周期性的相位转换结构和分支机制，且相位依赖的决策分析揭示了策略在不同相位中关注的状态特征与动作控制方式，证实神经网络策略能自发形成可理解的相位结构和逻辑分支。
SLEA-RL: Step-Level Experience Augmented Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Turn Agentic Training
Authors: Prince Zizhuang Wang, Shuli Jiang
First: 2026-03-18T07:16:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T07:16:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) agents have shown strong results on multi-turn tool-use tasks, yet they operate in isolation during training, failing to leverage experiences accumulated across episodes. Existing experience-augmented methods address this by organizing trajectories into retrievable libraries, but they retrieve experiences only once based on the initial task description and hold them constant throughout the episode. In multi-turn settings where observations change at every step, this static retrieval becomes increasingly mismatched as episodes progress. We propose SLEA-RL (Step-Level Experience-Augmented Reinforcement Learning), a framework that retrieves relevant experiences at each decision step conditioned on the current observation. SLEA-RL operates through three components: (i) step-level observation clustering that groups structurally equivalent environmental states for efficient cluster-indexed retrieval; (ii) a self-evolving experience library that distills successful strategies and failure patterns through score-based admission and rate-limited extraction; and (iii) policy optimization with step-level credit assignment for fine-grained advantage estimation across multi-turn episodes. The experience library evolves alongside the policy through semantic analysis rather than gradient updates. Experiments on long-horizon multi-turn agent benchmarks demonstrate that SLEA-RL achieves superior performance compared to various reinforcement learning baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SLEA-RL：面向多轮智能体训练的步级经验增强强化学习
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在多轮工具使用任务中展现出强大性能，但其训练过程孤立进行，未能利用跨回合积累的经验。现有经验增强方法通过将轨迹组织为可检索库来解决此问题，但仅基于初始任务描述检索一次经验，并在整个回合中保持固定。在多轮场景中，观测每步变化，这种静态检索会随回合推进逐渐失配。我们提出SLEA-RL（步级经验增强强化学习），该框架基于当前观测在每一步决策时检索相关经验。SLEA-RL通过三个组件运作：（i）步级观测聚类，将结构等价的环境状态分组以实现高效的聚类索引检索；（ii）自演化经验库，通过基于分数的准入机制与速率限制提取，蒸馏成功策略与失败模式；（iii）结合步级信用分配的策略优化，用于多轮回合中细粒度优势估计。经验库通过语义分析而非梯度更新，与策略协同演化。在长视野多轮智能体基准测试中，SLEA-RL相比各类强化学习基线实现了更优性能。

The paper addresses the limitation of existing experience-augmented reinforcement learning methods for multi-turn LLM agents, which retrieve experiences only once per episode based on the initial task description, leading to a mismatch as observations change dynamically. To overcome this, the authors propose SLEA-RL, a framework that performs step-level experience retrieval conditioned on current observations, utilizing observation clustering for efficient retrieval, a self-evolving experience library that distills strategies via score-based admission, and policy optimization with step-level credit assignment. Experimental results on long-horizon multi-turn agent benchmarks show that SLEA-RL outperforms various reinforcement learning baselines, demonstrating superior performance in leveraging dynamic experiences.
本文针对多轮大型语言模型智能体训练中现有经验增强强化学习方法仅基于初始任务描述一次性检索经验、导致观察动态变化时出现不匹配的问题，提出SLEA-RL框架。该方法通过基于当前观察的步骤级经验检索来应对，利用观察聚类实现高效检索，通过基于分数准入的自进化经验库提炼策略，并结合步骤级信用分配的策略优化。在长视野多轮智能体基准测试上的实验结果表明，SLEA-RL优于多种强化学习基线，在利用动态经验方面表现出更优的性能。
Meta-Reinforcement Learning with Self-Reflection for Agentic Search
Authors: Teng Xiao, Yige Yuan, Hamish Ivison, Huaisheng Zhu, Faeze Brahman, Nathan Lambert, Pradeep Dasigi, Noah A. Smith, Hannaneh Hajishirzi
First: 2026-03-11T21:40:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T07:07:34+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper introduces MR-Search, an in-context meta reinforcement learning (RL) formulation for agentic search with self-reflection. Instead of optimizing a policy within a single independent episode with sparse rewards, MR-Search trains a policy that conditions on past episodes and adapts its search strategy across episodes. MR-Search learns to learn a search strategy with self-reflection, allowing search agents to improve in-context exploration at test-time. Specifically, MR-Search performs cross-episode exploration by generating explicit self-reflections after each episode and leveraging them as additional context to guide subsequent attempts, thereby promoting more effective exploration during test-time. We further introduce a multi-turn RL algorithm that estimates a dense relative advantage at the turn level, enabling fine-grained credit assignment on each episode. Empirical results across various benchmarks demonstrate the advantages of MR-Search over baselines based RL, showing strong generalization and relative improvements of 9.2% to 19.3% across eight benchmarks. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/tengxiao1/MR-Search.

The method conditions the policy on past episodes, where after each episode, the agent generates explicit self-reflections to guide subsequent attempts, and employs a multi-turn RL algorithm with dense relative advantage estimation for fine-grained credit assignment. Experimental results across eight benchmarks show that MR-Search outperforms baseline RL methods, achieving relative improvements of 9.2% to 19.3% and demonstrating strong generalization capabilities.

Detecting Data Contamination from Reinforcement Learning Post-training for Large Language Models
Authors: Yongding Tao, Tian Wang, Yihong Dong, Huanyu Liu, Kechi Zhang, Xiaolong Hu, Ge Li
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-10T10:58:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T06:50:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026. Code is available at https://github.com/yongding-tao/RL-Data-Contamination
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Data contamination poses a significant threat to the reliable evaluation of Large Language Models (LLMs). This issue arises when benchmark samples may inadvertently appear in training sets, compromising the validity of reported performance. While detection methods have been developed for the pre-training and Supervised Fine-Tuning stages, a critical research gap exists for the increasingly significant phase of Reinforcement Learning (RL) post-training. As RL post-training becomes pivotal for advancing LLM reasoning, the absence of specialized contamination detection methods in this paradigm presents a critical vulnerability. To address this, we conduct the first systematic study of data detection within RL post-training scenario and propose Self-Critique. Our method is motivated by a key observation: after RL phase, the output entropy distribution of LLMs tends to collapse into highly specific and sparse modes. Self-Critique probes for the underlying policy collapse, i.e., the model's convergence to a narrow reasoning path, which causes this entropy reduction. To facilitate this research, we also introduce RL-MIA, a benchmark constructed to simulate this specific contamination scenario. Extensive experiments show that Self-Critique significantly outperforms baseline methods across multiple models and contamination tasks, achieving an AUC improvement of up to 30%. Whereas existing methods are close to a random guess for RL-phase contamination, our method makes detection possible.
中文标题/摘要
标题：检测大语言模型强化学习后训练阶段的数据污染
数据污染对大语言模型（LLMs）的可靠评估构成重大威胁。当基准样本无意中出现在训练集中时，会导致报告性能的有效性受损。虽然已有针对预训练和监督微调阶段的检测方法，但在日益重要的强化学习（RL）后训练阶段仍存在关键研究空白。随着RL后训练成为提升LLM推理能力的关键环节，该范式下缺乏专门的污染检测方法构成了严重漏洞。为此，我们首次系统研究了RL后训练场景下的数据检测问题，并提出“自我批判”方法。该方法的提出基于关键观察：经过RL阶段后，LLM的输出熵分布倾向于坍缩为高度特定且稀疏的模态。“自我批判”通过探查潜在策略坍缩（即模型收敛至狭窄推理路径导致熵减的现象）实现检测。为推进该研究，我们还构建了RL-MIA基准来模拟此类特定污染场景。大量实验表明，“自我批判”在多个模型和污染任务中显著优于基线方法，AUC提升最高达30%。现有方法对RL阶段污染的检测近乎随机猜测，而我们的方法实现了有效检测。

In-Context Compositional Q-Learning for Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qiushui Xu, Yuhao Huang, Yushu Jiang, Lei Song, Jinyu Wang, Wenliang Zheng, Jiang Bian
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-28T20:55:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T06:31:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted by The Fourteenth International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate estimation of the Q-function is a central challenge in offline reinforcement learning. However, existing approaches often rely on a shared global Q-function, which is inadequate for capturing the compositional structure of tasks that consist of diverse subtasks. We propose In-context Compositional Q-Learning (ICQL), an offline RL framework that formulates Q-learning as a contextual inference problem and uses linear Transformers to adaptively infer local Q-functions from retrieved transitions without explicit subtask labels. Theoretically, we show that, under two assumptions -- linear approximability of the local Q-function and accurate inference of weights from retrieved context -- ICQL achieves a bounded approximation error for the Q-function and enables near-optimal policy extraction. Empirically, ICQL substantially improves performance in offline settings, achieving gains of up to 16.4% on kitchen tasks and up to 8.8% and 6.3% on MuJoCo and Adroit tasks, respectively. These results highlight the underexplored potential of in-context learning for robust and compositional value estimation and establish ICQL as a principled and effective framework for offline RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向离线强化学习的上下文组合Q学习
Q函数的精确估计是离线强化学习的核心挑战。现有方法通常依赖共享的全局Q函数，难以捕捉由多样化子任务构成的任务组合结构。本文提出上下文组合Q学习（ICQL），该离线强化学习框架将Q学习建模为上下文推断问题，利用线性Transformer从检索到的转移样本中自适应推断局部Q函数，无需显式子任务标签。理论证明表明：在局部Q函数线性可近似、且能从检索上下文准确推断权重两个假设下，ICQL可实现Q函数的有界近似误差，并支持近最优策略提取。实验表明，ICQL在离线场景中显著提升性能：厨房任务提升达16.4%，MuJoCo与Adroit任务分别提升8.8%和6.3%。这些结果揭示了上下文学习在鲁棒组合价值估计中尚未充分挖掘的潜力，确立了ICQL作为离线强化学习理论严谨且高效的方法框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of accurate Q-function estimation in offline reinforcement learning, where existing methods using a shared global Q-function fail to capture the compositional structure of tasks with diverse subtasks. The authors propose In-context Compositional Q-Learning (ICQL), a framework that formulates Q-learning as a contextual inference problem, using linear Transformers to adaptively infer local Q-functions from retrieved transitions without explicit subtask labels. Theoretically, under assumptions of linear approximability and accurate weight inference, ICQL achieves bounded Q-function error and near-optimal policy extraction; empirically, it substantially improves performance, with gains of up to 16.4% on kitchen tasks and up to 8.8% and 6.3% on MuJoCo and Adroit tasks, demonstrating the potential of in-context learning for robust compositional value estimation.

CRE-T1 Preview Technical Report: Beyond Contrastive Learning for Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval
Authors: Guangzhi Wang, Yinghao Jiao, Zhi Liu
First: 2026-03-18T06:08:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T06:08:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The central challenge of reasoning-intensive retrieval lies in identifying implicitreasoning relationships between queries and documents, rather than superficial se-mantic or lexical similarity. The contrastive learning paradigm is fundamentallya static representation consolidation technique: during training, it encodes hier-archical relevance concepts into fixed geometric structures in the vector space,and at inference time it cannot dynamically adjust relevance judgments accord-ing to the specific reasoning demands of each query. Consequently, performancedegrades noticeably when vocabulary mismatch exists between queries and doc-uments or when implicit reasoning is required to establish relevance. This pa-per proposes Thought 1 (T1), a generative retrieval model that shifts relevancemodeling from static alignment to dynamic reasoning. On the query side, T1 dy-namically generates intermediate reasoning trajectories for each query to bridgeimplicit reasoning relationships and uses <embtoken> as a semantic aggregationpoint for the reasoning output. On the document side, it employs an instruction+ text + <embtoken> encoding format to support high-throughput indexing. Tointernalize dynamic reasoning capabilities into vector representations, we adopt athree-stage training curriculum and introduce GRPO in the third stage, enablingthe model to learn optimal derivation strategies for different queries through trial-and-error reinforcement learning. On the BRIGHT benchmark, T1-4B exhibitsstrong performance under the original query setting, outperforming larger modelstrained with contrastive learning overall, and achieving performance comparableto multi-stage retrieval pipelines. The results demonstrate that replacing static rep-resentation alignment with dynamic reasoning generation can effectively improvereasoning-intensive retrieval performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CRE-T1预览技术报告：超越对比学习的推理密集型检索
推理密集型检索的核心挑战在于识别查询与文档间的隐含推理关系，而非表面的语义或词汇相似性。对比学习范式本质上是静态表征固化技术：训练时将层级相关性概念编码为向量空间中的固定几何结构，推理时无法根据每个查询的具体推理需求动态调整相关性判断。因此，当查询与文档存在词汇失配或需要隐含推理建立关联时，性能显著下降。本文提出Thought 1（T1）生成式检索模型，将相关性建模从静态对齐转向动态推理。在查询侧，T1为每个查询动态生成中间推理轨迹以桥接隐含推理关系，并使用<embtoken>作为推理输出的语义聚合点。在文档侧，采用指令+文本+<embtoken>编码格式以支持高吞吐量索引。为将动态推理能力内化至向量表征，我们采用三阶段训练课程，并在第三阶段引入GRPO，使模型能通过试错强化学习掌握针对不同查询的最优推导策略。在BRIGHT基准测试中，T1-4B在原始查询设置下表现强劲，整体优于采用对比学习的更大规模模型，且达到与多阶段检索流程相当的性能。结果表明，用动态推理生成替代静态表征对齐能有效提升推理密集型检索性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of contrastive learning in reasoning-intensive retrieval, where static vector representations fail to capture implicit reasoning relationships between queries and documents, especially under vocabulary mismatch. The proposed Thought 1 (T1) model shifts from static alignment to dynamic reasoning by generating intermediate reasoning trajectories for each query, using a special token for semantic aggregation, and employing a structured encoding format for documents; it is trained with a three-stage curriculum including reinforcement learning to internalize dynamic reasoning. Experimental results on the BRIGHT benchmark show that the 4B-parameter T1 model outperforms larger contrastive models and matches multi-stage retrieval pipelines, demonstrating that dynamic reasoning generation effectively improves performance in reasoning-intensive retrieval tasks.
本文针对推理密集型检索中对比学习的局限性提出改进，即静态向量表示无法捕捉查询与文档间的隐含推理关系，尤其在词汇不匹配时表现不佳。提出的Thought 1（T1）模型将相关性建模从静态对齐转向动态推理，通过为每个查询动态生成中间推理轨迹、使用特殊标记进行语义聚合，并采用结构化编码格式处理文档；模型通过包含强化学习的三阶段训练课程学习动态推理能力。在BRIGHT基准测试中，40亿参数的T1模型在原始查询设置下性能优于更大的对比学习模型，并与多阶段检索流程相当，表明动态推理生成能有效提升推理密集型检索的性能。
PaperScout: An Autonomous Agent for Academic Paper Search with Process-Aware Sequence-Level Policy Optimization
Authors: Tingyue Pan, Jie Ouyang, Mingyue Cheng, Qingchuan Li, Zirui Liu, Daoyu Wang, Mingfan Pan, Shuo Yu, Qi Liu
First: 2026-01-15T03:21:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T05:55:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Academic paper search is a fundamental task in scientific research, yet most existing approaches rely on rigid, predefined workflows that struggle with complex, conditional queries. To address this limitation, we propose PaperScout, an autonomous agent that reformulates paper search as a sequential decision-making process. Unlike static workflows, PaperScout dynamically decides whether, when, and how to invoke search and expand tools based on accumulated retrieval context. However, training such agents presents a fundamental challenge: standard reinforcement learning methods, typically designed for single-turn tasks, suffer from a granularity mismatch when applied to multi-turn agentic tasks-where token-level optimization diverges from the granularity of sequence-level interactions-leading to noisy credit assignment and unstable training dynamics. We introduce Proximal Sequence Policy Optimization (PSPO), a process-aware, sequence-level policy optimization method that aligns optimization with agent--environment interaction. Comprehensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world benchmarks demonstrate that PaperScout significantly outperforms strong workflow-driven and RL baselines in both recall and relevance, validating the effectiveness of our adaptive agentic framework and optimization strategy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PaperScout：一种采用过程感知序列级策略优化的学术论文搜索自主智能体
学术论文搜索是科学研究中的基础任务，然而现有方法大多依赖僵化的预定义工作流，难以处理复杂的条件式查询。为突破这一局限，我们提出PaperScout——将论文搜索重构为序列决策过程的自主智能体。与静态工作流不同，PaperScout能基于累积检索上下文动态决定是否、何时及如何调用搜索与扩展工具。但训练此类智能体面临根本性挑战：标准强化学习方法通常针对单轮任务设计，应用于多轮智能体任务时存在粒度失配问题——令牌级优化与序列级交互的粒度差异导致信用分配噪声和训练动态不稳定。我们提出近端序列策略优化（PSPO），这是一种过程感知的序列级策略优化方法，使优化过程与智能体-环境交互保持一致。在合成与真实场景基准测试中的综合实验表明，PaperScout在召回率与相关性方面显著优于强工作流驱动及强化学习基线，验证了我们自适应智能体框架与优化策略的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of rigid, predefined workflows in academic paper search, which often fail to handle complex, conditional queries effectively. The method introduces PaperScout, an autonomous agent that frames paper search as a sequential decision-making process, dynamically choosing when and how to use search tools based on context, and it proposes Proximal Sequence Policy Optimization (PSPO) to address training challenges in multi-turn agentic tasks by aligning optimization with sequence-level interactions. The main experimental results from comprehensive benchmarks show that PaperScout significantly outperforms both workflow-driven and reinforcement learning baselines in terms of recall and relevance, validating the effectiveness of the adaptive agentic framework and optimization strategy.

Efficient Exploration at Scale
Authors: Seyed Mohammad Asghari, Chris Chute, Vikranth Dwaracherla, Xiuyuan Lu, Mehdi Jafarnia, Victor Minden, Zheng Wen, Benjamin Van Roy
First: 2026-03-18T05:47:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T05:47:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop an online learning algorithm that dramatically improves the data efficiency of reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Our algorithm incrementally updates reward and language models as choice data is received. The reward model is fit to the choice data, while the language model is updated by a variation of reinforce, with reinforcement signals provided by the reward model. Several features enable the efficiency gains: a small affirmative nudge added to each reinforcement signal, an epistemic neural network that models reward uncertainty, and information-directed exploration. With Gemma large language models (LLMs), our algorithm matches the performance of offline RLHF trained on 200K labels using fewer than 20K labels, representing more than a 10x gain in data efficiency. Extrapolating from our results, we expect our algorithm trained on 1M labels to match offline RLHF trained on 1B labels. This represents a 1,000x gain. To our knowledge, these are the first results to demonstrate that such large improvements are possible.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大规模高效探索
我们开发了一种在线学习算法，显著提升了基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）的数据效率。该算法在接收选择数据时，逐步更新奖励模型和语言模型：奖励模型拟合选择数据，语言模型则通过强化信号的变体进行更新，其中强化信号由奖励模型提供。效率提升得益于以下特性：为每个强化信号添加小幅正向激励、建模奖励不确定性的认知神经网络，以及信息导向探索。使用Gemma大语言模型（LLM）时，我们的算法仅需不到2万条标注数据即可达到离线RLHF使用20万条标注数据的性能，数据效率提升超过10倍。根据结果推断，我们预计用100万条标注数据训练的算法可匹配使用10亿条标注数据的离线RLHF性能，相当于实现1000倍的效率提升。据我们所知，这是首次证明如此大幅度的改进是可行的研究成果。

Motivated by the need to improve the data efficiency of reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), this paper develops an online learning algorithm that incrementally updates reward and language models as choice data is received. The method fits a reward model to the data and updates the language model via a reinforced variation, enhanced by a small affirmative nudge, an epistemic neural network for modeling reward uncertainty, and information-directed exploration. The main experimental results show that, using Gemma large language models, the algorithm matches the performance of offline RLHF trained on 200K labels with fewer than 20K labels, achieving over a 10x data efficiency gain, and extrapolates to a potential 1,000x gain at larger scales.

Lightweight Adaptation for LLM-based Technical Service Agent: Latent Logic Augmentation and Robust Noise Reduction
Authors: Yi Yu, Junzhuo Ma, Chenghuang Shen, Xingyan Liu, Jing Gu, Hangyi Sun, Guangquan Hu, Jianfeng Liu, Weiting Liu, Mingyue Pu, Yu Wang, Zhengdong Xiao, Rui Xie, Longjiu Luo, Qianrong Wang, Gurong Cui, Honglin Qiao, Wenlian Lu
First: 2026-03-18T05:01:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T05:01:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Adapting Large Language Models in complex technical service domains is constrained by the absence of explicit cognitive chains in human demonstrations and the inherent ambiguity arising from the diversity of valid responses. These limitations severely hinder agents from internalizing latent decision dynamics and generalizing effectively. Moreover, practical adaptation is often impeded by the prohibitive resource and time costs associated with standard training paradigms. To overcome these challenges and guarantee computational efficiency, we propose a lightweight adaptation framework comprising three key contributions. (1) Latent Logic Augmentation: We introduce Planning-Aware Trajectory Modeling and Decision Reasoning Augmentation to bridge the gap between surface-level supervision and latent decision logic. These approaches strengthen the stability of Supervised Fine-Tuning alignment. (2) Robust Noise Reduction: We construct a Multiple Ground Truths dataset through a dual-filtering method to reduce the noise by validating diverse responses, thereby capturing the semantic diversity. (3) Lightweight Adaptation: We design a Hybrid Reward mechanism that fuses an LLM-based judge with a lightweight relevance-based Reranker to distill high-fidelity reward signals while reducing the computational cost compared to standard LLM-as-a-Judge reinforcement learning. Empirical evaluations on real-world Cloud service tasks, conducted across semantically diverse settings, demonstrate that our framework achieves stability and performance gains through Latent Logic Augmentation and Robust Noise Reduction. Concurrently, our Hybrid Reward mechanism achieves alignment comparable to standard LLM-as-a-judge methods with reduced training time, underscoring the practical value for deploying technical service agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型的技术服务代理轻量化适配：潜在逻辑增强与鲁棒噪声抑制
在复杂技术服务领域适配大语言模型面临两大制约：人类演示中缺乏显式认知链，以及有效应答多样性导致的固有模糊性。这些限制严重阻碍代理内化潜在决策动态并实现有效泛化。此外，标准训练范式所需的高昂资源与时间成本常阻碍实际适配。为克服这些挑战并保障计算效率，我们提出一种轻量化适配框架，包含三项核心贡献：（1）潜在逻辑增强：通过规划感知轨迹建模与决策推理增强，弥合表层监督与潜在决策逻辑间的鸿沟，提升监督微调对齐的稳定性。（2）鲁棒噪声抑制：采用双重过滤方法构建多真实答案数据集，通过验证多样化应答降低噪声，从而捕捉语义多样性。（3）轻量化适配：设计混合奖励机制，融合基于大语言模型的评判器与轻量级相关性重排序器，在蒸馏高保真奖励信号的同时，较标准“大语言模型即评判器”的强化学习方法降低了计算成本。在真实云服务任务上的实证评估表明，本框架通过潜在逻辑增强与鲁棒噪声抑制实现了稳定性与性能提升；混合奖励机制在减少训练时间的同时，达到了与标准评判方法相当的对齐效果，彰显了技术服务代理部署的实用价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of adapting Large Language Models for technical service domains, where the lack of explicit cognitive chains in human demonstrations and response ambiguity hinder effective generalization, and standard training is resource-intensive. The authors propose a lightweight adaptation framework with three key methods: Latent Logic Augmentation, which uses Planning-Aware Trajectory Modeling and Decision Reasoning Augmentation to align surface-level supervision with latent decision logic; Robust Noise Reduction, which constructs a Multiple Ground Truths dataset via dual-filtering to capture semantic diversity while reducing noise; and a Lightweight Adaptation approach via a Hybrid Reward mechanism that fuses an LLM-based judge with a lightweight reranker to distill reward signals efficiently. Experimental results on real-world Cloud service tasks show that the framework achieves stability and performance gains through the augmentation and noise reduction components, while the hybrid reward mechanism matches the alignment of standard LLM-as-a-judge methods with reduced training time, highlighting its practical deployment value.

A Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework for Ride-Hailing Adjudication
Authors: Weiming Wu, Zi-Jian Cheng, Jie Meng, Peng Zhen, Shan Huang, Qun Li, Guobin Wu, Lan-Zhe Guo
First: 2026-03-18T03:46:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:46:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The efficient adjudication of responsibility disputes is pivotal for maintaining marketplace fairness. However, the exponential surge in ride-hailing volume renders manual review intractable, while conventional automated methods lack the reasoning transparency required for quasi-judicial decisions. Although Multimodal LLMs offer a promising paradigm, they fundamentally struggle to bridge the gap between general visual semantics and rigorous evidentiary protocols, often leading to perceptual hallucinations and logical looseness. To address these systemic misalignments, we introduce RideJudge, a Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework. Instead of relying on generic pre-training, we bridge the semantic gap via SynTraj, a synthesis engine that grounds abstract liability concepts into concrete trajectory patterns. To resolve the conflict between massive regulation volume and limited context windows, we propose an Adaptive Context Optimization strategy that distills expert knowledge, coupled with a Chain-of-Adjudication mechanism to enforce active evidentiary inquiry. Furthermore, addressing the inadequacy of sparse binary feedback for complex liability assessment, we implement a novel Ordinal-Sensitive Reinforcement Learning mechanism that calibrates decision boundaries against hierarchical severity. Extensive experiments show that our RideJudge-8B achieves 88.41\% accuracy, surpassing 32B-scale baselines and establishing a new standard for interpretable adjudication.

标题：面向网约车责任判定的渐进式视觉-逻辑对齐框架
高效处理责任争议对维护市场公平至关重要。然而，网约车订单量激增使人工审核难以实施，而传统自动化方法缺乏准司法裁决所需的推理透明度。尽管多模态大语言模型提供了有前景的范式，但其本质上难以弥合通用视觉语义与严谨证据规则之间的鸿沟，常导致感知幻觉与逻辑松散。为解决这些系统性错位，我们提出RideJudge——一种渐进式视觉-逻辑对齐框架。通过SynTraj合成引擎将抽象责任概念具象化为轨迹模式，以替代通用预训练方式。为化解海量规则与有限上下文窗口的矛盾，我们提出融合专家知识的自适应上下文优化策略，并配备证据链主动追溯机制。针对稀疏二元反馈在复杂责任判定中的不足，设计了基于层级严重度校准决策边界的有序敏感强化学习机制。大量实验表明，RideJudge-8B模型以88.41%的准确率超越32B规模基线，为可解释裁决树立了新标准。

本文针对网约车责任判定中人工审核不可行、现有自动化方法缺乏透明度和严谨推理的挑战，提出了一个渐进式视觉-逻辑对齐框架RideJudge。该方法通过SynTraj合成引擎将抽象责任概念具象化为轨迹模式，以弥合视觉语义与证据协议之间的差距，并采用自适应上下文优化和裁决链机制来处理海量规则和证据查询。实验结果表明，RideJudge-8B模型达到了88.41%的准确率，超越了32B规模的基线模型，为可解释的裁决系统设立了新标准。
TRUST-SQL: Tool-Integrated Multi-Turn Reinforcement Learning for Text-to-SQL over Unknown Schemas
Authors: Ai Jian, Xiaoyun Zhang, Wanrou Du, Jingqing Ruan, Jiangbo Pei, Weipeng Zhang, Ke Zeng, Xunliang Cai
First: 2026-03-17T12:30:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:45:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Text-to-SQL parsing has achieved remarkable progress under the Full Schema Assumption. However, this premise fails in real-world enterprise environments where databases contain hundreds of tables with massive noisy metadata. Rather than injecting the full schema upfront, an agent must actively identify and verify only the relevant subset, giving rise to the Unknown Schema scenario we study in this work. To address this, we propose TRUST-SQL (Truthful Reasoning with Unknown Schema via Tools). We formulate the task as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process where our autonomous agent employs a structured four-phase protocol to ground reasoning in verified metadata. Crucially, this protocol provides a structural boundary for our novel Dual-Track GRPO strategy. By applying token-level masked advantages, this strategy isolates exploration rewards from execution outcomes to resolve credit assignment, yielding a 9.9% relative improvement over standard GRPO. Extensive experiments across five benchmarks demonstrate that TRUST-SQL achieves an average absolute improvement of 30.6% and 16.6% for the 4B and 8B variants respectively over their base models. Remarkably, despite operating entirely without pre-loaded metadata, our framework consistently matches or surpasses strong baselines that rely on schema prefilling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TRUST-SQL：面向未知数据库模式的工具集成多轮强化学习文本转SQL方法
文本转SQL解析在全模式假设下已取得显著进展，但该前提在企业真实场景中往往失效——数据库常包含数百个具有海量噪声元数据的表。本文研究的未知模式场景要求智能体主动识别并验证相关子集，而非预先注入完整模式。为此，我们提出TRUST-SQL（基于工具的未知模式可信推理框架），将任务建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，使自主智能体通过结构化四阶段协议在已验证元数据中实现推理锚定。该协议为创新的双轨GRPO策略提供了结构化边界：通过应用词元级掩码优势值，该策略将探索奖励与执行结果解耦以解决信用分配问题，相较标准GRPO实现9.9%相对性能提升。在五个基准测试上的大量实验表明，TRUST-SQL的4B与8B变体相较基础模型分别获得30.6%与16.6%的平均绝对提升。值得注意的是，尽管完全无需预载元数据，本框架始终达到或超越依赖模式预填充的强基线方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the practical challenge of text-to-SQL parsing in real enterprise databases, which contain hundreds of tables with noisy metadata, moving beyond the unrealistic 'Full Schema Assumption'. The method introduces TRUST-SQL, which formulates the task as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process where an autonomous agent follows a structured four-phase protocol to actively identify relevant schema subsets, and employs a novel Dual-Track GRPO reinforcement learning strategy with token-level masked advantages to improve credit assignment. The main experimental results show that this approach yields a 9.9% relative improvement over standard GRPO, and extensive benchmarks demonstrate average absolute improvements of 30.6% and 16.6% for the 4B and 8B model variants over their base models, often matching or surpassing baselines that use pre-loaded schema information.
本研究的动机是解决现实企业环境中文本到SQL解析的实际挑战，这些环境包含数百个具有嘈杂元数据的表，从而超越了不切实际的“全模式假设”。方法上提出了TRUST-SQL，它将任务建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，其中自主代理遵循结构化的四阶段协议来主动识别相关模式子集，并采用一种新颖的具有令牌级掩码优势的双轨GRPO强化学习策略以改进信用分配。主要实验结果表明，该方法相比标准GRPO带来了9.9%的相对提升，在多个基准测试中，4B和8B模型变体相比其基础模型分别实现了30.6%和16.6%的平均绝对提升，其性能常常匹配甚至超越了依赖模式预填充的强基线模型。
ShuttleEnv: An Interactive Data-Driven RL Environment for Badminton Strategy Modeling
Authors: Ang Li, Xinyang Gong, Bozhou Chen, Yunlong Lu, Jiaming Ji, Yongyi Wang, Yaodong Yang, Wenxin Li
First: 2026-03-18T03:37:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:37:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present ShuttleEnv, an interactive and data-driven simulation environment for badminton, designed to support reinforcement learning and strategic behavior analysis in fast-paced adversarial sports. The environment is grounded in elite-player match data and employs explicit probabilistic models to simulate rally-level dynamics, enabling realistic and interpretable agent-opponent interactions without relying on physics-based simulation. In this demonstration, we showcase multiple trained agents within ShuttleEnv and provide live, step-by-step visualization of badminton rallies, allowing attendees to explore different play styles, observe emergent strategies, and interactively analyze decision-making behaviors. ShuttleEnv serves as a reusable platform for research, visualization, and demonstration of intelligent agents in sports AI. Our ShuttleEnv demo video URL: https://drive.google.com/file/d/1hTR4P16U27H2O0-w316bR73pxE2ucczX/view

标题：ShuttleEnv：用于羽毛球策略建模的交互式数据驱动强化学习环境
我们提出了ShuttleEnv，一个面向羽毛球的交互式数据驱动仿真环境，旨在支持快节奏对抗性体育中的强化学习与策略行为分析。该环境基于精英选手比赛数据构建，采用显式概率模型模拟回合级动态，无需依赖基于物理的仿真即可实现真实且可解释的智能体-对手交互。在本演示中，我们展示了ShuttleEnv中多个训练完成的智能体，并提供羽毛球回合的实时逐步可视化，使参与者能够探索不同比赛风格、观察涌现策略并交互式分析决策行为。ShuttleEnv可作为体育人工智能领域智能体研究、可视化与演示的可复用平台。演示视频地址：https://drive.google.com/file/d/1hTR4P16U27H2O0-w316bR73pxE2ucczX/view

Motivated by the need for a realistic platform to study strategic behavior in fast-paced adversarial sports like badminton, this paper introduces ShuttleEnv, a data-driven simulation environment. Physics-informed offline reinforcement learning eliminates catastrophic fuel waste in maritime routing
Authors: Aniruddha Bora, Julie Chalfant, Chryssostomos Chryssostomidis
First: 2026-03-18T03:28:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:28:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
International shipping produces approximately 3% of global greenhouse gas emissions, yet voyage routing remains dominated by heuristic methods. We present PIER (Physics-Informed, Energy-efficient, Risk-aware routing), an offline reinforcement learning framework that learns fuel-efficient, safety-aware routing policies from physics-calibrated environments grounded in historical vessel tracking data and ocean reanalysis products, requiring no online simulator. Validated on one full year (2023) of AIS data across seven Gulf of Mexico routes (840 episodes per method), PIER reduces mean CO2 emissions by 10% relative to great-circle routing. However, PIER's primary contribution is eliminating catastrophic fuel waste: great-circle routing incurs extreme fuel consumption (>1.5x median) in 4.8% of voyages; PIER reduces this to 0.5%, a 9-fold reduction. Per-voyage fuel variance is 3.5x lower (p<0.001), with bootstrap 95% CI for mean savings [2.9%, 15.7%]. Partial validation against observed AIS vessel behavior confirms consistency with the fastest real transits while exhibiting 23.1x lower variance. Crucially, PIER is forecast-independent: unlike A* path optimization whose wave protection degrades 4.5x under realistic forecast uncertainty, PIER maintains constant performance using only local observations. The framework combines physics-informed state construction, demonstration-augmented offline data, and a decoupled post-hoc safety shield, an architecture that transfers to wildfire evacuation, aircraft trajectory optimization, and autonomous navigation in unmapped terrain.
中文标题/摘要
标题：物理信息离线强化学习消除海上航线规划中的灾难性燃料浪费
国际航运约占全球温室气体排放量的3%，但航线规划仍主要依赖启发式方法。我们提出PIER（物理信息、节能、风险感知航线规划）框架，这是一种基于历史船舶轨迹数据和海洋再分析产品构建的物理校准环境、无需在线模拟器的离线强化学习框架，可学习节能且安全感知的航线策略。在墨西哥湾七条航线全年（2023年）AIS数据验证中（每种方法840个航程），PIER较大圆航线平均减少10%的CO2排放。其核心贡献在于消除灾难性燃料浪费：大圆航线有4.8%航程出现极端燃料消耗（>1.5倍中位数），而PIER将此比例降至0.5%，实现9倍降低。单航程燃料方差减少3.5倍（p<0.001），平均节能量的自助法95%置信区间为[2.9%, 15.7%]。基于实际AIS船舶行为的局部验证表明，PIER在保持与最快实际航次一致性的同时，方差降低23.1倍。关键优势在于PIER无需依赖预报：与A*路径优化在现实预报不确定性下波浪防护性能下降4.5倍相比，PIER仅通过局部观测即可保持稳定性能。该框架融合物理信息状态构建、演示增强的离线数据以及解耦的后验安全防护层，其架构可迁移至野火疏散、飞机轨迹优化及未知地形自主导航等领域。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the significant greenhouse gas emissions from international shipping and the limitations of heuristic routing methods, this paper introduces PIER, an offline reinforcement learning framework that learns fuel-efficient and safety-aware maritime routing policies from physics-calibrated environments using historical vessel and ocean data, without requiring an online simulator. The method combines physics-informed state construction, demonstration-augmented offline data, and a decoupled safety shield. Experimental validation on one year of AIS data across Gulf of Mexico routes shows PIER reduces mean CO2 emissions by 10% compared to great-circle routing and, more critically, cuts the incidence of catastrophic fuel waste (extreme consumption events) from 4.8% to 0.5%, a 9-fold reduction, while also demonstrating robust, forecast-independent performance that outperforms optimization methods under uncertainty.
针对国际航运温室气体排放严重且航线规划多依赖启发式方法的现状，本文提出了PIER框架，这是一种基于离线强化学习的方法，利用历史船舶轨迹和海洋再分析数据构建的物理校准环境，学习燃料高效且安全的航线策略，无需在线模拟器。该方法融合了物理信息状态构建、演示增强的离线数据以及解耦的安全防护机制。在墨西哥湾七条航线一年的AIS数据验证中，PIER相较于大圆航线平均减少10%的CO2排放，更重要的是将灾难性燃料浪费（极端高耗能航次）的发生率从4.8%大幅降低至0.5%，减少了9倍，同时其性能稳健，不依赖于预报，在不确定性下优于传统优化方法。
Recurrent Reasoning with Vision-Language Models for Estimating Long-Horizon Embodied Task Progress
Authors: Yuelin Zhang, Sijie Cheng, Chen Li, Zongzhao Li, Yuxin Huang, Yang Liu, Wenbing Huang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-18T03:13:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:13:29+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Accurately estimating task progress is critical for embodied agents to plan and execute long-horizon, multi-step tasks. Despite promising advances, existing Vision-Language Models (VLMs) based methods primarily leverage their video understanding capabilities, while neglecting their complex reasoning potential. Furthermore, processing long video trajectories with VLMs is computationally prohibitive for real-world deployment. To address these challenges, we propose the Recurrent Reasoning Vision-Language Model ($\text{R}^2$VLM). Our model features a recurrent reasoning framework that processes local video snippets iteratively, maintaining a global context through an evolving Chain of Thought (CoT). This CoT explicitly records task decomposition, key steps, and their completion status, enabling the model to reason about complex temporal dependencies. This design avoids the high cost of processing long videos while preserving essential reasoning capabilities. We train $\text{R}^2$VLM on large-scale, automatically generated datasets from ALFRED and Ego4D. Extensive experiments on progress estimation and downstream applications, including progress-enhanced policy learning, reward modeling for reinforcement learning, and proactive assistance, demonstrate that $\text{R}^2$VLM achieves strong performance and generalization, achieving a new state-of-the-art in long-horizon task progress estimation. The models and benchmarks are publicly available at \href{https://huggingface.co/collections/zhangyuelin/r2vlm}{huggingface}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于视觉语言模型循环推理的长时程具身任务进度估计
准确估计任务进度对具身智能体规划与执行长时程多步骤任务至关重要。现有基于视觉语言模型的方法主要利用其视频理解能力，却忽视了其复杂推理潜力，且处理长视频轨迹的计算成本过高。为此，我们提出循环推理视觉语言模型（R²VLM）。该模型采用循环推理框架迭代处理局部视频片段，通过动态演化的思维链保持全局上下文。该思维链显式记录任务分解、关键步骤及其完成状态，使模型能够推理复杂的时间依赖关系。该设计在避免长视频处理高成本的同时保留了核心推理能力。我们在ALFRED和Ego4D的大规模自动生成数据集上训练R²VLM。在进度估计及下游应用（包括进度增强策略学习、强化学习奖励建模和主动辅助）上的大量实验表明，R²VLM实现了优异的性能与泛化能力，在长时程任务进度估计中达到新的最优水平。模型与基准已公开于huggingface平台。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of accurately estimating progress in long-horizon embodied tasks, noting that existing Vision-Language Model (VLM) methods focus on video understanding but neglect complex reasoning and are computationally expensive for long videos. To overcome this, the authors propose the Recurrent Reasoning Vision-Language Model (R²VLM), which employs a recurrent framework to iteratively process local video snippets while maintaining a global context through an evolving Chain of Thought that records task decomposition, key steps, and completion status, enabling reasoning about temporal dependencies without processing entire long videos. Trained on automatically generated datasets from ALFRED and Ego4D, the model demonstrates strong performance in progress estimation and downstream applications like policy learning and reward modeling, achieving state-of-the-art results in long-horizon task progress estimation.
该论文针对长视野具身任务中准确估计进度的问题，指出现有基于视觉语言模型的方法主要利用视频理解能力而忽略了复杂推理，且处理长视频计算成本高昂。为此，作者提出了循环推理视觉语言模型（R²VLM），采用循环框架迭代处理局部视频片段，通过不断演化的思维链记录任务分解、关键步骤和完成状态来维持全局上下文，从而在不处理整个长视频的情况下推理时间依赖性。模型在ALFRED和Ego4D自动生成的大规模数据集上训练，在进度估计及下游应用如策略学习和奖励建模中表现出色，实现了长视野任务进度估计的最新最优性能。
InfoDensity: Rewarding Information-Dense Traces for Efficient Reasoning
Authors: Chengwei Wei, Jung-jae Kim, Longyin Zhang, Shengkai Chen, Nancy F. Chen
First: 2026-03-18T03:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:11:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) with extended reasoning capabilities often generate verbose and redundant reasoning traces, incurring unnecessary computational cost. While existing reinforcement learning approaches address this by optimizing final response length, they neglect the quality of intermediate reasoning steps, leaving models vulnerable to reward hacking. We argue that verbosity is not merely a length problem, but a symptom of poor intermediate reasoning quality. To investigate this, we conduct an empirical study tracking the conditional entropy of the answer distribution across reasoning steps. We find that high-quality reasoning traces exhibit two consistent properties: low uncertainty convergence and monotonic progress. These findings suggest that high-quality reasoning traces are informationally dense, that is, each step contributes meaningful entropy reduction relative to the total reasoning length. Motivated by this, we propose InfoDensity, a reward framework for RL training that combines an AUC-based reward and a monotonicity reward as a unified measure of reasoning quality, weighted by a length scaling term that favors achieving equivalent quality more concisely. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that InfoDensity matches or surpasses state-of-the-art baselines in accuracy while significantly reducing token usage, achieving a strong accuracy-efficiency trade-off.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InfoDensity：奖励信息密集的推理轨迹以实现高效推理
具备扩展推理能力的大型语言模型（LLMs）常生成冗长冗余的推理轨迹，导致不必要的计算成本。现有强化学习方法虽通过优化最终响应长度应对此问题，却忽略了中间推理步骤的质量，使模型易受奖励攻击。我们认为冗余不仅是长度问题，更是中间推理质量低下的表现。为探究此问题，我们通过实证研究追踪推理步骤中答案分布的条件熵，发现高质量推理轨迹具有两个一致特性：低不确定性收敛与单调进展。这些发现表明高质量推理轨迹具有信息密集性，即每个步骤相对于总推理长度均能实现有效的熵减。基于此，我们提出InfoDensity——一种用于强化学习训练的奖励框架，结合基于AUC的奖励与单调性奖励作为推理质量的统一度量，并通过长度缩放项加权以鼓励更简洁地达成同等质量。在数学推理基准测试中，InfoDensity在保持或超越先进基线精度的同时显著减少标记使用量，实现了优异的精度-效率平衡。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of verbose and redundant reasoning traces generated by large language models, which incur unnecessary computational costs. The authors argue that verbosity stems from poor intermediate reasoning quality, not just length, and they empirically identify that high-quality reasoning traces exhibit low uncertainty convergence and monotonic progress, making them informationally dense. To promote such reasoning, they propose InfoDensity, a reinforcement learning reward framework that combines AUC-based and monotonicity rewards to measure reasoning quality, scaled by length to favor conciseness. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that InfoDensity matches or exceeds state-of-the-art baselines in accuracy while significantly reducing token usage, achieving a strong accuracy-efficiency trade-off.
本文针对大语言模型在推理过程中生成冗长且冗余的推理轨迹导致不必要计算成本的问题展开研究。作者认为冗长性不仅是长度问题，更源于中间推理质量低下，并通过实证分析发现高质量推理轨迹具有低不确定性收敛和单调进展的特性，即信息密度高。为此，他们提出了InfoDensity，一个强化学习奖励框架，结合基于AUC的奖励和单调性奖励来统一衡量推理质量，并通过长度缩放项鼓励以更简洁的方式达到同等质量。在数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，InfoDensity在准确率上匹配或超越了现有先进基线，同时显著减少了令牌使用量，实现了优异的准确率与效率平衡。
SALSA-RL: Stability Analysis in the Latent Space of Actions for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xuyang Li, Romit Maulik
First: 2025-02-21T15:09:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:10:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern deep reinforcement learning (DRL) methods have made significant advances in handling continuous action spaces. However, real-world control systems, especially those requiring precise and reliable performance, often demand interpretability in the sense of a-priori assessments of agent behavior to identify safe or failure-prone interactions with environments. To address this limitation, this work proposes SALSA-RL (Stability Analysis in the Latent Space of Actions), a novel RL framework that models control actions as dynamic, time-dependent variables evolving within a latent space. By employing a pre-trained encoder-decoder and a state-dependent linear system, this approach enables interpretability through local stability analysis, where instantaneous growth in action-norms can be predicted before their execution. It is demonstrated that SALSA-RL can be deployed in a non-invasive manner for assessing the local stability of actions from pretrained RL agents without compromising on performance across diverse benchmark environments. By enabling a more interpretable analysis of action generation, SALSA-RL provides a powerful tool for advancing the design, analysis, and theoretical understanding of RL systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SALSA-RL：强化学习中动作潜在空间的稳定性分析
现代深度强化学习方法在处理连续动作空间方面取得了显著进展。然而，现实世界的控制系统，特别是那些需要精确可靠性能的系统，通常要求对智能体行为进行先验评估的可解释性，以识别与环境交互中的安全或易故障模式。为应对这一局限，本研究提出SALSA-RL（动作潜在空间稳定性分析）——一种将控制动作建模为在潜在空间中演化的动态时变变量的新型强化学习框架。通过采用预训练的编码器-解码器和状态依赖线性系统，该方法能够通过局部稳定性分析实现可解释性，在执行前即可预测动作范数的瞬时增长。实验证明，SALSA-RL能以非侵入式方式部署，用于评估预训练强化学习智能体动作的局部稳定性，且在不同基准环境中均保持性能无损。通过实现对动作生成过程更具可解释性的分析，SALSA-RL为推进强化学习系统的设计、分析和理论理解提供了有力工具。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the lack of interpretability and a-priori safety assessment in deep reinforcement learning (DRL) for real-world control systems, which require reliable performance. The method introduces SALSA-RL, a novel framework that models actions as dynamic variables in a latent space using a pre-trained encoder-decoder and a state-dependent linear system, enabling interpretability through local stability analysis to predict action-norm growth before execution. The main experimental results demonstrate that SALSA-RL can be applied non-invasively to pretrained RL agents, assessing action stability without compromising performance across diverse benchmark environments, thereby providing a tool for advancing RL system design and analysis.
本研究的动机是解决深度强化学习在现实世界控制系统中缺乏可解释性和先验安全性评估的问题，这些系统需要可靠的性能。方法上提出了SALSA-RL这一新颖框架，通过使用预训练的编码器-解码器和状态相关的线性系统，将动作建模为潜在空间中的动态变量，从而通过局部稳定性分析实现可解释性，以在执行前预测动作范数的增长。主要实验结果表明，SALSA-RL可以非侵入式地应用于预训练的强化学习智能体，在不影响多种基准环境性能的情况下评估动作稳定性，为推进强化学习系统的设计和分析提供了有力工具。
ReLMXEL: Adaptive RL-Based Memory Controller with Explainable Energy and Latency Optimization
Authors: Panuganti Chirag Sai, Gandholi Sarat, R. Raghunatha Sarma, Venkata Kalyan Tavva, Naveen M
First: 2026-03-18T03:07:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:07:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reducing latency and energy consumption is critical to improving the efficiency of memory systems in modern computing. This work introduces ReLMXEL (Reinforcement Learning for Memory Controller with Explainable Energy and Latency Optimization), a explainable multi-agent online reinforcement learning framework that dynamically optimizes memory controller parameters using reward decomposition. ReLMXEL operates within the memory controller, leveraging detailed memory behavior metrics to guide decision-making. Experimental evaluations across diverse workloads demonstrate consistent performance gains over baseline configurations, with refinements driven by workload-specific memory access behaviour. By incorporating explainability into the learning process, ReLMXEL not only enhances performance but also increases the transparency of control decisions, paving the way for more accountable and adaptive memory system designs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReLMXEL：基于自适应强化学习的可解释性能耗与延迟优化内存控制器
降低延迟与能耗对提升现代计算中内存系统的效率至关重要。本研究提出ReLMXEL（基于强化学习的可解释性能耗与延迟优化内存控制器），这是一个可解释的多智能体在线强化学习框架，通过奖励分解动态优化内存控制器参数。ReLMXEL在内存控制器内部运行，利用细粒度的内存行为指标指导决策。多样化工作负载的实验评估表明，该框架在基准配置基础上实现了持续性能提升，其优化机制由工作负载特定的内存访问行为驱动。通过将可解释性融入学习过程，ReLMXEL不仅提升了性能，还增强了控制决策的透明度，为构建更高可问责性与自适应性的内存系统设计开辟了新路径。
Summary / 总结
This work is motivated by the need to reduce latency and energy consumption in modern memory systems. It introduces ReLMXEL, an explainable multi-agent online reinforcement learning framework that dynamically optimizes memory controller parameters through reward decomposition, using detailed memory behavior metrics to guide decisions. Experimental results across diverse workloads show consistent performance improvements over baseline configurations, with optimizations tailored to specific memory access patterns, while the incorporation of explainability enhances both performance and decision transparency for more accountable system designs.
本研究旨在降低现代内存系统的延迟和能耗，提出了ReLMXEL框架，这是一种可解释的多智能体在线强化学习方法，通过奖励分解动态优化内存控制器参数，并利用详细的内存行为指标指导决策。在不同工作负载下的实验结果表明，该框架相比基线配置实现了持续的性能提升，优化过程针对特定内存访问模式进行；同时，其可解释性设计不仅提高了性能，还增强了控制决策的透明度，为构建更可靠、自适应的内存系统奠定了基础。
Contrastive Reasoning Alignment: Reinforcement Learning from Hidden Representations
Authors: Haozheng Luo, Yimin Wang, Jiahao Yu, Binghui Wang, Yan Chen
First: 2026-03-18T03:00:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:00:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose CRAFT, a red-teaming alignment framework that leverages model reasoning capabilities and hidden representations to improve robustness against jailbreak attacks. Unlike prior defenses that operate primarily at the output level, CRAFT aligns large reasoning models to generate safety-aware reasoning traces by explicitly optimizing objectives defined over the hidden state space. Methodologically, CRAFT integrates contrastive representation learning with reinforcement learning to separate safe and unsafe reasoning trajectories, yielding a latent-space geometry that supports robust, reasoning-level safety alignment. Theoretically, we show that incorporating latent-textual consistency into GRPO eliminates superficially aligned policies by ruling them out as local optima. Empirically, we evaluate CRAFT on multiple safety benchmarks using two strong reasoning models, Qwen3-4B-Thinking and R1-Distill-Llama-8B, where it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art defenses such as IPO and SafeKey. Notably, CRAFT delivers an average 79.0% improvement in reasoning safety and 87.7% improvement in final-response safety over the base models, demonstrating the effectiveness of hidden-space reasoning alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对比推理对齐：基于隐层表征的强化学习
我们提出CRAFT——一种利用模型推理能力与隐层表征的红队对齐框架，旨在提升对越狱攻击的鲁棒性。与主要在输出层面操作的现有防御方法不同，CRAFT通过显式优化隐状态空间定义的目标，使大型推理模型生成具备安全意识的推理轨迹。方法上，CRAFT将对比表征学习与强化学习相结合，以区分安全与不安全的推理路径，从而构建支持鲁棒推理级安全对齐的隐空间几何结构。理论上，我们证明将隐式-文本一致性纳入GRPO可排除表面对齐策略，使其无法成为局部最优解。实证方面，我们在多个安全基准上使用Qwen3-4B-Thinking和R1-Distill-Llama-8B两个强推理模型评估CRAFT，其表现始终优于IPO、SafeKey等前沿防御方法。值得注意的是，CRAFT在推理安全性上平均提升79.0%，在最终响应安全性上平均提升87.7%，验证了隐空间推理对齐的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance the robustness of large language models against jailbreak attacks, this paper introduces CRAFT, a red-teaming alignment framework that shifts focus from output-level defenses to aligning reasoning processes via hidden representations. The method integrates contrastive representation learning with reinforcement learning to separate safe and unsafe reasoning trajectories in the hidden state space, theoretically ensuring latent-textual consistency to avoid superficially aligned policies. Experimental results on safety benchmarks with models like Qwen3-4B-Thinking and R1-Distill-Llama-8B show that CRAFT outperforms state-of-the-art defenses, achieving average improvements of 79.0% in reasoning safety and 87.7% in final-response safety over base models.
本文旨在提升大型语言模型对抗越狱攻击的鲁棒性，提出了CRAFT这一红队对齐框架，其动机是从输出层防御转向利用隐藏表示对齐推理过程。方法上，CRAFT结合对比表示学习和强化学习，在隐藏状态空间中分离安全与不安全的推理轨迹，并通过理论保证潜在-文本一致性以避免表面对齐策略。在Qwen3-4B-Thinking和R1-Distill-Llama-8B等模型上的安全基准实验表明，CRAFT优于现有先进防御方法，相比基础模型在推理安全性和最终响应安全性上平均分别提升79.0%和87.7%。
